\maketitle

\section*{Conventions}
\begin{itemize}
\item Tone diacritics: \textbf{á} = High, \textbf{ā} = Mid, \textbf{à} = Low (unmarked = tone unknown)
\item Morpheme boundaries shown with hyphens
\item Glosses use Leipzig Glossing Rules abbreviations in \textsc{small caps}
\item \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{Italics}}: King James Version translation
\end{itemize}

\tableofcontents
\newpage

\section*{Abbreviations}
\addcontentsline{toc}{section}{Abbreviations}

\subsection*{Standard Leipzig Glossing Abbreviations}
\begin{tabular}{@{}ll@{\hspace{2em}}ll@{}}
\textsc{1} & first person & \textsc{imm} & immediate \\
\textsc{2} & second person & \textsc{imp} & imperative \\
\textsc{3} & third person & \textsc{incl} & inclusive \\
\textsc{abil} & abilitative & \textsc{ins} & instrumental \\
\textsc{abl} & ablative & \textsc{intens} & intensive \\
\textsc{all} & allative & \textsc{irr} & irrealis \\
\textsc{appl} & applicative & \textsc{iter} & iterative \\
\textsc{caus} & causative & \textsc{loc} & locative \\
\textsc{com} & comitative & \textsc{neg} & negative \\
\textsc{compl} & completive & \textsc{nmlz} & nominalizer \\
\textsc{cont} & continuative & \textsc{pfv} & perfective \\
\textsc{cvb} & converb & \textsc{pl} & plural \\
\textsc{dat} & dative & \textsc{poss} & possessive \\
\textsc{dimin} & diminutive & \textsc{prosp} & prospective \\
\textsc{erg} & ergative & \textsc{q} & question particle \\
\textsc{excl} & exclusive & \textsc{recip} & reciprocal \\
\textsc{exp} & experiential & \textsc{refl} & reflexive \\
\textsc{gen} & genitive & \textsc{rel} & relativizer \\
\textsc{hab} & habitual & \textsc{res} & resultative \\
\textsc{horiz} & horizontal & \textsc{sg} & singular \\
\end{tabular}

\vspace{1em}
\subsection*{Tedim Chin-Specific Conventions}
\begin{tabular}{@{}ll@{}}
\textsc{1sg$\rightarrow$3} & first singular acting on third person \\
\textsc{2$\rightarrow$1} & second person acting on first person \\
\textsc{3$\rightarrow$1} & third person acting on first person \\
\textsc{ag} & agent (nominalizer) \\
\textsc{comp} & comparative \\
\textsc{down} & downward directional \\
\textsc{hab.cont} & habitual continuative \\
\textsc{i} & verb form I (citation form) \\
\textsc{ii} & verb form II (dependent form) \\
\textsc{more} & comparative (more) \\
\textsc{neg.abil} & negative abilitative (cannot) \\
\textsc{toward} & goal directional \\
\textsc{up} & upward directional \\
\end{tabular}

\vspace{1em}
\noindent\textbf{Verb Forms:} Tedim Chin verbs have two conjugation forms.
\textsc{i} (Form I) is the citation/independent form; \textsc{ii} (Form II)
appears in dependent clauses and certain constructions.

\section*{Chapter 1}
\addcontentsline{toc}{section}{Chapter 1}

\begin{exe}
\exi{1}
\gll Pasian' Tá-pà Jesuh Khrih tàwh kī-sāi Lungdam-ná Thù híh bàng àhì hì. \\
     god child-male \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{khrih} \textsc{com} \textsc{refl}-concern rejoice-\textsc{nmlz} word this like be.\textsc{3sg} \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{The beginning of the gospel of Jesus Christ, the Son of God;}}

\exi{2}
\gll Kamsang Isaiah Lái Sìangtho sùng-àh, nàngmà mái-àh kà kamtai pà kà sawl à, àmàh ìn nà pái nàdìng lam-pì à bāwl-khol dìng hì. \\
     prophet \textsc{isaiah} midst holy inside-\textsc{loc} \textsc{2sg}.self face-\textsc{loc} \textsc{1sg} messenger father \textsc{1sg} send \textsc{3sg} \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{erg} \textsc{2sg} go \textsc{purp} road \textsc{3sg} make-prepare \textsc{irr} \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{As it is written in the prophets, Behold, I send my messenger before thy face, Which shall prepare thy way before thee.}}

\exi{3}
\gll Gàm sùng-àh mì khàt kiko à, topa' pái nàdìng lam-pì bāwl ùn-lá, à tot dìng lam-pì tāng-sàk ùn' cí hì cí-ìn à kī-gelh-ná tàwh hòng kī-pan-khìa hì. \\
     land inside-\textsc{loc} person one cry.out \textsc{3sg} lord go \textsc{purp} road make \textsc{pl}.\textsc{imp}-and \textsc{3sg} contend \textsc{irr} road give-\textsc{caus} \textsc{imp}.\textsc{pl} say \textsc{decl} say-\textsc{quot} \textsc{3sg} \textsc{refl}-write-\textsc{nmlz} \textsc{com} \textsc{3→1} \textsc{refl}-begin-exit \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{The voice of one crying in the wilderness, Prepare ye the way of the Lord, Make his paths straight.}}

\exi{4}
\gll Túa màh bàng-ìn gàm sùng-àh Johan hòng vák à, màwh-ná ki-sìk-ìn tùi kī-phum ùn; túa hí-lèh nà màwh-ná ùh Pasian ìn hòng mái-sàk dìng hì, cí-ìn thù à hìlh hì. \\
     that \textsc{emph} like-\textsc{erg} land inside-\textsc{loc} \textsc{johan} \textsc{3→1} walk \textsc{3sg} err-\textsc{nmlz} turn-\textsc{erg} water \textsc{refl}-immerse \textsc{imp}.\textsc{pl} that be-if \textsc{2sg} err-\textsc{nmlz} 2/3PL god \textsc{erg} \textsc{3→1} face-\textsc{caus} \textsc{irr} \textsc{decl} say-\textsc{quot} word \textsc{3sg} tell \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{John did baptize in the wilderness, and preach the baptism of repentance for the remission of sins.}}

\exi{5}
\gll Johan' thù-hìlh-ná à ngái dìng-ìn Jerusalem khùa à kī-pan Judea gàm sùng-à ōm mì khèmpeuh-tè à hòng pái ùh hì. Àmaute ìn à màwh-ná-tè ùh và pulak ùh à, Jordan Gun sùng-àh Johan ìn àmaute à tùi-phum hì. \\
     \textsc{johan} word-teach-\textsc{nmlz} \textsc{3sg} listen.\textsc{i} \textsc{irr}-\textsc{erg} \textsc{jerusalem} town \textsc{3sg} \textsc{refl}-begin \textsc{judea} land inside-\textsc{3sg} exist person all-\textsc{pl} \textsc{3sg} \textsc{3→1} go 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} err-\textsc{nmlz}-\textsc{pl} 2/3PL go.and declare 2/3PL \textsc{3sg} \textsc{jordan} river inside-\textsc{loc} \textsc{johan} \textsc{erg} \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{3sg} water-immerse \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And there went out unto him all the land of Judæa, and they of Jerusalem, and were all baptized of him in the river of Jordan, confessing their sins.}}

\exi{6}
\gll Johan ìn kalaoh múl kī-gán pùan silh-ìn, sá-vun káwng-gak tàwh à káwng gak à, kauphe lè gàm-lak khuaizu tàwh à kī-vák hì. \\
     \textsc{johan} \textsc{erg} camel hair \textsc{refl}-bear cloth clothe-\textsc{erg} meat-fur road-girdle \textsc{com} \textsc{3sg} road trap \textsc{3sg} locust and land-midst locust \textsc{com} \textsc{3sg} \textsc{refl}-walk \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And John was clothed with camel's hair, and with a girdle of a skin about his loins; and he did eat locusts and wild honey;}}

\exi{7}
\gll Àmàh ìn mì-tè tùngàh thù hìlh à, kà nùng-àh hòng pái dìng pà pèn kèi sàng-ìn nak-pì-tàk-ìn lianzaw à, kun-ìn à khedap khau à sut-sàk dìng nangawnin kà kilawm-zò kèi hì. \\
     \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{erg} person-\textsc{pl} on-\textsc{loc} word tell \textsc{3sg} \textsc{1sg} live-\textsc{loc} \textsc{3→1} go \textsc{irr} father \textsc{top} \textsc{neg}.\textsc{emph} high-\textsc{erg} strong-big-exact-\textsc{erg} greater \textsc{3sg} bow-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} shoe rope \textsc{3sg} spoil-\textsc{caus} \textsc{irr} henceforth \textsc{1sg} worthy-able \textsc{neg}.\textsc{emph} \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{and preached, saying, There cometh one mightier than I after me, the latchet of whose shoes I am not worthy to stoop down and unloose.}}

\exi{8}
\gll Kèimah ìn tùi sùng-àh nòtè kòng phum à, àmàh ìn Khá Sìangtho sùng-àh nòtè hòng phum dìng hì à cí hì. \\
     \textsc{1sg}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{erg} water inside-\textsc{loc} \textsc{2pl}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{1sg→3} immerse \textsc{3sg} \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{erg} \textsc{neg}.\textsc{perf} holy inside-\textsc{loc} \textsc{2pl}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{3→1} immerse \textsc{irr} \textsc{decl} \textsc{3sg} say \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{I indeed have baptized you with water: but he shall baptize you with the Holy Ghost.}}

\exi{9}
\gll Túa lái-tàk-ìn Galilee gàm sùng-à ōm Nà-zareth khùa pàn-ìn Jesuh hòng pái à, Jordan Gun sùng-àh Johan ìn àmàh à tùi-phum hì. \\
     that midst-exact-\textsc{erg} \textsc{galilee} land inside-\textsc{3sg} exist \textsc{2sg}-? town \textsc{abl}-\textsc{erg} \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{3→1} go \textsc{3sg} \textsc{jordan} river inside-\textsc{loc} \textsc{johan} \textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{3sg} water-immerse \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And it came to pass in those days, that Jesus came from Nazareth of Galilee, and was baptized of John in Jordan.}}

\exi{10}
\gll Tùi sùng pàn-ìn Jesuh à thawh-khìat khìt phèt-ìn vàn-tùng kī-hòng-ìn, àmà tùngàh vakhu bàng-ìn Khá Sìangtho à hòng kúm-sùk à mú hì. \\
     water inside \textsc{abl}-\textsc{erg} \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{3sg} rise-emerge \textsc{seq} twin-\textsc{erg} sky-on \textsc{refl}-open-\textsc{cvb} \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{poss} on-\textsc{loc} dove like-\textsc{erg} \textsc{neg}.\textsc{perf} holy \textsc{3sg} \textsc{3→1} bow-\textsc{down} \textsc{3sg} see.\textsc{i} \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And straightway coming up out of the water, he saw the heavens opened, and the Spirit like a dove descending upon him:}}

\exi{11}
\gll Vàn-tùng pàn-ìn àw khàt hòng ging à, nàng pèn kà ít màhmàh kà Tá-pà nà hì à, nàng tùngàh kà lùng-kím màhmàh hì à cí hì. \\
     sky-on \textsc{abl}-\textsc{erg} voice one \textsc{3→1} sound \textsc{3sg} \textsc{2sg}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{top} \textsc{1sg} love very \textsc{1sg} child-male \textsc{2sg} \textsc{decl} \textsc{3sg} \textsc{2sg}.\textsc{pro} on-\textsc{loc} \textsc{1sg} heart-full very \textsc{decl} \textsc{3sg} say \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{and there came a voice from heaven, saying , Thou art my beloved Son, in whom I am well pleased.}}

\exi{12}
\gll Tha-khàt thù-ìn Khá Sìangtho ìn gàm-lak-àh Jesuh à pái-sàk hì. \\
     spirit-one word-\textsc{erg} \textsc{neg}.\textsc{perf} holy \textsc{erg} land-midst-\textsc{loc} \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{3sg} go-\textsc{caus} \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And immediately the Spirit driveth him into the wilderness.}}

\exi{13}
\gll Gàm-lak-àh nì sàwm-li sùng ōm à, Satan ìn túa hùn sungteng à ze-èt hì. Túa lái-àh gàm-sá gilo-tè zòng ōm à, àhì zòng-ìn vàn-tùng mì-tè hòng pái-ìn àmàh huh-ìn àn à vák ùh hì. \\
     land-midst-\textsc{loc} day ten-four inside exist \textsc{3sg} \textsc{satan} \textsc{erg} that time nine \textsc{3sg} tempt \textsc{decl} that midst-\textsc{loc} land-meat \textsc{gilo}-\textsc{pl} also exist \textsc{3sg} be.\textsc{3sg} although-\textsc{erg} sky-on person-\textsc{pl} \textsc{3→1} go-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{pro} help-\textsc{cvb} \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{poss} \textsc{3sg} walk 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And he was there in the wilderness forty days, tempted of Satan; and was with the wild beasts; and the angels ministered unto him.}}

\exi{14}
\gll Thong sùng-àh Johan à kī-khìat khìt cìang-ìn Galilee gàm sùng-àh Jesuh hòng pái à, Pasian kìang pàn-ìn hòng pái Lungdam-ná Thù-thàk gēn à, \\
     prison inside-\textsc{loc} \textsc{johan} \textsc{3sg} \textsc{refl}-depart \textsc{seq} then-\textsc{erg} \textsc{galilee} land inside-\textsc{loc} \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{3→1} go \textsc{3sg} god beside \textsc{abl}-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3→1} go rejoice-\textsc{nmlz} word-true speak \textsc{3sg} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{Now after that John was put in prison, Jesus came into Galilee, preaching the gospel of the kingdom of God,}}

\exi{15}
\gll à hùn-hòih hòng túng-tà à, Pasian' Ùk dìng hùn hòng kī-pan-tà hì. Nà màwh-ná ùh kī-sìk-kík ùn-lá, híh Lungdam-ná Thù-thàk um ùn cí-ìn à hìlh hì. \\
     \textsc{3sg} time-good \textsc{3→1} arrive-\textsc{pfv} \textsc{3sg} god rule \textsc{irr} time \textsc{3→1} \textsc{refl}-begin-\textsc{pfv} \textsc{decl} \textsc{2sg} err-\textsc{nmlz} 2/3PL \textsc{refl}-turn-\textsc{iter} \textsc{pl}.\textsc{imp}-and this rejoice-\textsc{nmlz} word-true believe \textsc{imp}.\textsc{pl} say-\textsc{quot} \textsc{3sg} tell \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{and saying, The time is fulfilled, and the kingdom of God is at hand: repent ye, and believe the gospel.}}

\exi{16}
\gll Galilee Tùi-li gei tàwn-ìn Jesuh à pái lái-tàk-ìn, Simon lè à nàu Andru, ngabeng-tè àhìh manun, ngen tàwh nga khuh-ìn à ōm à mú hì. \\
     \textsc{galilee} water-flow edge loaf-\textsc{erg} \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{3sg} go midst-exact-\textsc{erg} \textsc{simon} and \textsc{3sg} child \textsc{andru} fisherman-\textsc{pl} be.\textsc{3sg}.\textsc{rel} sin pray \textsc{com} five cover-\textsc{cvb} \textsc{3sg} exist \textsc{3sg} see.\textsc{i} \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{Now as he walked by the sea of Galilee, he saw Simon and Andrew his brother casting a net into the sea: for they were fishers.}}

\exi{17}
\gll Jesuh ìn àmau tegel kìang-àh, kèi hòng zúi ùn; nga mat bàng-ìn mì tampi à huai-tè kòng sùak-sàk dìng hì à cí hì. \\
     \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{erg} \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{pro} both beside-\textsc{loc} \textsc{neg}.\textsc{emph} \textsc{3→1} follow \textsc{imp}.\textsc{pl} five steal like-\textsc{erg} person many \textsc{3sg} dread-\textsc{pl} \textsc{1sg→3} become-\textsc{caus} \textsc{irr} \textsc{decl} \textsc{3sg} say \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And Jesus said unto them, Come ye after me, and I will make you to become fishers of men.}}

\exi{18}
\gll Àmau tegel ìn zòng à ngen ùh nusia-ìn Jesuh à zúi-pah ùh hì. \\
     \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{pro} both \textsc{erg} also \textsc{3sg} pray 2/3PL abandon-\textsc{erg} \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{3sg} follow-toward 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And straightway they forsook their nets, and followed him.}}

\exi{19}
\gll Tàwm-khàt à pái khìt cìang-ìn Zebedi' tá-pà James lè à nàu Johan zòng, à gunkuang tùng uhah à ngen ùh khui-ìn à ōm à mú leuleu hì. \\
     few-one \textsc{3sg} go \textsc{seq} then-\textsc{erg} \textsc{zebedi} child-male \textsc{james} and \textsc{3sg} child \textsc{johan} also \textsc{3sg} ship on 2/3PL.\textsc{loc} \textsc{3sg} pray 2/3PL fold-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} exist \textsc{3sg} see.\textsc{i} again \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And when he had gone a little farther thence, he saw James the son of Zebedee, and John his brother, who also were in the ship mending their nets.}}

\exi{20}
\gll Jesuh ìn àmaute à mùh phèt-ìn sampah à, àmau tegel ìn zòng à pà ùh Zebedi lè à thacial-tè ùh nusia-ìn Jesuh' nùng à zúi ùh hì. \\
     \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{erg} \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{3sg} see twin-\textsc{erg} proclaim \textsc{3sg} \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{pro} both \textsc{erg} also \textsc{3sg} father 2/3PL \textsc{zebedi} and \textsc{3sg} wages-\textsc{pl} 2/3PL abandon-\textsc{erg} \textsc{jesuh} later \textsc{3sg} follow 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And straightway he called them: and they left their father Zebedee in the ship with the hired servants, and went after him.}}

\exi{21}
\gll Túa cìang-ìn Kapernaum khùa tùng ùh à, à Sabbath nì-ìn kī-khòp-ná ínn sùng-àh Jesuh pái-ìn thù hìlh dìng à kī-pan hì. \\
     that then-\textsc{erg} \textsc{kapernaum} town on 2/3PL \textsc{3sg} \textsc{3sg} \textsc{sabbath} day-\textsc{erg} \textsc{refl}-gather-\textsc{nmlz} house inside-\textsc{loc} \textsc{jesuh} go-\textsc{erg} word tell \textsc{irr} \textsc{3sg} \textsc{refl}-begin \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And they went into Capernaum; and straightway on the sabbath day he entered into the synagogue, and taught.}}

\exi{22}
\gll À thù-hìlh-ná à zá mì khèmpeuh ìn àmà thù-gēn-ná zia hàng-ìn lam-dàng à sá ùh hì. Àmàh ìn Thù-khàm hìlh sía-tè bàng-ìn thù gēn lò-ìn à-ana néi mì-tè bàng-ìn thù à gēn-zàw hì. \\
     \textsc{3sg} word-teach-\textsc{nmlz} \textsc{3sg} hear person all \textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{poss} word-speak-\textsc{nmlz} manner because-\textsc{erg} other.way \textsc{3sg} flesh 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{erg} law tell evil-\textsc{pl} like-\textsc{erg} word speak \textsc{neg}-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg}-child.\textsc{pl} have person-\textsc{pl} like-\textsc{erg} word \textsc{3sg} speak-\textsc{more} \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And they were astonished at his doctrine: for he taught them as one that had authority, and not as the scribes.}}

\exi{23}
\gll Túa lái-tàk-ìn kī-khòp-ná ínn sùng-àh dawivei mì khàt hòng lút à, \\
     that midst-exact-\textsc{erg} \textsc{refl}-gather-\textsc{nmlz} house inside-\textsc{loc} devil person one \textsc{3→1} enter \textsc{3sg} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And there was in their synagogue a man with an unclean spirit; and he cried out,}}

\exi{24}
\gll nà-zareth khùa-mì Jesuh àw, kòtè tàwh nàng bàng kī-sāi ì-hí hìam? Kòtè à sù-sía dìng-ìn híh lái-àh hòng ōm nà hì hìam? Pasian' mì sìangtho nà híh-lam kòng théi hì cí-ìn à kiko hì. \\
     \textsc{2sg}-? town-person \textsc{jesuh} voice \textsc{1pl}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{com} \textsc{2sg}.\textsc{pro} like \textsc{refl}-concern \textsc{1pl}.\textsc{incl}-be \textsc{q} \textsc{1pl}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{3sg} \textsc{caus}-bad \textsc{irr}-\textsc{erg} this midst-\textsc{loc} \textsc{3→1} exist \textsc{2sg} \textsc{decl} \textsc{q} god person holy \textsc{2sg} this-direction \textsc{1sg→3} know \textsc{decl} say-\textsc{quot} \textsc{3sg} cry.out \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{saying, Let us alone; what have we to do with thee, thou Jesus of Nazareth? art thou come to destroy us? I know thee who thou art, the Holy One of God.}}

\exi{25}
\gll Jesuh ìn, pau kèi ìn; híh mipa sùng pàn-ìn pái-khìa ìn cí-ìn túa dawi tùngàh thù à pía hì. \\
     \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{erg} \textsc{pau} \textsc{neg}.\textsc{emph} \textsc{erg} this man inside \textsc{abl}-\textsc{erg} go-exit \textsc{erg} say-\textsc{quot} that fear on-\textsc{loc} word \textsc{3sg} give \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And Jesus rebuked him, saying, Hold thy peace, and come out of him.}}

\exi{26}
\gll Dawi gilo ìn túa mipa kòng-kaw sàk-ìn à lin-sàk-gàwp khìt cìang-ìn nak-pì-tàk-ìn áwng-ìn àmà sùng pàn-ìn à pái-khìa hì. \\
     fear enemy \textsc{erg} that man \textsc{1sg→3}-tear cause-\textsc{cvb} \textsc{3sg} hope-cause-\textsc{intens} \textsc{seq} then-\textsc{erg} strong-big-exact-\textsc{erg} void-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{poss} inside \textsc{abl}-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} go-exit \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And when the unclean spirit had torn him, and cried with a loud voice, he came out of him.}}

\exi{27}
\gll Mì khèmpeuh ìn lamdang-sá ùh à, khàt-lè-khàt ìn, à bangci thù àhì hìam? Bàng thù-thàk hìlh tūan àhì hìam? Híh mipa ìn dawi gilo-tè thupiak nàdìng à-ana néi à, dawi gilo-tè ìn àmà thù à máng ùh hì cí-ìn à kī-kúm ùh hì. \\
     person all \textsc{erg} different-\textsc{intns} 2/3PL \textsc{3sg} one-and-one \textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} how word be.\textsc{3sg} \textsc{q} like word-true tell ride be.\textsc{3sg} \textsc{q} this man \textsc{erg} fear \textsc{gilo}-\textsc{pl} commandment \textsc{purp} \textsc{3sg}-child.\textsc{pl} have \textsc{3sg} fear \textsc{gilo}-\textsc{pl} \textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{poss} word \textsc{3sg} dream 2/3PL \textsc{decl} say-\textsc{quot} \textsc{3sg} \textsc{refl}-year 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And they were all amazed, insomuch that they questioned among themselves, saying, What thing is this? what new doctrine is this? for with authority commandeth he even the unclean spirits, and they do obey him.}}

\exi{28}
\gll Túa àhìh cìang-ìn híh Jesuh' thù ìn Galilee gàm sùng khèmpeuh thàk-hàt-ìn à zèl-pāk hì. \\
     that be.\textsc{3sg}.\textsc{rel} then-\textsc{erg} this \textsc{jesuh} word \textsc{erg} \textsc{galilee} land inside all new-strong-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} fame-spread \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And immediately his fame spread abroad throughout all the region round about Galilee.}}

\exi{29}
\gll Túa cìang-ìn kī-khòp-ná ínn pàn-ìn àmaute pái-khìa-ìn Simon lè à nàu Andru' ínn-àh pái-sùak-pah ùh à, James lè à nàu Johan ìn zòng à zúi ùh hì. \\
     that then-\textsc{erg} \textsc{refl}-gather-\textsc{nmlz} house \textsc{abl}-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{pro} go-exit-\textsc{erg} \textsc{simon} and \textsc{3sg} child \textsc{andru} house-\textsc{loc} go-become-unable 2/3PL \textsc{3sg} \textsc{james} and \textsc{3sg} child \textsc{johan} \textsc{erg} also \textsc{3sg} follow 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And forthwith, when they were come out of the synagogue, they entered into the house of Simon and Andrew, with James and John.}}

\exi{30}
\gll Simon' sùng-nù nat-tun-ìn lupna ngàk à, Jesuh à tun-phèt-ìn túa nù' nat-ná thù àmà kìang-àh ki-gēn hì. \\
     \textsc{simon} inside-female sick-enter-\textsc{inst} bed wait \textsc{3sg} \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{3sg} now-tell-\textsc{erg} that female ill-\textsc{nmlz} word \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{poss} beside-\textsc{loc} conversation \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{But Simon's wife's mother lay sick of a fever, and anon they tell him of her.}}

\exi{31}
\gll Àmàh zòng túa nù kìang-àh pái à, à khùt-ìn len-ìn à phong-tò hì. À nat-ná dām à, à zin-tè zòng à do-zò pah hì. \\
     \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{pro} also that female beside-\textsc{loc} go \textsc{3sg} \textsc{3sg} hand-\textsc{erg} net-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} reveal-\textsc{dir} \textsc{decl} \textsc{3sg} ill-\textsc{nmlz} good \textsc{3sg} \textsc{3sg} \textsc{zin}-\textsc{pl} also \textsc{3sg} throw-\textsc{abil} do.so \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And he came and took her by the hand, and lifted her up; and immediately the fever left her, and she ministered unto them.}}

\exi{32}
\gll Túa nì-tàk lām, nì à túm khìt cìang-ìn mì-tè ìn Jesuh kìang-àh cin-à khèmpeuh lè dawivei khèmpeuh à hòng pái-pìh ùh hì. \\
     that day-exact way day \textsc{3sg} all \textsc{seq} then-\textsc{erg} person-\textsc{pl} \textsc{erg} \textsc{jesuh} beside-\textsc{loc} said-\textsc{loc} all and devil all \textsc{3sg} \textsc{3→1} go-\textsc{appl} 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And at even, when the sun did set, they brought unto him all that were diseased, and them that were possessed with devils.}}

\exi{33}
\gll Túa khùa-mì khèmpeuh à ínn-tù-à-làh hòng kī-khàwm ùh hì. \\
     that town-person all \textsc{3sg} house-stand-\textsc{loc}-take \textsc{3→1} \textsc{refl}-gather 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And all the city was gathered together at the door.}}

\exi{34}
\gll Jesuh ìn nat-ná namkim à véi mì tampi dām-sàk à, dawi tampi tak zòng à hawlkhia hì. Dawi-tè ìn Jesuh théi ùh àhìh màn-ìn, Jesuh ìn dawi-tè thù gēn-sàk lò hì. \\
     \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{erg} ill-\textsc{nmlz} rainbow \textsc{3sg} sick person many well-\textsc{caus} \textsc{3sg} fear many truly also \textsc{3sg} drive.out \textsc{decl} demon-\textsc{pl} \textsc{erg} \textsc{jesuh} know 2/3PL be.\textsc{3sg}.\textsc{rel} reason-\textsc{erg} \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{erg} demon-\textsc{pl} word speak-\textsc{caus} \textsc{neg} \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And he healed many that were sick of divers diseases, and cast out many devils; and suffered not the devils to speak, because they knew him.}}

\exi{35}
\gll À zing cìang phal-vak mà-ìn Jesuh tho-ìn gàm-daih-ná mùn khàt-àh nà pái-ìn thù à ngen hì. \\
     \textsc{3sg} morning then permit-quick self-\textsc{erg} \textsc{jesuh} rise-\textsc{erg} land-wide-\textsc{nmlz} place one-\textsc{loc} \textsc{2sg} go-\textsc{erg} word \textsc{3sg} pray \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And in the morning, rising up a great while before day, he went out, and departed into a solitary place, and there prayed.}}

\exi{36}
\gll Àhì zòng-ìn Simon lè à lawm-tè ìn Jesuh à zòng dìng-ìn nùng-zùih ùh à, \\
     be.\textsc{3sg} although-\textsc{erg} \textsc{simon} and \textsc{3sg} friend-\textsc{pl} \textsc{erg} \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{3sg} also \textsc{irr}-\textsc{erg} behind-follow 2/3PL \textsc{3sg} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And Simon and they that were with him followed after him.}}

\exi{37}
\gll àmàh à mùh ùh cìang-ìn, mì khèmpeuh ìn nàng hòng kan ùh hì à cí ùh hì. \\
     \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{3sg} see 2/3PL then-\textsc{erg} person all \textsc{erg} \textsc{2sg}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{3→1} stay 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \textsc{3sg} say 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And when they had found him, they said unto him, All men seek for thee.}}

\exi{38}
\gll Àhìh hàng-ìn Jesuh ìn, híh kī-im-nái-à ōm khùa-dàng-tè-àh pái nì. Kèima hòng pái-ná pèn thù-hìlh dìng àhìh màn-ìn túa khùa-tè-àh thù kà hìlh dìng hì à cí hì. \\
     be.\textsc{3sg}.\textsc{rel} because-\textsc{erg} \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{erg} this \textsc{refl}-stay-near-\textsc{loc} exist town-other-\textsc{pl}-\textsc{loc} go day \textsc{1sg}.self \textsc{3→1} go-\textsc{nmlz} \textsc{top} word-teach \textsc{irr} be.\textsc{3sg}.\textsc{rel} reason-\textsc{erg} that town-\textsc{pl}-\textsc{loc} word \textsc{1sg} tell \textsc{irr} \textsc{decl} \textsc{3sg} say \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And he said unto them, Let us go into the next towns, that I may preach there also: for therefore came I forth.}}

\exi{39}
\gll Túa àhìh cìang-ìn Galilee gàm sùng khèmpeuh-àh àmàh zìn à, à kī-khòp-ná ùh ínn-tè-àh thù hìlh-ìn dawi-tè à hawlkhia hì. \\
     that be.\textsc{3sg}.\textsc{rel} then-\textsc{erg} \textsc{galilee} land inside all-\textsc{loc} \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{pro} travel \textsc{3sg} \textsc{3sg} \textsc{refl}-gather-\textsc{nmlz} 2/3PL house-\textsc{pl}-\textsc{loc} word teach-\textsc{cvb} demon-\textsc{pl} \textsc{3sg} drive.out \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And he preached in their synagogues throughout all Galilee, and cast out devils.}}

\exi{40}
\gll Mì-phak khàt Jesuh kìang-àh hòng pái-ìn khukdin à, topa àw, hòng dām-sàk núam pèuh lecin nong dām-sàk théi dìng hì cí-ìn à thùm hì. \\
     person-half one \textsc{jesuh} beside-\textsc{loc} \textsc{3→1} go-\textsc{erg} kneeling \textsc{3sg} lord voice \textsc{3→1} well-\textsc{caus} want every offend \textsc{2→1} well-\textsc{caus} know \textsc{irr} \textsc{decl} say-\textsc{quot} \textsc{3sg} three \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And there came a leper to him, beseeching him, and kneeling down to him, and saying unto him, If thou wilt, thou canst make me clean.}}

\exi{41}
\gll Jesuh ìn hèh-pìh-huai-sá àhìh màn-ìn à khùt zān-ìn lawng à, nàng kòng dām-sàk núam hì à cí hì. \\
     \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{erg} compassion-with-mix-\textsc{past} be.\textsc{3sg}.\textsc{rel} reason-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} hand night-\textsc{erg} touch \textsc{3sg} \textsc{2sg}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{1sg→3} well-\textsc{caus} want \textsc{decl} \textsc{3sg} say \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And Jesus, moved with compassion, put forth his hand, and touched him, and saith unto him, I will; be thou clean.}}

\exi{42}
\gll Tha-khàt thù-ìn à phaknat-ná bèi-ìn à dām-siang hì. \\
     spirit-one word-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} leprosy-\textsc{nmlz} finish-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} be.well-holy \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And as soon as he had spoken, immediately the leprosy departed from him, and he was cleansed.}}

\exi{43}
\gll Túa cìang-ìn Jesuh ìn khauh-tàk-ìn àmà tùngàh thù gēn-ìn pai-khìa-sak pah à, \\
     that then-\textsc{erg} \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{erg} strong-true-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{poss} on-\textsc{loc} word speak-\textsc{cvb} send.out do.so \textsc{3sg} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And he straitly charged him, and forthwith sent him away;}}

\exi{44}
\gll híh thù kuama kìang-àh gēn kèi ìn. Sìam-pì-pa kìang-àh pái-sùak pà-hin àmàh kī-vel-sàk ìn. Túa cìang-ìn nà dām-siang-ná thù mì khèmpeuh ìn à thèih nàdìngìn Moses thù-pìak-sá bàng-ìn bìak-pìak-ná bāwl ìn à cí hì. \\
     this word charge beside-\textsc{loc} speak \textsc{neg}.\textsc{emph} \textsc{erg} priest beside-\textsc{loc} go-become father-this \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{refl}-around-\textsc{caus} \textsc{erg} that then-\textsc{erg} \textsc{2sg} be.well-holy-\textsc{nmlz} word person all \textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} know.\textsc{ii} \textsc{purp}.\textsc{erg} \textsc{moses} word-give-\textsc{pl}.\textsc{poss} like-\textsc{erg} worship-give.to-\textsc{nmlz} make \textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} say \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{and saith unto him, See thou say nothing to any man: but go thy way, shew thyself to the priest, and offer for thy cleansing those things which Moses commanded, for a testimony unto them.}}

\exi{45}
\gll Àhìh hàng-ìn à mipa pái-khìa-ìn à pái-ná khèmpeuh-àh híh thù-piang khèmpeuh gēn bel-ìn à néi hì. Híh thù nak-gēn lúa-ìn kī-théi-thang gàwp àhìh màn-ìn, túa hùn à ki-pan-ìn mì-tè' thèih-ìn khùa sùng-àh Jesuh lút théi nàwn lò hì. Túa àhìh màn-ìn gàm-daih-ná mùn-àh àmàh ōm à, mùn khèmpeuh pàn-ìn àmà kìang-àh mì-tè à hòng pái ùh hì. \\
     be.\textsc{3sg}.\textsc{rel} because-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} man go-exit-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} go-\textsc{nmlz} all-\textsc{loc} this word-born all speak trust-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} have \textsc{decl} this word much-speak exceed-\textsc{erg} \textsc{refl}-know-spread all be.\textsc{3sg}.\textsc{rel} reason-\textsc{erg} that time \textsc{3sg} from person-\textsc{pl} know.\textsc{ii}-\textsc{cvb} town inside-\textsc{loc} \textsc{jesuh} enter know \textsc{cont} \textsc{neg} \textsc{decl} that be.\textsc{3sg}.\textsc{rel} reason-\textsc{erg} land-wide-\textsc{nmlz} place-\textsc{loc} \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{pro} exist \textsc{3sg} place all \textsc{abl}-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{poss} beside-\textsc{loc} person-\textsc{pl} \textsc{3sg} \textsc{3→1} go 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{But he went out, and began to publish it much, and to blaze abroad the matter, insomuch that Jesus could no more openly enter into the city, but was without in desert places: and they came to him from every quarter.}}

\end{exe}
\newpage

\section*{Chapter 2}
\addcontentsline{toc}{section}{Chapter 2}

\begin{exe}
\exi{1}
\gll Tuazawh nì tàwm-khàt khìt cìang-ìn Kapernaum khùa-àh Jesuh hòng pái-kík à, ínn-àh à ōm-ná thù hòng kī-théi-thang hì. \\
     after.that day few-one \textsc{seq} then-\textsc{erg} \textsc{kapernaum} town-\textsc{loc} \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{3→1} go-\textsc{iter} \textsc{3sg} house-\textsc{loc} \textsc{3sg} exist-\textsc{nmlz} word \textsc{3→1} \textsc{refl}-know-spread \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And again he entered into Capernaum after some days; and it was noised that he was in the house.}}

\exi{2}
\gll Mì tampi tak hòng kī-khàwm ùh àhìh màn-ìn ínn-sùng khèmpeuh, kòng-khàk pualam nangawnah mì à dim hì. Jesuh ìn àmaute kìang-àh Pasian' thù hìlh-ìn à ōm lái-tàk-ìn, \\
     person many truly \textsc{3→1} \textsc{refl}-gather 2/3PL be.\textsc{3sg}.\textsc{rel} reason-\textsc{erg} house-inside all \textsc{1sg→3}-limit outside forever person \textsc{3sg} full \textsc{decl} \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{erg} \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{pro} beside-\textsc{loc} god word teach-\textsc{cvb} \textsc{3sg} exist midst-exact-\textsc{erg} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And straightway many were gathered together, insomuch that there was no room to receive them , no, not so much as about the door: and he preached the word unto them.}}

\exi{3}
\gll mì-hìng li ìn Jesuh kìang-àh khùt-lè-khe-zàw mì khàt à pái-pìh dìng-ìn hòng pua ùh hì. \\
     person-kind four \textsc{erg} \textsc{jesuh} beside-\textsc{loc} hand-and-foot-more person one \textsc{3sg} go-\textsc{appl} \textsc{irr}-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3→1} carry.on.back 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And they come unto him, bringing one sick of the palsy, which was borne of four.}}

\exi{4}
\gll Àhì zòng-ìn mì-hon-pì kī-nèh-lúa àhìh màn-ìn Jesuh kìang-àh pái-pìh théi lò ùh hì. Túa àhìh màn-ìn Jesuh' ōm-ná sān ínn túng-khum hòng-let-ìn, à lupna pheek tàwh à mipa à khai-sùk ùh hì. \\
     be.\textsc{3sg} although-\textsc{erg} person-multitude \textsc{refl}-eat.\textsc{ii}-too be.\textsc{3sg}.\textsc{rel} reason-\textsc{erg} \textsc{jesuh} beside-\textsc{loc} go-\textsc{appl} know \textsc{neg} 2/3PL \textsc{decl} that be.\textsc{3sg}.\textsc{rel} reason-\textsc{erg} \textsc{jesuh} exist-\textsc{nmlz} flee house arrive-cover \textsc{3→1}-return-\textsc{cvb} \textsc{3sg} bed bed \textsc{com} \textsc{3sg} man \textsc{3sg} hang-down 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And when they could not come nigh unto him for the press, they uncovered the roof where he was: and when they had broken it up, they let down the bed wherein the sick of the palsy lay.}}

\exi{5}
\gll Jesuh ìn híh mì-tè' up màhmàh-ná thù à mùh cìang-ìn khùt-lè-khe-zàw mipa kìang-àh, kà tá àw, nà màwh-ná-tè hòng ki-maisak hì à cí hì. \\
     \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{erg} this person-\textsc{pl} \textsc{pl}.\textsc{q} very-\textsc{nmlz} word \textsc{3sg} see then-\textsc{erg} hand-and-foot-more man beside-\textsc{loc} \textsc{1sg} child voice \textsc{2sg} err-\textsc{nmlz}-\textsc{pl} \textsc{3→1} appear \textsc{decl} \textsc{3sg} say \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{When Jesus saw their faith, he said unto the sick of the palsy, Son, thy sins be forgiven thee.}}

\exi{6}
\gll Túa lái-àh à ōm, Thù-khàm hìlh sía-tè pàwl-khàt ìn à lùng-sìm sùng uhah, \\
     that midst-\textsc{loc} \textsc{3sg} exist law tell evil-\textsc{pl} some-one \textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} stone-mind inside 2/3PL.\textsc{loc} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{But there were certain of the scribes sitting there, and reasoning in their hearts,}}

\exi{7}
\gll bàng hàng-ìn híh mipa, Pasian tàwh à kī-kím bàng-ìn kingaihsun-ìn híh bàng-ìn pau ngam àhì hìam? Pasian sìm-lòh kuamah ìn màwh-ná mái-sàk théi lò hì cí-ìn à ngaihsun ùh hì. \\
     like because-\textsc{erg} this man god \textsc{com} \textsc{3sg} \textsc{refl}-nation like-\textsc{erg} think-\textsc{erg} this like-\textsc{erg} \textsc{pau} dare be.\textsc{3sg} \textsc{q} god count-unable nobody \textsc{erg} err-\textsc{nmlz} face-\textsc{caus} know \textsc{neg} \textsc{decl} say-\textsc{quot} \textsc{3sg} think 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{Why doth this man thus speak blasphemies? who can forgive sins but God only?}}

\exi{8}
\gll Jesuh ìn à lùng-sìm sùng uha àmau ngàih-sut-na théi-pah àhìh màn-ìn àmaute kìang-àh, bàng hàng-ìn túa bàng-ìn ngaihsun nà hì ùh hìam? \\
     \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} stone-mind inside 2/3PL.\textsc{loc} \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{pro} think-\textsc{nmlz} know-perceive be.\textsc{3sg}.\textsc{rel} reason-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{pro} beside-\textsc{loc} like because-\textsc{erg} that like-\textsc{erg} think \textsc{2sg} \textsc{decl} 2/3PL \textsc{q} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And immediately when Jesus perceived in his spirit that they so reasoned within themselves, he said unto them, Why reason ye these things in your hearts?}}

\exi{9}
\gll Híh khùt-lè-khe-zàw mipa kìang-àh, nà màwh-ná hòng ki-maisak khín hì' cìh dìng lè, tho-ìn nà lupna pheek lá ìnlà pái dih ìn' cìh dìng koi bàih-zàw àhì hìam? \\
     this hand-and-foot-more man beside-\textsc{loc} \textsc{2sg} err-\textsc{nmlz} \textsc{3→1} appear \textsc{imm} \textsc{decl} say.\textsc{nom} \textsc{irr} and rise-\textsc{erg} \textsc{2sg} bed bed take and.then go consider \textsc{erg} say.\textsc{nom} \textsc{irr} whence owe-more be.\textsc{3sg} \textsc{q} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{Whether is it easier to say to the sick of the palsy, Thy sins be forgiven thee; or to say, Arise, and take up thy bed, and walk?}}

\exi{10}
\gll Àhì zòng-ìn Mì-hìng Tá-pà ìn leitung-àh màwh-mái-sàk thèih nàdìng thù néi hì, cí-ìn nà thèih nà-dìng-ùn kòng lāk dìng hì à cí hì. Túa àhìh màn-ìn khùt-lè-khe-zàw mipa kìang-àh, \\
     be.\textsc{3sg} although-\textsc{erg} person-kind child-male \textsc{erg} earth-\textsc{loc} sin-face-\textsc{caus} know.\textsc{ii} \textsc{purp} word have \textsc{decl} say-\textsc{quot} \textsc{2sg} know.\textsc{ii} \textsc{2sg}-\textsc{irr}-\textsc{imp} \textsc{1sg→3} among \textsc{irr} \textsc{decl} \textsc{3sg} say \textsc{decl} that be.\textsc{3sg}.\textsc{rel} reason-\textsc{erg} hand-and-foot-more man beside-\textsc{loc} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{But that ye may know that the Son of man hath power on earth to forgive sins, (he saith to the sick of the palsy,)}}

\exi{11}
\gll tho-ìn nà lupna pheek lá ìnlà, nà ínn-àh ciah ìn à cí hì. \\
     rise-\textsc{erg} \textsc{2sg} bed bed take and.then \textsc{2sg} house-\textsc{loc} return \textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} say \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{I say unto thee, Arise, and take up thy bed, and go thy way into thine house.}}

\exi{12}
\gll Túa mipa zòng àmaute khèmpeuh' mùh-ìn tho à, à lupna pheek lá-ìn à pái-khìa pah hì. Àmaute khèmpeuh ìn lamdang-sá màhmàh ùh à, Pasian phàt-ìn, híh bàng màhmàh ì mú ngèi nái het kèi hì à cí ùh hì. \\
     that man also \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{pro} all see.\textsc{ii}-\textsc{cvb} rise \textsc{3sg} \textsc{3sg} bed bed take-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} go-exit do.so \textsc{decl} \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{pro} all \textsc{erg} different-\textsc{intns} very 2/3PL \textsc{3sg} god praise-\textsc{cvb} this like very \textsc{1pl}.\textsc{incl} see.\textsc{i} \textsc{exp} near trouble \textsc{neg}.\textsc{emph} \textsc{decl} \textsc{3sg} say 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And immediately he arose, took up the bed, and went forth before them all; insomuch that they were all amazed, and glorified God, saying, We never saw it on this fashion.}}

\exi{13}
\gll Túa cìang-ìn Galilee Tùi-li gei-àh Jesuh à pái-kík hì. Àmà kìang-àh mì-hon-pì hòng pái ùh à, Jesuh ìn túa mihon-tè thù à hìlh hì. \\
     that then-\textsc{erg} \textsc{galilee} water-flow edge-\textsc{loc} \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{3sg} go-\textsc{iter} \textsc{decl} \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{poss} beside-\textsc{loc} person-multitude \textsc{3→1} go 2/3PL \textsc{3sg} \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{erg} that poor.person-\textsc{pl} word \textsc{3sg} tell \textsc{decl} \\

\exi{14}

\exi{15}

\exi{16}

\exi{17}
\gll Jesuh ìn híh thù à zàk cìang-ìn àmaute kìang-àh, cí-dām-tè ìn sía-vuan kī-sàm lò ùh à, cin-à mì-tè bèk ìn kī-sàm ùh hì. \gll Khàt-véi, Sabbath nì khàt-ìn Jesuh lè à nùng-zúi-tè, mangbuh lò nawk-ìn à pái ùh hì. À pái-kà-om-ùn à nùng-zúi-tè ìn máng-buh-vui à zut ùh hì. \\

\gll Túa cìang-ìn Jesuh ìn, sabbath nì, mì-hìng-tè' phàt-tuam nàdìngìn à kī-bāwl hì à, mì-hìng pèn Sabbath nì à phàt-tuam nàdìngìn à kī-bāwl hì lò hì. \\

\section*{Chapter 3}
\addcontentsline{toc}{section}{Chapter 3}

\begin{exe}
\exi{1}
\gll Túa cìang-ìn kī-khòp-ná ínn sùng-àh Jesuh pái-kík à, túa lái-àh à khùt à lang-khàt à zàw mì khàt nà ōm hì. \\
     that then-\textsc{erg} \textsc{refl}-gather-\textsc{nmlz} house inside-\textsc{loc} \textsc{jesuh} go-\textsc{iter} \textsc{3sg} that midst-\textsc{loc} \textsc{3sg} hand \textsc{3sg} side-one \textsc{3sg} more person one \textsc{2sg} exist \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And he entered again into the synagogue; and there was a man there which had a withered hand.}}

\exi{2}
\gll Jesuh gamta-khial hì, cí-ìn à mawhsak núam mì pàwl-khàt túa lái-àh ōm ùh à, Sabbath nì-ìn híh mipa à damsak-khá hìam, cí-ìn vil gìgè ùh hì. \\
     \textsc{jesuh} send.away-err \textsc{decl} say-\textsc{quot} \textsc{3sg} adversary want person some-one that midst-\textsc{loc} exist 2/3PL \textsc{3sg} \textsc{sabbath} day-\textsc{erg} this man \textsc{3sg} heal-still \textsc{q} say-\textsc{quot} watch \textsc{hab} 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And they watched him, whether he would heal him on the sabbath day; that they might accuse him.}}

\exi{3}
\gll Jesuh ìn khùt-zàw mipa kìang-àh, híh à mái lām-àh hòng dìng ìn à cí hì. \\
     \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{erg} hand-shrivel man beside-\textsc{loc} this \textsc{3sg} face way-\textsc{loc} \textsc{3→1} \textsc{irr} \textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} say \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And he saith unto the man which had the withered hand, Stand forth.}}

\exi{4}
\gll Túa cìang-ìn mì-tè kìang-àh, sabbath nì-ìn bàng ì híh dìng ì Thù-khàm ìn hòng dèih àhì hìam? Huh dìng màw, gimsak dìng; mì khàt à nuntak-ná hot dìng màw, thàh dìng; koi hòng dèih-zàw àhì hìam cí-ìn à dòng hì. Àhìh hàng-ìn kuamah ìn dawng lò hì. \\
     that then-\textsc{erg} person-\textsc{pl} beside-\textsc{loc} \textsc{sabbath} day-\textsc{erg} like \textsc{1pl}.\textsc{incl} this \textsc{irr} \textsc{1pl}.\textsc{incl} law \textsc{erg} \textsc{3→1} want be.\textsc{3sg} \textsc{q} help \textsc{irr} see judge \textsc{irr} person one \textsc{3sg} live-\textsc{nmlz} steer \textsc{irr} see slay \textsc{irr} whence \textsc{3→1} want-more be.\textsc{3sg} \textsc{q} say-\textsc{quot} \textsc{3sg} until \textsc{decl} be.\textsc{3sg}.\textsc{rel} because-\textsc{erg} nobody \textsc{erg} receive \textsc{neg} \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And he saith unto them, Is it lawful to do good on the sabbath days, or to do evil? to save life, or to kill? But they held their peace.}}

\exi{5}
\gll Jesuh ìn hehmai tàwh à kiim à pam ēn kawi-kawi à, àhì zòng-ìn à khialh-ná ùh lè à thuphawk thèih lòh-ná ùh hàng-ìn mì-tè khá-sìat-huai à sá zèl hì. Túa cìang-ìn à mipa kìang-àh, nà khùt zān ìn à cí hì. Àmàh ìn zòng à khùt zān à, dām-ìn à ngèina bàng-kík hì. \\
     \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{erg} boldness \textsc{com} \textsc{3sg} around \textsc{3sg} fold \textsc{en} crooked\textasciitilde{}REDUP \textsc{3sg} be.\textsc{3sg} although-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} wrong-\textsc{nmlz} 2/3PL and \textsc{3sg} wise know.\textsc{ii} \textsc{neg}-\textsc{nmlz} 2/3PL because-\textsc{erg} person-\textsc{pl} spirit-evil-full \textsc{3sg} flesh scatter \textsc{decl} that then-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} man beside-\textsc{loc} \textsc{2sg} hand break \textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} say \textsc{decl} \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{erg} also \textsc{3sg} hand break \textsc{3sg} be.well-\textsc{cvb} \textsc{3sg} know-\textsc{nmlz} what-\textsc{iter} \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And when he had looked round about on them with anger, being grieved for the hardness of their hearts, he saith unto the man, Stretch forth thine hand. And he stretched it out: and his hand was restored whole as the other.}}

\exi{6}
\gll Túa àhìh cìang-ìn kī-khòp-ná ínn pàn-ìn Farisi mì-tè pái-khìa-ìn Herod pàwl-tè kimkhat tàwh kī-khòp-ná néi-pàh ùh à, Jesuh à thàh-thèih nàdìng ùh à vái-hawm ùh hì. \\
     that be.\textsc{3sg}.\textsc{rel} then-\textsc{erg} \textsc{refl}-gather-\textsc{nmlz} house \textsc{abl}-\textsc{erg} \textsc{farisi} person-\textsc{pl} go-exit-\textsc{erg} \textsc{herod} group-\textsc{pl} half \textsc{com} \textsc{refl}-gather-\textsc{nmlz} have-\textsc{neg}.\textsc{abil} 2/3PL \textsc{3sg} \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{3sg} slay-\textsc{abil} \textsc{purp} 2/3PL \textsc{3sg} plan-counsel 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And the Pharisees went forth, and straightway took counsel with the Herodians against him, how they might destroy him.}}

\exi{7}
\gll Túa lái pàn-ìn Galilee Tùi-li-àh Jesuh lè à nùng-zúi-tè pái ùh à, Galilee gàm, Judea gàm, \\
     that midst \textsc{abl}-\textsc{erg} \textsc{galilee} water-flow-\textsc{loc} \textsc{jesuh} and \textsc{3sg} life-follow-\textsc{pl} go 2/3PL \textsc{3sg} \textsc{galilee} land \textsc{judea} land \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{But Jesus withdrew himself with his disciples to the sea: and a great multitude from Galilee followed him, and from Judæa,}}

\exi{8}
\gll Jerusalem khùa, Idumia gàm, Jordan galkhat, Tái-à khùa-pì kiim lè Sidon khùa-pì kiim-à ōm gàm-tè ìn àmà hìh-sá thù-tè zā-khin ùh àhìh màn-ìn, híh gàm-tè pàn-ìn mihon tampi tak, àmà kìang-àh hòng pái ùh hì. \\
     \textsc{jerusalem} town \textsc{idumia} land \textsc{jordan} battle rebuke-\textsc{loc} village-big around and \textsc{sidon} village-big around-\textsc{nom} exist land-\textsc{pl} \textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{poss} be-\textsc{perf} word-\textsc{pl} hundred-more 2/3PL be.\textsc{3sg}.\textsc{rel} reason-\textsc{erg} this land-\textsc{pl} \textsc{abl}-\textsc{erg} poor.person many truly \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{poss} beside-\textsc{loc} \textsc{3→1} go 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{and from Jerusalem, and from Idumæa, and from beyond Jordan; and they about Tyre and Sidon, a great multitude, when they had heard what great things he did, came unto him.}}

\exi{9}
\gll Mihon-tè tám-lúa màhmàh àhìh màn-ìn àmaute ìn Jesuh à nèh-cìp-gàwp khàk lòh nàdìngìn àmà ōm nàdìng gunkuang khàt à kòih nà-dìng-ùn à nùng-zúi-tè à sawl hì. \\
     poor.person-\textsc{pl} many-exceed very be.\textsc{3sg}.\textsc{rel} reason-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{erg} \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{3sg} eat.\textsc{ii}-tightly-\textsc{intens} limit \textsc{neg}-\textsc{nom} \textsc{purp}.\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{poss} exist \textsc{purp} ship one \textsc{3sg} put \textsc{2sg}-\textsc{irr}-\textsc{imp} \textsc{3sg} life-follow-\textsc{pl} \textsc{3sg} send \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And he spake to his disciples, that a small ship should wait on him because of the multitude, lest they should throng him.}}

\exi{10}
\gll Àmàh ìn cin-à mì tampi damsak-khín àhìh màn-ìn, Jesuh à lawn-thèih nà-dìng-ùn cin-à khèmpeuh ìn àmàh hòng nàih ciat ùh hì. \\
     \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{erg} said-\textsc{loc} person many heal-\textsc{imm} be.\textsc{3sg}.\textsc{rel} reason-\textsc{erg} \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{3sg} cast-\textsc{abil} \textsc{2sg}-\textsc{irr}-\textsc{imp} said-\textsc{loc} all \textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{3→1} \textsc{2sg}-love each 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{For he had healed many; insomuch that they pressed upon him for to touch him, as many as had plagues.}}

\exi{11}
\gll Túa lái-tàk-ìn mì-tè' sùng-à lút dawi-tè ìn Jesuh à mùh ùh cìang-ìn à mái-àh pú-kin kiko ùh à, nàng pèn Pasian' Tá-pà nà hì hì à cí ùh hì. \\
     that midst-exact-\textsc{erg} person-\textsc{pl} inside-\textsc{3sg} enter demon-\textsc{pl} \textsc{erg} \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{3sg} see 2/3PL then-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} face-\textsc{loc} grandfather-god cry.out 2/3PL \textsc{3sg} \textsc{2sg}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{top} god child-male \textsc{2sg} \textsc{decl} \textsc{decl} \textsc{3sg} say 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And unclean spirits, when they saw him, fell down before him, and cried, saying, Thou art the Son of God.}}

\exi{12}
\gll Dawi-tè ìn àmàh kua mì àhì cìh-ná thù à gēn-khìat lòh nà-dìng-ùn Jesuh ìn nak-pì-tàk-ìn dawi-tè à khàm hì. \\
     demon-\textsc{pl} \textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{pro} who person be.\textsc{3sg} say.\textsc{nom}-\textsc{nmlz} word \textsc{3sg} speak-depart \textsc{neg}-\textsc{nom} \textsc{2sg}-\textsc{irr}-\textsc{imp} \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{erg} strong-big-exact-\textsc{erg} demon-\textsc{pl} \textsc{3sg} gold \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And he straitly charged them that they should not make him known.}}

\exi{13}
\gll Túa lái pàn-ìn à mual-tùng lām-àh Jesuh pái-tò à, mì à dèih-tèng àmà kìang-àh à sam hì. Túa à sap mì-tè àmà kìang-àh hòng pái ùh à, \\
     that midst \textsc{abl}-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} mountain-top way-\textsc{loc} \textsc{jesuh} go-\textsc{up} \textsc{3sg} person \textsc{3sg} want-all \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{poss} beside-\textsc{loc} \textsc{3sg} open \textsc{decl} that \textsc{3sg} call person-\textsc{pl} \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{poss} beside-\textsc{loc} \textsc{3→1} go 2/3PL \textsc{3sg} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And he goeth up into a mountain, and calleth unto him whom he would: and they came unto him.}}

\exi{14}
\gll àmàh ìn mì sàwm lè nìh teel-ìn, sawl-tàk-tè, cí-ìn mīn à phuah hì. Jesuh ìn, kèi tàwh à kikhawl dìng-ìn no-tèng kà hòng teel hì. Thù à hìlh dìng-ìn zòng kà hòng sawl dìng à, \\
     \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{erg} person ten and two choose-\textsc{cvb} send-exact-\textsc{pl} say-\textsc{quot} name \textsc{3sg} thunder \textsc{decl} \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{erg} \textsc{neg}.\textsc{emph} \textsc{com} \textsc{3sg} walk.with \textsc{irr}-\textsc{erg} young-until \textsc{1sg} \textsc{3→1} choose \textsc{decl} word \textsc{3sg} tell \textsc{irr}-\textsc{erg} also \textsc{1sg} \textsc{3→1} send \textsc{irr} \textsc{3sg} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And he ordained twelve, that they should be with him, and that he might send them forth to preach,}}

\exi{15}
\gll dawi hawl-khìat nàdìng vangliat-ná nà néi dìng ùh hì à cí hì. \\
     fear persecute \textsc{purp} strong-\textsc{nmlz} \textsc{2sg} have \textsc{irr} 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \textsc{3sg} say \textsc{decl} \\

\exi{16}
\gll Túa à teel mì sàwm lè nìh-tè: Simon jesuh ìn à mīn thàk dìng-ìn Peter à phuah pà, \\
     that \textsc{3sg} choose person ten and two-\textsc{pl} \textsc{simon} \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} name new \textsc{irr}-\textsc{erg} \textsc{peter} \textsc{3sg} thunder father \\

\exi{17}
\gll Zebedi' tá-pà James lè à naupa Johan jesuh ìn híh unau-tè pèn vang-ing bàng à cìh nòp-ná Boanerges mīn à phuah-tè, \\

\exi{18}

     \textsc{andru} \textsc{filip} ? \textsc{matthai} \textsc{thomas} \textsc{alfeas} child-male \textsc{james} \textsc{thaddeas} \textsc{simon} land sojourn father \\

\exi{19}

\exi{20}
\gll àmà kìang-àh mì-hon-pì hòng kī-khàwm-kík zèl àhìh màn-ìn Jesuh lè à nùng-zúi-tè ìn àn nà-ngawn né théi lò ùh hì. \\
     \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{poss} beside-\textsc{loc} person-multitude \textsc{3→1} \textsc{refl}-gather-\textsc{iter} scatter be.\textsc{3sg}.\textsc{rel} reason-\textsc{erg} \textsc{jesuh} and \textsc{3sg} life-follow-\textsc{pl} \textsc{erg} \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{poss} \textsc{2sg}-own eat know \textsc{neg} 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And the multitude cometh together again, so that they could not so much as eat bread.}}

\exi{21}
\gll À innkuanpih-tè ìn híh thù à zàk ùh cìang-ìn Jesuh à lá dìng-ìn hòng kúan-khìa ùh hì. Bàng hàng hìam cìh lèh, jesuh mihai sùak-tà hì à kī-cìh-ná thù à zá ùh hì. \\
     \textsc{3sg} household-\textsc{pl} \textsc{erg} this word \textsc{3sg} hear.\textsc{ii} 2/3PL then-\textsc{erg} \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{3sg} take \textsc{irr}-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3→1} family-\textsc{exit} 2/3PL \textsc{decl} like reason \textsc{q} say.\textsc{nom} and \textsc{jesuh} wise become-\textsc{pfv} \textsc{decl} \textsc{3sg} \textsc{refl}-say-\textsc{nmlz} word \textsc{3sg} hear 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And when his friends heard of it , they went out to lay hold on him: for they said, He is beside himself.}}

\exi{22}
\gll Jerusalem khùa pàn à hòng pái Thù-khàm hìlh sía-tè pàwl-khàt ìn, híh pà sùng-àh Beelzebul lút hì. Dawimangpa ìn àmà tùngàh dawi hawl-khìat thèih nàdìng vangliat-ná pía hì à cí ùh hì. \\

\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And the scribes which came down from Jerusalem said, He hath Beelzebub, and by the prince of the devils casteth he out devils.}}

\exi{23}

     that be.\textsc{3sg}.\textsc{rel} then-\textsc{erg} \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{poss} beside-\textsc{loc} person-\textsc{pl} call-\textsc{cvb} preach-measure-\textsc{nmlz} \textsc{com} word tell \textsc{3sg} \textsc{satan} \textsc{erg} \textsc{satan} how persecute know.\textsc{ii} \textsc{irr} be.\textsc{3sg} \textsc{q} \\

\exi{27}
\gll Mì tha-hàt-pá hèn-cìp masa lò-pì-ìn kuamah ìn mì tha-hàt-pá' ínn-sùng pàn à nèih-sa-te làk-sàk zò lò dìng hì. À hèn-cìp khìt cìang bèk-ìn laksak-zò pàn bèk dìng hì. \\
     person strength-strong-\textsc{nmlz} tie-tightly first \textsc{neg}-big-\textsc{erg} nobody \textsc{erg} person strength-strong-\textsc{nmlz} house-inside \textsc{abl} \textsc{3sg} possessions take-\textsc{caus} south \textsc{neg} \textsc{irr} \textsc{decl} \textsc{3sg} tie-tightly \textsc{seq} then sleep-\textsc{erg} redeem-\textsc{compl} \textsc{abl} only \textsc{irr} \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{No man can enter into a strong man's house, and spoil his goods, except he will first bind the strong man; and then he will spoil his house.}}

\exi{28}
\gll túa àhìh cìang-ìn híh thù phawk ùn! Mì-hìng-tè' màwh-ná lè à kam-pau sìat-ná-tè ùh ki-maisak théi dìng hì. \\
     that be.\textsc{3sg}.\textsc{rel} then-\textsc{erg} this word remember \textsc{imp}.\textsc{pl} person-kind-\textsc{pl} err-\textsc{nmlz} and \textsc{3sg} word-speak spoil-\textsc{nmlz}-\textsc{pl} 2/3PL appear know \textsc{irr} \textsc{decl} \\

\exi{29}
\gll Àhì zòng-ìn Khá Sìangtho langpang-ìn thù à gēn-tè ìn màwh-ná kip sù-khá ùh àhìh màn-ìn à màwh-ná ùh ki-maisak ngèi lò dìng hì à cí hì. \\

     person some-one-\textsc{pl} \textsc{erg} \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{erg} fear sick \textsc{decl} say 2/3PL be.\textsc{3sg}.\textsc{rel} reason-\textsc{erg} this like-\textsc{erg} word \textsc{3sg} speak be.\textsc{3sg} \textsc{decl} \\

\exi{31}

     that midst-exact-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} female and \textsc{3sg} child-\textsc{pl} \textsc{3→1} on 2/3PL \textsc{3sg} house outside-\textsc{loc} wait-\textsc{cvb} \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{3sg} open \textsc{irr}-\textsc{erg} person \textsc{3sg} send 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\

\exi{32}
\gll Àmà kiim-àh à tù mihonpi-tè ìn, nà nù lè nà nàu-tè, ínn pua-àh ōm ùh à, nàng hòng sam ùh hì à cí ùh hì. \\
     \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{poss} around-\textsc{loc} \textsc{3sg} now noble-\textsc{pl} \textsc{erg} \textsc{2sg} female and \textsc{2sg} child-\textsc{pl} house carry.on.back-\textsc{loc} exist 2/3PL \textsc{3sg} \textsc{2sg}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{3→1} open 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \textsc{3sg} say 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\

     \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{erg} \textsc{1sg} female and \textsc{1sg} child-\textsc{pl} \textsc{1pl}.\textsc{incl} say.\textsc{nom} who-\textsc{pl} be.\textsc{3sg} \textsc{q} say-\textsc{quot} \textsc{3sg} until \textsc{decl} \\

\exi{34}

\exi{35}
\gll Pasian' deihna bàng-ìn à gamta mì khèmpeuh kà nù lè kà sanggam-tè àhì ùh hì à cí hì. \\
     god desire like-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} send.away person all \textsc{1sg} female and \textsc{1sg} brother-\textsc{pl} be.\textsc{3sg} 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \textsc{3sg} say \textsc{decl} \\

\newpage

\section*{Chapter 4}
\addcontentsline{toc}{section}{Chapter 4}

\begin{exe}
\exi{1}
\gll Jesuh ìn Galilee Tùi-li gei-àh thù-hìlh dìng ki-pan-kík leuleu hì. Àmà kiim-àh à kī-khàwm mì-tè tám-lúa àhìh màn-ìn gunkuang sùng-àh pái-ìn à tù hì. À gunkuang pèn tùi tùngàh ōm à, mihonpi-tè ahihleh tùi-gei leilak-àh ōm ùh hì. \\
     \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{erg} \textsc{galilee} water-flow edge-\textsc{loc} word-teach \textsc{irr} begin-\textsc{iter} again \textsc{decl} \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{poss} around-\textsc{loc} \textsc{3sg} \textsc{refl}-gather person-\textsc{pl} many-exceed be.\textsc{3sg}.\textsc{rel} reason-\textsc{erg} ship inside-\textsc{loc} go-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} now \textsc{decl} \textsc{3sg} ship \textsc{top} water on-\textsc{loc} exist \textsc{3sg} noble-\textsc{pl} if water-edge ground-\textsc{loc} exist 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And he began again to teach by the sea side: and there was gathered unto him a great multitude, so that he entered into a ship, and sat in the sea; and the whole multitude was by the sea on the land.}}

\exi{2}
\gll Àmàh ìn thugen-teh-ná tàwh thù tampi hìlh à, à thù-hìlh-ná-àh: \\
     \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{erg} preach-measure-\textsc{nmlz} \textsc{com} word many tell \textsc{3sg} \textsc{3sg} word-teach-\textsc{nmlz}-\textsc{loc} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And he taught them many things by parables, and said unto them in his doctrine,}}

\exi{3}
\gll ngái ùn! Khaici vawh-pà, khaici vawh dìng-ìn à kúan-khìa hì. \\
     listen.\textsc{i} \textsc{imp}.\textsc{pl} sow go.and-male sow name \textsc{irr}-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} family-\textsc{exit} \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{Hearken; Behold, there went out a sower to sow:}}

\exi{4}
\gll Khaici à vawh cìang-ìn pàwl-khàt-tè lām-dung tù à, và-sá-tè hòng leeng-ìn tàwm-ìn à né ùh hì. \\
     sow \textsc{3sg} name then-\textsc{erg} some-one-\textsc{pl} way-straight now \textsc{3sg} go.and-\textsc{past}-\textsc{pl} \textsc{3→1} chariot-\textsc{erg} \textsc{dimin}-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} eat 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{and it came to pass, as he sowed, some fell by the way side, and the fowls of the air came and devoured it up.}}

\exi{5}
\gll Pàwl-khàt-tè léi-hòih à sah lòh-ná mùn, suang à kī-taw-phah tùng tù à, léi sah lò àhìh màn-ìn thàk-hàt-ìn po-pah hì. \\
     some-one-\textsc{pl} earth-good \textsc{3sg} witness \textsc{neg}-\textsc{nmlz} place stone \textsc{3sg} \textsc{refl}-receive-place on now \textsc{3sg} buy witness \textsc{neg} be.\textsc{3sg}.\textsc{rel} reason-\textsc{erg} new-strong-\textsc{erg} spring-up \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And some fell on stony ground, where it had not much earth; and immediately it sprang up, because it had no depth of earth:}}

\exi{6}
\gll Túa àn-kungno-tè ìn zung thuk khá zò lò àhìh màn-ìn nì-sá ìn à kàt cìang-ìn à kēu-túm-pah ùh hì. \\
     that food-desire-\textsc{pl} \textsc{erg} root deep \textsc{neg}.\textsc{perf} south \textsc{neg} be.\textsc{3sg}.\textsc{rel} reason-\textsc{erg} day-hot \textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} catch then-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} scratch-sun-strike 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{but when the sun was up, it was scorched; and because it had no root, it withered away.}}

\exi{7}
\gll Pàwl-khàt-tè lingbul-sum ōm-ná lāk tù à, ling-tè hòng sel-ìn dep-gàwp àhìh màn-ìn bangmah gah-zò lò hì. \\

\exi{36}
\gll Túa àhìh cìang-ìn à nùng-zúi-tè ìn mihonpi-tè nusia-ìn Jesuh à nà tūan-ná-sá gunkuang tùngàh kà-hí-n à gunkuang tàwh à pái-khìat-pìh ùh hì. Gunkuang dàng-tè ìn zòng àmau à zúi ùh hì. \\
     that be.\textsc{3sg}.\textsc{rel} then-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} life-follow-\textsc{pl} \textsc{erg} noble-\textsc{pl} abandon-\textsc{erg} \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{3sg} \textsc{2sg} ride-\textsc{nmlz}-\textsc{perf} ship on-\textsc{loc} \textsc{1sg}-be-\textsc{pst} \textsc{3sg} ship \textsc{com} \textsc{3sg} go-emerge-\textsc{appl} 2/3PL \textsc{decl} ship other-\textsc{pl} \textsc{erg} also \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{3sg} follow 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And when they had sent away the multitude, they took him even as he was in the ship. And there were also with him other little ships.}}

\exi{37}
\gll Túa lái-tàk-ìn nak-pì-tàk-ìn huih-pì hòng nùng à, tùi-hual hòng ōm-ìn gunkuang sùng-àh tùi hòng dim dek-tàk hì. \\
     that midst-exact-\textsc{erg} strong-big-exact-\textsc{erg} wind-great \textsc{3→1} later \textsc{3sg} water-wave \textsc{3→1} exist-\textsc{cvb} ship inside-\textsc{loc} water \textsc{3→1} full low-true \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And there arose a great storm of wind, and the waves beat into the ship, so that it was now full.}}

\exi{38}
\gll Jesuh pèn gunkuang nùng lām-àh lù-khàm khàm-ìn ì-mú-ìn à ōm hì. À nùng-zúi-tè ìn àmàh phong-ìn, sía àw, kòtè sit-à lè ung phamawh hòng sá lò nà hì hìam à cí ùh hì. \\
     \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{top} ship later way-\textsc{loc} head-cover forbid-\textsc{cvb} \textsc{1pl}.\textsc{incl}-see-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} exist \textsc{decl} \textsc{3sg} life-follow-\textsc{pl} \textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{pro} reveal-\textsc{cvb} evil voice \textsc{1pl}.\textsc{pro} cut.off-\textsc{loc} and \textsc{pl}.\textsc{fut} necessary \textsc{3→1} flesh \textsc{neg} \textsc{2sg} \textsc{decl} \textsc{q} \textsc{3sg} say 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And he was in the hinder part of the ship, asleep on a pillow: and they awake him, and say unto him, Master, carest thou not that we perish?}}

\exi{39}
\gll Jesuh zòng tho-ìn, nùng nàwn kèi ìn cí-ìn huih-pì thù pía à, tuihual-tè kìang-àh, kī-lok nàwn kèi ùn à cí hì. Túa cìang-ìn huih-nùng khawl-ìn dai khip-khep pah hì. \\
     \textsc{jesuh} also rise-\textsc{erg} later \textsc{cont} \textsc{neg}.\textsc{emph} \textsc{erg} say-\textsc{quot} wind-great word give \textsc{3sg} flood-\textsc{pl} beside-\textsc{loc} \textsc{refl}-shake \textsc{cont} \textsc{neg}.\textsc{emph} \textsc{imp}.\textsc{pl} \textsc{3sg} say \textsc{decl} that then-\textsc{erg} wind-continue rest-\textsc{erg} still wind-calm do.so \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And he arose, and rebuked the wind, and said unto the sea, Peace, be still. And the wind ceased, and there was a great calm.}}

\exi{40}
\gll Túa cìang-ìn Jesuh ìn à nùng-zúi-tè kìang-àh, bàng hàng-ìn lau nà hì ùh hìam? Tù cìang dòng up-ná néi nái lò nà hì ùh hìam à cí hì. \\
     that then-\textsc{erg} \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} life-follow-\textsc{pl} beside-\textsc{loc} like because-\textsc{erg} fear \textsc{2sg} \textsc{decl} 2/3PL \textsc{q} now then until believe-\textsc{nmlz} have near \textsc{neg} \textsc{2sg} \textsc{decl} 2/3PL \textsc{q} \textsc{3sg} say \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And he said unto them, Why are ye so fearful? how is it that ye have no faith?}}

\exi{41}
\gll À nùng-zúi-tè ìn lamdang-sá màhmàh ùh à, huih-pì lè tuihual-tè nà-ngawn, àmà sawl bàng-ìn à gamta ùh hì à cí ùh hì. \\
     \textsc{3sg} life-follow-\textsc{pl} \textsc{erg} different-\textsc{intns} very 2/3PL \textsc{3sg} wind-great and flood-\textsc{pl} \textsc{2sg}-own \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{poss} send like-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} send.away 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \textsc{3sg} say 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And they feared exceedingly, and said one to another, What manner of man is this, that even the wind and the sea obey him?}}

\end{exe}

\section*{Chapter 5}
\addcontentsline{toc}{section}{Chapter 5}

\begin{exe}
\exi{1}
\gll Túa cìang-ìn Jesuh lè à nùng-zúi-tè Galilee Tùi-li galkhat, Gadara mì-tè' gàm sùng à tùng ùh hì. \\
     that then-\textsc{erg} \textsc{jesuh} and \textsc{3sg} life-follow-\textsc{pl} \textsc{galilee} water-flow battle \textsc{gadara} person-\textsc{pl} land inside \textsc{3sg} on 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\

\exi{2}
\gll Gunkuang tùng pàn-ìn Jesuh à kúm-sùk khìt phèt-ìn, han lāk pàn-ìn à hòng pái mì khàt ìn nà dawntuah hì. \\
     ship on \textsc{abl}-\textsc{erg} \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{3sg} bow-\textsc{down} \textsc{seq} twin-\textsc{erg} sepulchre among \textsc{abl}-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} \textsc{3→1} go person one \textsc{erg} \textsc{2sg} meet \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And when he was come out of the ship, immediately there met him out of the tombs a man with an unclean spirit,}}

\exi{3}
\gll Híh mipa dawivei hì à, han lāk-àh à tèng hì. Kuamah ìn híh mipa, sìk-khau tàwh hèn-zò nàwn lò ùh hì. \\
     this man devil \textsc{decl} \textsc{3sg} sepulchre among-\textsc{loc} \textsc{3sg} remain \textsc{decl} nobody \textsc{erg} this man iron-chain \textsc{com} tie-\textsc{compl} \textsc{cont} \textsc{neg} 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{who had his dwelling among the tombs; and no man could bind him, no, not with chains:}}

\exi{4}
\gll Tám-véi-pì tak, à khùt lè à khe, sìk-khau tàwh kī-hèn khín ngèi à, àhì zòng-ìn à kī-hèn sìm-ìn à sikkhau-tè bot-sat-ìn, à khe-à kī-bùlh kol-tè à sù-khàm gàwp hì. Àmàh hàt-lúa àhìh màn-ìn kuamah ìn híh zò lò hì. \\
     many-time-great truly \textsc{3sg} hand and \textsc{3sg} foot iron-chain \textsc{com} \textsc{refl}-tie \textsc{imm} \textsc{exp} \textsc{3sg} be.\textsc{3sg} although-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} \textsc{refl}-tie count-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} bond-\textsc{pl} break-thread-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} foot-\textsc{loc} \textsc{refl}-root wheel-\textsc{pl} \textsc{3sg} touch-reach all \textsc{decl} \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{pro} strong-exceed be.\textsc{3sg}.\textsc{rel} reason-\textsc{erg} nobody \textsc{erg} this south \textsc{neg} \textsc{decl} \\

\exi{5}
\gll Sun lè zān-ìn han lāk lè mual-tùng tèng-àh vák kawi-kawi à, áwng gàwp-ìn, suang hí-am-tè tàwh àmàh à kī-kui-liam hì. \\
     basket and night-\textsc{erg} sepulchre among and mountain-top dwell-\textsc{loc} walk crooked\textasciitilde{}REDUP \textsc{3sg} open \textsc{intens}-\textsc{erg} stone be-sink-\textsc{pl} \textsc{com} \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{3sg} \textsc{refl}-ring-joint \textsc{decl} \\

\exi{6}

\exi{8}

     this like-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} say.\textsc{nom}-\textsc{nmlz} \textsc{top} \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{erg} fear voice this man inside \textsc{abl}-\textsc{erg} go-exit \textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} say.\textsc{nom}-\textsc{nmlz} reason be.\textsc{3sg} \textsc{decl} \\

\exi{9}

Túa vòk hon-pì-tè à vèk-pì-ìn tulnih bàng phà hì. Mual-tùng pàn-ìn tái-sùk henhan ùh à, tùi-li sùng kī-den-ná-ìn tùi-kía mangkhin ùh hì. \\

\exi{14}
