\exi{25}
\gll Túa-tè lāk-àh, kúm sàwm lè nìh sùng tàwn-tùng sí-luang nat-ná à néi nu-méi khàt à ōm hì. \\
     \textsc{dist}-\textsc{pl} among-\textsc{loc} year ten and two inside ever-always die-flow ill-\textsc{nmlz} \textsc{3sg} have woman one \textsc{3sg} exist \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And a certain woman, which had an issue of blood twelve years,}}

\exi{26}
\gll Sía-vuan tampi ìn àmàh bāwl à, à sum nèih khèmpeuh zàng-khín ná-pì-ìn nòp-tuam-zàw lò-ìn gìm sèm-sèm-zàw hì. \\
     sick-heal many \textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{pro} make \textsc{3sg} \textsc{3sg} extinguish have-\textsc{nom} all use-\textsc{imm} manner-big-\textsc{erg} like-also-more \textsc{neg}-\textsc{erg} faint serve\textasciitilde{}REDUP-more \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{and had suffered many things of many physicians, and had spent all that she had, and was nothing bettered, but rather grew worse,}}

\exi{27}
\gll Túa nu-méi ìn Jesuh' thù zá àhìh màn-ìn mihon-tè kawm-àh Jesuh' nùng à zúi hì. \\
     that woman \textsc{erg} \textsc{jesuh} word hear be.\textsc{3sg}.\textsc{rel} reason-\textsc{erg} poor.person-\textsc{pl} beam-\textsc{loc} \textsc{jesuh} later \textsc{3sg} follow \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{when she had heard of Jesus, came in the press behind, and touched his garment.}}

\exi{28}
\gll Túa nù ìn, à pùan mong nà-ngawn và lawngkha leng, dām ning cí-ìn à ngaihsun hì. \\
     that female \textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} cloth hem \textsc{2sg}-own go.and touch line good will say-\textsc{quot} \textsc{3sg} think \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{For she said, If I may touch but his clothes, I shall be whole.}}

\exi{29}
\gll À và lawn-khit phèt-ìn à sí-luang khawl-pah à, àmà sùng-à à nat-ná à dām-lam à ki-phawk hì. \\
     \textsc{3sg} go.and look-recover twin-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} die-flow dry-\textsc{compl} \textsc{3sg} \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{poss} inside-\textsc{3sg} \textsc{3sg} ill-\textsc{nmlz} \textsc{3sg} be.well-\textsc{toward} \textsc{3sg} remember \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And straightway the fountain of her blood was dried up; and she felt in her body that she was healed of that plague.}}

\exi{30}
\gll Jesuh ìn àmà sùng pàn-ìn à vangliat-ná à pái-khìat-lam phawk-pah àhìh màn-ìn mihonpi-tè lāk-àh khùa-dāk-ìn, kua ìn kà pùan hòng lawng nà hì ùh hìam à cí hì. \\
     \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{poss} inside \textsc{abl}-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} strong-\textsc{nmlz} \textsc{3sg} go-out-direction touch-exactly be.\textsc{3sg}.\textsc{rel} reason-\textsc{erg} noble-\textsc{pl} among-\textsc{loc} town-division-\textsc{erg} who \textsc{erg} \textsc{1sg} cloth \textsc{3→1} touch \textsc{2sg} \textsc{decl} 2/3PL \textsc{q} \textsc{3sg} say \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And Jesus, immediately knowing in himself that virtue had gone out of him, turned him about in the press, and said, Who touched my clothes?}}

\exi{31}
\gll À nùng-zúi-tè ìn, mihonpi-tè ìn nàng hòng nèh-cìh-lam nà théi hì. Bàng hàng-ìn kua ìn hòng lawng nà hì ùh hìam, cí màwk nà hì hìam à cí ùh hì. \\
     \textsc{3sg} life-follow-\textsc{pl} \textsc{erg} noble-\textsc{pl} \textsc{erg} \textsc{2sg}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{3→1} eat.\textsc{ii}-say.\textsc{nom}-\textsc{toward} \textsc{2sg} know \textsc{decl} like because-\textsc{erg} who \textsc{erg} \textsc{3→1} touch \textsc{2sg} \textsc{decl} 2/3PL \textsc{q} say perhaps \textsc{2sg} \textsc{decl} \textsc{q} \textsc{3sg} say 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And his disciples said unto him, Thou seest the multitude thronging thee, and sayest thou, Who touched me?}}

\exi{32}
\gll Àhì zòng-ìn àmàh à lawng-tè à thèih nàdìngìn Jesuh khùa-dāk kawi-kawi lái hì. \\
     be.\textsc{3sg} although-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{3sg} look-\textsc{pl} \textsc{3sg} know.\textsc{ii} \textsc{purp}.\textsc{erg} \textsc{jesuh} town-near crooked\textasciitilde{}REDUP midst \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And he looked round about to see her that had done this thing.}}

\exi{33}
\gll Túa nu-méi ìn àmà tùngà thù-piang théi àhìh màn-ìn lau-kawm ling-kawm-ìn hòng pái-ìn à khe-phung-àh hòng bok à, à thù-piang khèmpeuh àhì bàng-bàng-ìn à hòng gēn hì. \\
     that woman \textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{poss} on-\textsc{3sg} word-born know be.\textsc{3sg}.\textsc{rel} reason-\textsc{erg} fear-edge tremble-together-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3→1} go-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} foot-group-\textsc{loc} \textsc{3→1} fall \textsc{3sg} \textsc{3sg} word-born all be.\textsc{3sg} what-\textsc{redup}-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} \textsc{3→1} speak \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{But the woman fearing and trembling, knowing what was done in her, came and fell down before him, and told him all the truth.}}

\exi{34}
\gll Jesuh ìn zòng túa nù kìang-àh, kà tá-nù àw, nà up-ná ìn nàng hòng damsak-zò hì. Cidamsuak ìnlà, lùng-nuam takin và ciah ìn à cí hì. \\
     \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{erg} also that female beside-\textsc{loc} \textsc{1sg} child-female voice \textsc{2sg} believe-\textsc{nmlz} \textsc{erg} \textsc{2sg}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{3→1} heal-\textsc{compl} \textsc{decl} ? and.then heart-pleased really go.and return \textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} say \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And he said unto her, Daughter, thy faith hath made thee whole; go in peace, and be whole of thy plague.}}

\exi{35}
\gll Túa lái-tàk-ìn kī-khòp-ná ínn ùk-pà' ínn pàn-ìn kamtai-tè hòng tùng ùh à, nà tá-nù sí khin-tá hì. Bàng hàng-ìn Sía-pa màwk gimsak nàwn dìng nà hì hìam à cí ùh hì. \\
     that midst-exact-\textsc{erg} \textsc{refl}-gather-\textsc{nmlz} house rule-male house \textsc{abl}-\textsc{erg} messenger-\textsc{pl} \textsc{3→1} on 2/3PL \textsc{3sg} \textsc{2sg} child-female die move-\textsc{nmlz} \textsc{decl} like because-\textsc{erg} evil-man perhaps judge \textsc{cont} \textsc{irr} \textsc{2sg} \textsc{decl} \textsc{q} \textsc{3sg} say 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{While he yet spake, there came from the ruler of the synagogue's house certain which said, Thy daughter is dead: why troublest thou the Master any further?}}

\exi{36}
\gll Àhì zòng-ìn Jesuh ìn àmau thù ki-gēn don lò-ìn kī-khòp-ná ínn ùk-pà kìang-àh, lùng-himawh kèi ìn; up-ná néi pèuh ìn à cí hì. \\
     be.\textsc{3sg} although-\textsc{erg} \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{erg} \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{pro} word conversation regard \textsc{neg}-\textsc{erg} \textsc{refl}-gather-\textsc{nmlz} house rule-male beside-\textsc{loc} heart-fear \textsc{neg}.\textsc{emph} \textsc{erg} believe-\textsc{nmlz} have every \textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} say \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{As soon as Jesus heard the word that was spoken, he saith unto the ruler of the synagogue, Be not afraid, only believe.}}

\exi{37}
\gll Túa lái pàn-ìn Jesuh ìn Peter lè James lè à nàu Johan longal kuamah dàng kī-zuisak nàwn lò hì. \\
     that midst \textsc{abl}-\textsc{erg} \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{erg} \textsc{peter} and \textsc{james} and \textsc{3sg} child \textsc{johan} save nobody other \textsc{refl}-follow.for \textsc{cont} \textsc{neg} \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And he suffered no man to follow him, save Peter, and James, and John the brother of James.}}

\exi{38}
\gll Kī-khòp-ná ínn ùk-pà' ínn à tun ùh cìang-ìn mì-tè' kàh-ná lè thùm-ná, à gam-lum-na ùh à mú hì. \\
     \textsc{refl}-gather-\textsc{nmlz} house rule-male house \textsc{3sg} arrive 2/3PL then-\textsc{erg} person-\textsc{pl} fight-\textsc{nmlz} and three-\textsc{nmlz} \textsc{3sg} south 2/3PL \textsc{3sg} see.\textsc{i} \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And he cometh to the house of the ruler of the synagogue, and seeth the tumult, and them that wept and wailed greatly.}}

\exi{39}
\gll Àmàh sùng-túm-ìn, bàng hàng-ìn hi-cí gàm-lum nà hì ùh hìam? Bàng hàng-ìn kàp nà hì ùh hìam? Numei-no à sí hì lò hì; à ìh-mú hí-bèk hì à cí hì. \\
     \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{pro} inside-all-\textsc{erg} like because-\textsc{erg} this-say land-round \textsc{2sg} \textsc{decl} 2/3PL \textsc{q} like because-\textsc{erg} weep \textsc{2sg} \textsc{decl} 2/3PL \textsc{q} woman-young \textsc{3sg} die \textsc{decl} \textsc{neg} \textsc{decl} \textsc{3sg} \textsc{1pl}-see be-sleep \textsc{decl} \textsc{3sg} say \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And when he was come in, he saith unto them, Why make ye this ado, and weep? the damsel is not dead, but sleepeth.}}

\exi{40}
\gll Àmaute ìn Jesuh zah-pìh bāwl-ìn nùih-sān ùh àhìh màn-ìn Jesuh ìn àmaute khèmpeuh pusuak-sàk à, numei-no' pà lè à nù, lè à nùng-zúi thùm-tè tàwh, numei-no' lupna ínn-déi-àh à pái ùh hì. \\
     \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{erg} \textsc{jesuh} fear-\textsc{appl} make-\textsc{cvb} laugh-at 2/3PL be.\textsc{3sg}.\textsc{rel} reason-\textsc{erg} \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{erg} \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{pro} all mouth-\textsc{caus} \textsc{3sg} woman-young father and \textsc{3sg} female and \textsc{3sg} life-follow three-\textsc{pl} \textsc{com} woman-young bed house-chamber-\textsc{loc} \textsc{3sg} go 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And they laughed him to scorn. But when he had put them all out, he taketh the father and the mother of the damsel, and them that were with him, and entereth in where the damsel was lying.}}

\exi{41}
\gll Túa cìang-ìn numei-no' khùt len-ìn, numei-no àw, tho ìn à cìh-ná,  Talitha kumi  à cí hì. \\
     that then-\textsc{erg} woman-young hand net-\textsc{erg} woman-young voice rise \textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} say.\textsc{nom}-\textsc{nmlz}  \textsc{talitha} arise  \textsc{3sg} say \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And he took the damsel by the hand, and said unto her, Talitha cumi; which is, being interpreted, Damsel, I say unto thee, arise.}}

\exi{42}
\gll Numei-no zòng thàk-hàt-ìn tho-ìn lām à pái-pah hì. àmàh kúm sàwm lè nìh phà tá hì Túa cìang-ìn àmaute ìn lamdang-sá màhmàh ùh hì. \\
     woman-young also new-strong-\textsc{erg} rise-\textsc{erg} way \textsc{3sg} go-arrive \textsc{decl} \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{pro} year ten and two branch child \textsc{decl} that then-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{erg} different-\textsc{intns} very 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And straightway the damsel arose, and walked; for she was of the age of twelve years. And they were astonished with a great astonishment.}}

\exi{43}
\gll Híh thù, kuama kìang-àh à gēn lòh nà-dìng-ùn Jesuh ìn nak-pì-tàk-ìn àmaute khàm à, túa cìang-ìn, numei-no àn pía ùn cí-ìn à sawl hì. \\
     this word charge beside-\textsc{loc} \textsc{3sg} speak \textsc{neg}-\textsc{nom} \textsc{2sg}-\textsc{irr}-\textsc{imp} \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{erg} strong-big-exact-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{pro} gold \textsc{3sg} that then-\textsc{erg} woman-young \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{poss} give \textsc{imp}.\textsc{pl} say-\textsc{quot} \textsc{3sg} send \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And he charged them straitly that no man should know it; and commanded that something should be given her to eat.}}

\end{exe}
\newpage

\section*{Chapter 6}
\addcontentsline{toc}{section}{Chapter 6}

\begin{exe}
\exi{1}
\gll Túa lái pàn-ìn àmà pian-ná khùa Nazareth-àh Jesuh pái à, à nùng-zúi-tè ìn à zúi ùh hì. \\
     that midst \textsc{abl}-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{poss} birth-\textsc{nmlz} town \textsc{nazareth}-\textsc{loc} \textsc{jesuh} go \textsc{3sg} \textsc{3sg} life-follow-\textsc{pl} \textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} follow 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And he went out from thence, and came into his own country; and his disciples follow him.}}

\exi{2}
\gll À Sabbath nì cìang-ìn kī-khòp-ná ínn-àh thù à hìlh hì. Àmà thù-hìlh à zá mì tám-pì-tè ìn lamdang-sá-ìn, híh pà ìn híh thù-tè koi pàn-ìn à ngàh àhì hìam? Híh pà tùngàh à ki-pía pilna à bàng pilna àhì hìam? Bangci-ìn na-lam-dàng hi-cí bāwl-thèih àhì hìam? \\
     \textsc{3sg} \textsc{sabbath} day then-\textsc{erg} \textsc{refl}-gather-\textsc{nmlz} house-\textsc{loc} word \textsc{3sg} tell \textsc{decl} \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{poss} word-teach \textsc{3sg} hear person many-big-\textsc{pl} \textsc{erg} different-\textsc{intns}-\textsc{erg} this father \textsc{erg} this word-\textsc{pl} whence \textsc{abl}-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} get be.\textsc{3sg} \textsc{q} this father on-\textsc{loc} \textsc{3sg} be.given learning \textsc{3sg} like learning be.\textsc{3sg} \textsc{q} how.\textsc{erg} \textsc{nmlz}-other.way this-say make-\textsc{abil} be.\textsc{3sg} \textsc{q} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And when the sabbath day was come, he began to teach in the synagogue: and many hearing him were astonished, saying, From whence hath this man these things? and what wisdom is this which is given unto him, that even such mighty works are wrought by his hands?}}

\exi{3}
\gll Àmàh khùt-sìam-pá hí-lel à, Mary' tá-pà hì lò àhì hìam? James, Josef, Judas, lè Simon-tè' u hì lò àhì hìam? À nàu numei-tè zòng híh lái màh à ōm hì lò àhì ùh hìam à cí ùh hì. Túa hì à, àmàh sàng-zò lò ùh hì. \\
     \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{pro} hand-make-\textsc{nmlz} be-hold \textsc{3sg} \textsc{mary} child-male \textsc{decl} \textsc{neg} be.\textsc{3sg} \textsc{q} \textsc{james} \textsc{josef} \textsc{judas} and \textsc{simon}-\textsc{pl} elder.sibling \textsc{decl} \textsc{neg} be.\textsc{3sg} \textsc{q} \textsc{3sg} child woman-\textsc{pl} also this midst \textsc{emph} \textsc{3sg} exist \textsc{decl} \textsc{neg} be.\textsc{3sg} 2/3PL \textsc{q} \textsc{3sg} say 2/3PL \textsc{decl} that \textsc{decl} \textsc{3sg} \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{pro} high-\textsc{compl} \textsc{neg} 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{Is not this the carpenter, the son of Mary, the brother of James, and Joses, and of Juda, and Simon? and are not his sisters here with us? And they were offended at him.}}

\exi{4}
\gll Túa cìang-ìn Jesuh ìn àmaute kìang-àh, kamsang khàt pèn, àmà khùa, àmà beh-tè, lè àmà ínn-sùng longal-àh kī-zahtak-ìn pah-tawi-ná à ngàh hì à cí hì. \\
     that then-\textsc{erg} \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{erg} \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{pro} beside-\textsc{loc} prophet one \textsc{top} \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{poss} town \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{poss} tribe-\textsc{pl} and \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{poss} house-inside save-\textsc{loc} \textsc{refl}-honor-\textsc{cvb} do-honor-\textsc{nmlz} \textsc{3sg} get \textsc{decl} \textsc{3sg} say \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{But Jesus said unto them, A prophet is not without honour, but in his own country, and among his own kin, and in his own house.}}

\exi{5}
\gll Túa hì à, cin-à tàwm-khàt-tè tùngàh khùt ngái-ìn à dām-sàk cìh sìm-lòh, túa lái-àh na-lam-dàng lìan bāwl théi lò hì. \\
     that \textsc{decl} \textsc{3sg} said-\textsc{loc} few-one-\textsc{pl} on-\textsc{loc} hand listen.\textsc{i}-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} well-\textsc{caus} say.\textsc{nom} count-unable that midst-\textsc{loc} \textsc{nmlz}-other.way great make know \textsc{neg} \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And he could there do no mighty work, save that he laid his hands upon a few sick folk, and healed them .}}

\exi{6}
\gll Àmaute ìn àmàh à up-lòh màn-ìn lam-dàng à sá màhmàh hì. Túa cìang-ìn túa kiim-à ōm khùa-néu-tè-àh thù-hìlh-ìn à pái kawi-kawi hì. \\
     \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{3sg} look-\textsc{neg} reason-\textsc{erg} other.way \textsc{3sg} flesh very \textsc{decl} that then-\textsc{erg} that around-\textsc{nom} exist village-small-\textsc{pl}-\textsc{loc} word-teach-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} go crooked\textasciitilde{}REDUP \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And he marvelled because of their unbelief. And he went round about the villages, teaching.}}

\exi{7}
\gll Jesuh ìn sàwm lè nìh-tè sam à, àmaute tùngàh dawi hawl-khìat nàdìng vangliat-ná pía-ìn, àmaute nìh nihin à sawlkhia hì. \\
     \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{erg} ten and two-\textsc{pl} open \textsc{3sg} \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{pro} on-\textsc{loc} fear persecute \textsc{purp} strong-\textsc{nmlz} give-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{pro} two today \textsc{3sg} send.forth \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And he called unto him the twelve, and began to send them forth by two and two; and gave them power over unclean spirits;}}

\exi{8}
\gll Àmaute kìang-àh, cìang-khùt sìm-lòh, nà khual-zìn-ná uhah bangmah keng kèi ùn. Àn àhì à, ip àhì à, sum àhì zòng-ìn keng kèi ùn. \\
     \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{pro} beside-\textsc{loc} then-hand count-unable \textsc{2sg} sojourn-travel-\textsc{nmlz} 2/3PL.\textsc{loc} nothing only \textsc{neg}.\textsc{emph} \textsc{imp}.\textsc{pl} \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{poss} be.\textsc{3sg} \textsc{3sg} cover be.\textsc{3sg} \textsc{3sg} extinguish be.\textsc{3sg} although-\textsc{erg} only \textsc{neg}.\textsc{emph} \textsc{imp}.\textsc{pl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{and commanded them that they should take nothing for their journey, save a staff only; no scrip, no bread, no money in their purse:}}

\exi{9}
\gll Khedap bùlh ùn-lá, àhì zòng-ìn pùan-āk nìh silh-thuah kèi ùn. \\
     shoe bind \textsc{pl}.\textsc{imp}-and be.\textsc{3sg} although-\textsc{erg} cloth-put two clothe-always \textsc{neg}.\textsc{emph} \textsc{imp}.\textsc{pl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{but be shod with sandals; and not put on two coats.}}

\exi{10}
\gll À zìn dìng-ìn à hòng dèih ínn khàt peuhpeuh-àh tùng ùn-lá, túa khùa pàn-ìn nà pai-khìat mateng ùh túa ínn màh-àh ōm pái-sùak ùn. \\
     \textsc{3sg} travel \textsc{irr}-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} \textsc{3→1} want house one whatsoever-\textsc{loc} on \textsc{pl}.\textsc{imp}-and that town \textsc{abl}-\textsc{erg} \textsc{2sg} go.out until 2/3PL that house likewise-\textsc{loc} exist go-become \textsc{imp}.\textsc{pl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And he said unto them, In what place soever ye enter into an house, there abide till ye depart from that place.}}

\exi{11}
\gll Nà pái-ná ùh khùa khàt-pèuh ìn nòtè hòng sàng lò-ìn, nà thù-hìlh-ná ùh hòng ngàih-nòp kèi uhleh, túa khùa nusia-ìn, nà khe uha leivui bàng-tè sín-sān ùn. Túa pèn àmaute à dìng-ìn hìlh-kholh-ná àhì hì cí-ìn à vái-khàk hì. \\
     \textsc{2sg} go-\textsc{nmlz} 2/3PL town one-every \textsc{erg} \textsc{2pl}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{3→1} high \textsc{neg}-\textsc{erg} \textsc{2sg} word-teach-\textsc{nmlz} 2/3PL \textsc{3→1} hear-want \textsc{neg}.\textsc{emph} 2/3PL.if that town abandon-\textsc{erg} \textsc{2sg} foot 2/3PL.\textsc{loc} dust what-\textsc{pl} shake\textasciitilde{}REDUP \textsc{imp}.\textsc{pl} that \textsc{top} \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{3sg} \textsc{irr}-\textsc{erg} teach-\textsc{intens}-\textsc{nmlz} be.\textsc{3sg} \textsc{decl} say-\textsc{quot} \textsc{3sg} go-command \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And whosoever shall not receive you, nor hear you, when ye depart thence, shake off the dust under your feet for a testimony against them. Verily I say unto you, It shall be more tolerable for Sodom and Gomorrha in the day of judgment, than for that city.}}

\exi{12}
\gll Túa àhìh cìang-ìn àmaute kúan-khìa ùh à, mì-tè à màwh-ná pà-nun à kī-sìk nà-dìng-ùn thù à hìlh ùh hì. \\
     that be.\textsc{3sg}.\textsc{rel} then-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{pro} family-\textsc{exit} 2/3PL \textsc{3sg} person-\textsc{pl} \textsc{3sg} err-\textsc{nmlz} father-life \textsc{3sg} \textsc{refl}-turn \textsc{2sg}-\textsc{irr}-\textsc{imp} word \textsc{3sg} tell 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\

\gll Túa cìang-ìn Jesuh ìn à anlum nga lè à ngasa tàwn nìh-tè lá à, vàn-tùng lām ēn-tò-ìn Pasian tùngàh lungdam-ná à ko hì. À àn-lum-tè balnen à, mì-tè tùngàh à pìak dìng-ìn nùng-zúi-tè à pía hì. Túa màh bàng-ìn ngasa tàwn nìh-tè zòng àmaute khèmpeuh à hawm-sàk hì. \\
     that then-\textsc{erg} \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} food five and \textsc{3sg} fish loaf two-\textsc{pl} take \textsc{3sg} sky-on way look-up-\textsc{inst} god on-\textsc{loc} rejoice-\textsc{nmlz} \textsc{3sg} long \textsc{decl} \textsc{3sg} bread-show-\textsc{pl} tear \textsc{3sg} person-\textsc{pl} on-\textsc{loc} \textsc{3sg} give.to \textsc{irr}-\textsc{erg} life-follow-\textsc{pl} \textsc{3sg} give \textsc{decl} that \textsc{emph} like-\textsc{erg} fish loaf two-\textsc{pl} also \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{pro} all \textsc{3sg} join-\textsc{caus} \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And when he had taken the five loaves and the two fishes, he looked up to heaven, and blessed, and brake the loaves, and gave them to his disciples to set before them; and the two fishes divided he among them all.}}

\exi{42}
\gll Àmaute khèmpeuh ìn né-ìn à khàm ùh hì. \\
     \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{pro} all \textsc{erg} eat-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} gold 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And they did all eat, and were filled.}}

\exi{43}
\gll Túa cìang-ìn nùng-zúi-tè ìn à kī-khàm-val anlum lè ngasa khàwm ùh à, pái-pel sàwm lè nìh à dim hì. \\
     that then-\textsc{erg} life-follow-\textsc{pl} \textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} \textsc{refl}-gather-basket food and fish gather 2/3PL \textsc{3sg} go-vessel ten and two \textsc{3sg} full \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And they took up twelve baskets full of the fragments, and of the fishes.}}

\exi{44}
\gll Túa àn à né mì sùng pàn-ìn pasal cíng-tèng tulnga à phà hì. \\
     that \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{poss} \textsc{3sg} eat person inside \textsc{abl}-\textsc{erg} husband complete-all five.thousand \textsc{3sg} branch \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And they that did eat of the loaves were about five thousand men.}}

\exi{45}
\gll Túa khìt phèt-ìn Jesuh ìn à nùng-zúi-tè gunkuang-àh tuang-sàk-ìn, à galkhat à ōm Bethsaida khùa-àh mà-pái-sàk à, àmàh ìn mihon-tè à khùa ciatah à ciah dìng-ìn à sawl hì. \\
     that \textsc{seq} twin-\textsc{erg} \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} life-follow-\textsc{pl} ship-\textsc{loc} feed-\textsc{caus}-\textsc{inst} \textsc{3sg} battle \textsc{3sg} exist Bethsaida town-\textsc{loc} \textsc{emph}-go-\textsc{caus} \textsc{3sg} \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{erg} poor.person-\textsc{pl} \textsc{3sg} town each \textsc{3sg} return \textsc{irr}-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} send \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And straightway he constrained his disciples to get into the ship, and to go to the other side before unto Bethsaida, while he sent away the people.}}

\exi{46}

     \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{com} \textsc{3sg} \textsc{refl}-divide \textsc{seq} then-\textsc{erg} word-prayer \textsc{irr}-\textsc{erg} mountain-top-\textsc{loc} \textsc{3sg} climb-up \textsc{decl} \\

\exi{47}
\gll Khuamial cìang-ìn tùi lai-zang dòng gunkuang túng-tà à, Jesuh ahihleh leitung-àh àmàh guak-ìn om-lai hì. \\
     darkness then-\textsc{erg} water middle-side until ship arrive-\textsc{pfv} \textsc{3sg} \textsc{jesuh} if earth-\textsc{loc} \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{pro} alone-\textsc{erg} rest-still \textsc{decl} \\

\exi{48}
\gll Huih ìn à nùng-zúi-tè lèh-mut àhìh màn-ìn gunkuang hot zò lò-ìn hàk-sá à sàk-ná thù ùh Jesuh ìn à théi hì. Túa hì à, zing-sàng lām nái thùm pàn nái gùk kī-kal khawng-ìn à nùng-zúi-tè kìang lām-àh tùi-tùng tàwn-ìn Jesuh à pái hì. Àmaute à kheng-sùak dìng bàng-ìn pái à, \\
     wind \textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} life-follow-\textsc{pl} turn-contrary be.\textsc{3sg}.\textsc{rel} reason-\textsc{erg} ship steer south \textsc{neg}-\textsc{erg} \textsc{intens}-\textsc{past} \textsc{3sg} cause-\textsc{nmlz} word 2/3PL \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} know \textsc{decl} that \textsc{decl} \textsc{3sg} morning-high way near three \textsc{abl} near six \textsc{refl}-middle about-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} life-follow-\textsc{pl} beside way-\textsc{loc} water-upon loaf-\textsc{erg} \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{3sg} go \textsc{decl} \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{3sg} row-emerge \textsc{irr} like-\textsc{erg} go \textsc{3sg} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And he saw them toiling in rowing; for the wind was contrary unto them: and about the fourth watch of the night he cometh unto them, walking upon the sea, and would have passed by them.}}

\exi{49}
\gll àhì zòng-ìn à nùng-zúi-tè ìn tùi-tùng à mì pái à mùh cìang-ùn, sikha hì cí-ìn ngaihsun ùh àhìh màn-ìn à áwng-kék gàwp ùh hì. \\
     be.\textsc{3sg} although-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} life-follow-\textsc{pl} \textsc{erg} water-upon \textsc{3sg} person go \textsc{3sg} see then-\textsc{pl}.\textsc{imp} wizard \textsc{decl} say-\textsc{quot} think 2/3PL be.\textsc{3sg}.\textsc{rel} reason-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} roar-\textsc{intens} all 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{But when they saw him walking upon the sea, they supposed it had been a spirit, and cried out:}}

\exi{50}
\gll Bàng hàng hìam cìh lèh àmàh à mùh ùh cìang-ìn lau màhmàh ùh hì. Àhìh hàng-ìn Jesuh ìn thàk-hàt-ìn àmaute ho-pìh-pàh à, lùng-nuam-ìn ōm ùn. Kèimah kà hì hì; lau kèi ùn à cí hì. \\
     like reason \textsc{q} say.\textsc{nom} and \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{3sg} see 2/3PL then-\textsc{erg} fear very 2/3PL \textsc{decl} be.\textsc{3sg}.\textsc{rel} because-\textsc{erg} \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{erg} new-strong-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{pro} greet-\textsc{appl}-\textsc{neg}.\textsc{abil} \textsc{3sg} heart-pleasant-\textsc{erg} exist \textsc{imp}.\textsc{pl} \textsc{1sg}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{1sg} \textsc{decl} \textsc{decl} fear \textsc{neg}.\textsc{emph} \textsc{imp}.\textsc{pl} \textsc{3sg} say \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{for they all saw him, and were troubled. And immediately he talked with them, and saith unto them, Be of good cheer: it is I; be not afraid.}}

\exi{51}
\gll Túa cìang-ìn àmaute ōm-ná gunkuang tùngàh Jesuh kàh-tò à, huih-pì zòng à dai-pah hì. Nùng-zúi-tè ìn lam-dàng à sá màhmàh ùh hì. \\
     that then-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{pro} exist-\textsc{nmlz} ship on-\textsc{loc} \textsc{jesuh} climb-up \textsc{3sg} wind-great also \textsc{3sg} still-unable \textsc{decl} life-follow-\textsc{pl} \textsc{erg} other.way \textsc{3sg} flesh very 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And he went up unto them into the ship; and the wind ceased: and they were sore amazed in themselves beyond measure, and wondered.}}

\exi{52}
\gll Bàng hàng hìam cìh lèh lùng-sìm nà-vák lò ùh àhìh màn-ìn anlum tàwh kī-sāi thù-piang tèl théi lò ùh hì. \\
     like reason \textsc{q} say.\textsc{nom} and stone-mind \textsc{2sg}-walk \textsc{neg} 2/3PL be.\textsc{3sg}.\textsc{rel} reason-\textsc{erg} food \textsc{com} \textsc{refl}-concern word-born know know \textsc{neg} 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{For they considered not the miracle of the loaves: for their heart was hardened.}}

\exi{53}
\gll Tùi à kantan khìt ùh cìang-ìn Gennesaret gàm tùng ùh à, tùi-gei-àh à gunkuang ùh à khih ùh hì. \\
     water \textsc{3sg} cross.over \textsc{seq} 2/3PL then-\textsc{erg} \textsc{gennesaret} land on 2/3PL \textsc{3sg} water-edge-\textsc{loc} \textsc{3sg} ship 2/3PL \textsc{3sg} bind 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And when they had passed over, they came into the land of Gennesaret, and drew to the shore.}}

\exi{54}
\gll Gunkuang pàn-ìn à pai-khìat khìt phetun mì-tè ìn Jesuh à-hìh-lām à théi-pah ùh hì. \\
     ship \textsc{abl}-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} go.out \textsc{seq} hear person-\textsc{pl} \textsc{erg} \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{3sg}-be-way \textsc{3sg} know-perceive 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\

\exi{55}
\gll Túa gàm sùng tèng-àh mì-tè tái kawi-kawi ùh à, Jesuh ōm hì, cí-ìn à kī-gēn-ná mùn peuhpeuh-àh cí-ná-tè à lupna pheek ùh tàwh hòng pua ùh hì. \\
     that land inside dwell-\textsc{loc} person-\textsc{pl} check crooked\textasciitilde{}REDUP 2/3PL \textsc{3sg} \textsc{jesuh} exist \textsc{decl} say-\textsc{quot} \textsc{3sg} \textsc{refl}-explain-\textsc{nmlz} place whatsoever-\textsc{loc} say-\textsc{nmlz}-\textsc{pl} \textsc{3sg} bed bed 2/3PL \textsc{com} \textsc{3→1} carry.on.back 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{and ran through that whole region round about, and began to carry about in beds those that were sick, where they heard he was.}}

\exi{56}
\gll Khùa-pì, khùa-néu, lè khùa-keh-tè à à pái-ná khèmpeuh-àh, mì-tè ìn mihon kī-khòp-ná mùn-àh cí-ná-tè hòng pua ùh à, à pùan-mong-teep beek à lawn-sàk nàdìng dèih-ìn Jesuh kìang-àh à thùm ùh hì. À pùan-mong-teep à lawngkha mì khèmpeuh cí-dām pah-pah ùh hì. \\
     village-big town-small and town-cross-\textsc{pl} \textsc{3sg} \textsc{3sg} go-\textsc{nmlz} all-\textsc{loc} person-\textsc{pl} \textsc{erg} poor.person \textsc{refl}-gather-\textsc{nmlz} place-\textsc{loc} say-\textsc{nmlz}-\textsc{pl} \textsc{3→1} carry.on.back 2/3PL \textsc{3sg} \textsc{3sg} cloth-cover-fringe only \textsc{3sg} cast-\textsc{caus} \textsc{purp} want-\textsc{cvb} \textsc{jesuh} beside-\textsc{loc} \textsc{3sg} three 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \textsc{3sg} cloth-cover-fringe \textsc{3sg} touch person all say-well immediately\textasciitilde{}REDUP 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And whithersoever he entered, into villages, or cities, or country, they laid the sick in the streets, and besought him that they might touch if it were but the border of his garment: and as many as touched him were made whole.}}

\end{exe}

\section*{Chapter 7}
\addcontentsline{toc}{section}{Chapter 7}

\begin{exe}
\exi{1}
\gll Túa lái-tàk-ìn Jerusalem pàn-ìn à hòng pái Farisi mì-tè lè Thù-khàm hìlh sía-tè, Jesuh kìang-àh hòng kī-khàwm ùh hì. \\
     that midst-exact-\textsc{erg} \textsc{jerusalem} \textsc{abl}-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} \textsc{3→1} go \textsc{farisi} person-\textsc{pl} and law tell evil-\textsc{pl} \textsc{jesuh} beside-\textsc{loc} \textsc{3→1} \textsc{refl}-gather 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{Then came together unto him the Pharisees, and certain of the scribes, which came from Jerusalem.}}

\exi{2}
\gll À nùng-zúi-tè pàwl-khàt ìn khang-lūi ngèina zúi lò-ìn, khùt sil-lò-ìn àn à nèk-lam ùh à mú-khá ùh hì. \\
     \textsc{3sg} life-follow-\textsc{pl} some-one \textsc{erg} generation-old know-\textsc{nmlz} follow \textsc{neg}-\textsc{erg} hand wash-\textsc{neg}-\textsc{inst} \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{poss} \textsc{3sg} eat-direction 2/3PL \textsc{3sg} see.\textsc{i}-place 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And when they saw some of his disciples eat bread with defiled, that is to say, with unwashen, hands, they found fault.}}

\exi{3}
\gll farisi mì-tè lè Jew mì-tè khèmpeuh ìn khang-lūi ngèina zúi-ìn khùt sil-lò-ìn àn né lò ùh hì. \\
     \textsc{farisi} person-\textsc{pl} and \textsc{jew} person-\textsc{pl} all \textsc{erg} generation-old know-\textsc{nmlz} follow-\textsc{erg} hand wash-\textsc{neg}-\textsc{inst} \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{poss} eat \textsc{neg} 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{For the Pharisees, and all the Jews, except they wash their hands oft, eat not, holding the tradition of the elders.}}

\exi{4}
\gll Nèk-thèih zūak-ná pàn-ìn à kī-léi nà-tè zòng àmau teek màh ìn à sawp kèi uhleh né lò ùh hì. Khang-lūi ngèina à zùih ùh, hāi khawng, beel khawng, sum-ngo kī-bāwl beellekuang khawng-tè sawp dìng cìh ngèina à zùih ùh tampi ōm hì \\
     eat.\textsc{ii}-\textsc{abil} sell-\textsc{nmlz} \textsc{abl}-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} \textsc{refl}-buy \textsc{2sg}-\textsc{pl} also \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{pro} master \textsc{emph} \textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} wrap \textsc{neg}.\textsc{emph} 2/3PL.if eat \textsc{neg} 2/3PL \textsc{decl} generation-old know-\textsc{nmlz} \textsc{3sg} follow-\textsc{nom} 2/3PL cup about pan about brass-iron \textsc{refl}-make dish cup-\textsc{pl} wrap \textsc{irr} say.\textsc{nom} know-\textsc{nmlz} \textsc{3sg} follow-\textsc{nom} 2/3PL many exist \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And when they come from the market, except they wash, they eat not. And many other things there be, which they have received to hold, as the washing of cups, and pots, brasen vessels, and of tables.}}

\exi{5}
\gll Túa àhìh màn-ìn Farisi mì-tè lè Thù-khàm hìlh sía-tè ìn Jesuh kìang-àh, bàng hàng-ìn nà nùng-zúi-tè ìn, khang-lūi lai-pèk pàn-ìn tuni dòng-ìn à kī-zúi pulepa ngèina-tè zúi lò-ìn, khùt sil-lò-ìn àn né àhì ùh hìam cí-ìn à dòng ùh hì. \\
     that be.\textsc{3sg}.\textsc{rel} reason-\textsc{erg} \textsc{farisi} person-\textsc{pl} and law tell evil-\textsc{pl} \textsc{erg} \textsc{jesuh} beside-\textsc{loc} like because-\textsc{erg} \textsc{2sg} life-follow-\textsc{pl} \textsc{erg} generation-old writing-wash \textsc{abl}-\textsc{erg} today collect-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} \textsc{refl}-follow ancestor knowledge-\textsc{pl} follow \textsc{neg}-\textsc{erg} hand wash-\textsc{neg}-\textsc{inst} \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{poss} eat be.\textsc{3sg} 2/3PL \textsc{q} say-\textsc{quot} \textsc{3sg} until 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{Then the Pharisees and scribes asked him, Why walk not thy disciples according to the tradition of the elders, but eat bread with unwashen hands?}}

\exi{6}
\gll Jesuh ìn àmaute dawng à, à tùng-thama à hòih-ìn à kilang-khem nòtè' thù, Isaiah ìn à gēn-kholh-na mán màhmàh hì. Àmà gēn-ná-àh, pasian ìn híh bàng-ìn gēn hì: Híh mì-tè ìn à kam-pì bèk ùh tàwh kèi hòng zahtak-bāwl ùh à, à lùng-sìm tak-tak ùh kèi tàwh ki-gamla hì. \\
     \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{erg} \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{pro} receive \textsc{3sg} \textsc{3sg} rebuke-after \textsc{3sg} be.good-\textsc{cvb} \textsc{3sg} height-restrain \textsc{2pl}.\textsc{pro} word \textsc{isaiah} \textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} prophecy finish very \textsc{decl} \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{poss} speak-\textsc{nmlz}-\textsc{loc} god \textsc{erg} this like-\textsc{erg} speak \textsc{decl} this person-\textsc{pl} \textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} word-big only 2/3PL \textsc{com} \textsc{neg}.\textsc{emph} \textsc{3→1} honor-do 2/3PL \textsc{3sg} \textsc{3sg} stone-mind great\textasciitilde{}REDUP 2/3PL \textsc{neg}.\textsc{emph} \textsc{com} territory \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{He answered and said unto them, Well hath Esaias prophesied of you hypocrites, as it is written, This people honoureth me with their lips, But their heart is far from me.}}

\exi{7}
\gll Mì-hìng-tè' bāwl-tàwm thù-khàm-te, Pasian' thù-khàm zah-ìn mì-tè tùngàh hìlh ùh àhìh màn-ìn, kèi hòng bìak hangun à kī-manna ōm lò hì' cí hì. \\
     person-kind-\textsc{pl} make-break law-\textsc{pl} god law fear-\textsc{cvb} person-\textsc{pl} on-\textsc{loc} tell 2/3PL be.\textsc{3sg}.\textsc{rel} reason-\textsc{erg} \textsc{neg}.\textsc{emph} \textsc{3→1} worship \textsc{hangun} \textsc{3sg} \textsc{refl}-manna exist \textsc{neg} \textsc{decl} say \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{Howbeit in vain do they worship me, Teaching for doctrines the commandments of men.}}

\exi{8}
\gll Nòtè ìn Pasian' thù-khàm nawlkhin-ìn, mì-hìng-tè' thù-hìlh-ná nà zúi zawsop ùh hì à cí hì. \\
     \textsc{2pl}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{erg} god law ways-\textsc{cvb} person-kind-\textsc{pl} word-teach-\textsc{nmlz} \textsc{2sg} follow judge 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \textsc{3sg} say \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{For laying aside the commandment of God, ye hold the tradition of men, as the washing of pots and cups: and many other such like things ye do.}}

\exi{9}
\gll Túa cìang-ìn Jesuh ìn à thù-gēn zomlai à, nà khang-lūi ngèina ùh nà zùih-thèih nà-dìng-ùn Pasian' thù-khàm-te à nawlkhin-zia nà sìam màhmàh ùh hì. \\
     that then-\textsc{erg} \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} speech journey \textsc{3sg} \textsc{2sg} generation-old know-\textsc{nmlz} 2/3PL \textsc{2sg} follow-\textsc{abil} \textsc{2sg}-\textsc{irr}-\textsc{imp} god law-\textsc{pl} \textsc{3sg} ways-manner \textsc{2sg} skill very 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And he said unto them, Full well ye reject the commandment of God, that ye may keep your own tradition.}}

\exi{10}
\gll Moses ìn, nà nù lè nà pà zah-tàk ùn. À nù à pà à sam-sía-tè kī-thàt hèn' cí hì. \\
     \textsc{moses} \textsc{erg} \textsc{2sg} female and \textsc{2sg} father fear-true \textsc{imp}.\textsc{pl} \textsc{3sg} female \textsc{3sg} father \textsc{3sg} bless-curse-\textsc{pl} \textsc{refl}-kill \textsc{juss} say \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{For Moses said, Honour thy father and thy mother; and, Whoso curseth father or mother, let him die the death:}}

\exi{11}
\gll Àhì zòng-ìn nòtè ìn, mì khàt-pèuh ìn à nù à pà à pìak-thèih dìng nà khàt peuhpeuh à nèih hàng-ìn, híh pèn korban pasian à' dìng hì, cí pèuh lèh, \\
     be.\textsc{3sg} although-\textsc{erg} \textsc{2pl}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{erg} person one-every \textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} female \textsc{3sg} father \textsc{3sg} give.to-\textsc{abil} \textsc{irr} \textsc{2sg} one every \textsc{3sg} have-\textsc{nom} because-\textsc{erg} this \textsc{top} \textsc{korban} god \textsc{3sg} \textsc{irr} \textsc{decl} say every and \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{but ye say, If a man shall say to his father or mother, It is Corban, that is to say, a gift, by whatsoever thou mightest be profited by me; he shall be free .}}

\exi{12}
\gll à nù lè à pà à huh nàdìng pàn-ìn sùak-tà théi hì' cí-ìn thù nà hìlh ùh hì. \\
     \textsc{3sg} female and \textsc{3sg} father \textsc{3sg} help \textsc{purp} \textsc{abl}-\textsc{erg} become-\textsc{pfv} know \textsc{decl} say-\textsc{quot} word \textsc{2sg} tell 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And ye suffer him no more to do ought for his father or his mother;}}

\exi{13}
\gll Híh bàng dán-ìn mì-tè thù nà hìlh-ná ùh tàwh Pasian' thù nà pam-paih ùh hì. Híh bàng-zia-ìn nà gamtat-ná ùh à-dàng tampi zòng om-lai hì à cí hì. \\
     this like manner-\textsc{erg} person-\textsc{pl} word \textsc{2sg} teach-\textsc{nmlz} 2/3PL \textsc{com} god word \textsc{2sg} restore-heal 2/3PL \textsc{decl} this what-like-\textsc{inst} \textsc{2sg} rule.land-\textsc{nmlz} 2/3PL \textsc{3sg}-other many also rest-still \textsc{decl} \textsc{3sg} say \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{making the word of God of none effect through your tradition, which ye have delivered: and many such like things do ye.}}

\exi{14}
\gll Túa cìang-ìn Jesuh ìn mihonpi-tè sàm-ìn àmaute kìang-àh, mì khèmpeuh àw, kà thù-gēn hòng ngái ùn-lá, kà thù-gēn-tè théi-tèl ùn. \\
     that then-\textsc{erg} \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{erg} noble-\textsc{pl} call-\textsc{cvb} \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{pro} beside-\textsc{loc} person all voice \textsc{1sg} speech \textsc{3→1} listen.\textsc{i} \textsc{pl}.\textsc{imp}-and \textsc{1sg} word-tell-\textsc{pl} know.\textsc{i}-exact \textsc{imp}.\textsc{pl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And when he had called all the people unto him , he said unto them, Hearken unto me every one of you , and understand:}}

\exi{15}
\gll À pualam pàn-ìn mì-tè sùng-àh túm-ìn mì à nin-sàk-thèi bangmah ōm lò hì. Àhì zòng-ìn mì-tè sùng pàn-ìn à pusuak khìa-tè ìn mì nin-sàk-thèi hì. \\
     \textsc{3sg} outside \textsc{abl}-\textsc{erg} person-\textsc{pl} inside-\textsc{loc} all-\textsc{erg} person \textsc{3sg} defile-\textsc{caus}-\textsc{abil} nothing exist \textsc{neg} \textsc{decl} be.\textsc{3sg} although-\textsc{erg} person-\textsc{pl} inside \textsc{abl}-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} mouth exit-\textsc{pl} \textsc{erg} person defile-\textsc{caus}-\textsc{abil} \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{there is nothing from without a man, that entering into him can defile him: but the things which come out of him, those are they that defile the man.}}

\exi{16}

     noble-\textsc{pl} abandon-\textsc{erg} house inside-\textsc{loc} \textsc{3sg} enter \textsc{seq} then-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} life-follow-\textsc{pl} \textsc{erg} this preach-measure-\textsc{nmlz} word \textsc{3sg} until 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\

     \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{erg} \textsc{2pl}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{erg} also nothing \textsc{3sg} know \textsc{neg} be-perhaps \textsc{decl} \textsc{neg} \textsc{2sg} \textsc{decl} 2/3PL \textsc{q} \textsc{3sg} outside \textsc{abl}-\textsc{erg} person-\textsc{pl} inside-\textsc{loc} \textsc{3sg} all \textsc{2sg}-\textsc{pl} \textsc{erg} person strengthen know \textsc{neg} \textsc{decl} \\

\newpage

\section*{Chapter 8}
\addcontentsline{toc}{section}{Chapter 8}

\begin{exe}
\exi{1}
\gll Túa khìt à sawt lò-ìn Jesuh kìang-àh mihon tampi tak hòng kī-khàwm leuleu ùh à, àmaute ìn àn-nèk dìng néi nàwn lò ùh àhìh màn-ìn Jesuh ìn à nùng-zúi-tè sàm-ìn àmaute kìang-àh, \\
     that \textsc{seq} \textsc{3sg} long.time \textsc{neg}-\textsc{erg} \textsc{jesuh} beside-\textsc{loc} poor.person many truly \textsc{3→1} \textsc{refl}-gather again 2/3PL \textsc{3sg} \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{erg} \textsc{3pl}-eat.\textsc{ii} \textsc{irr} have \textsc{cont} \textsc{neg} 2/3PL be.\textsc{3sg}.\textsc{rel} reason-\textsc{erg} \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} life-follow-\textsc{pl} call-\textsc{cvb} \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{pro} beside-\textsc{loc} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{In those days the multitude being very great, and having nothing to eat, Jesus called his disciples unto him , and saith unto them,}}

\exi{2}
\gll híh mì-tè, kèi kìang-àh nì thùm bàng hòng ōm-khín ùh à, tù-ìn nèk dìng néi nàwn lò ùh àhìh màn-ìn hehpih-huai kà sá hì. \\
     this person-\textsc{pl} \textsc{neg}.\textsc{emph} beside-\textsc{loc} day three like \textsc{3→1} exist-\textsc{imm} 2/3PL \textsc{3sg} now-\textsc{erg} eat.\textsc{ii} \textsc{irr} have \textsc{cont} \textsc{neg} 2/3PL be.\textsc{3sg}.\textsc{rel} reason-\textsc{erg} angry-dread \textsc{1sg} flesh \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{I have compassion on the multitude, because they have now been with me three days, and have nothing to eat:}}

\exi{3}
\gll Àmaute pàwl-khàt gàm-lá-pì pàn-ìn à hòng pái ùh àhìh màn-ìn gil-kial-ìn ciah-sàk leng, lam-kal-àh cimawh khá dìng ùh hì à cí hì. \\
     \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{pro} some-one land-take-big \textsc{abl}-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} \textsc{3→1} go 2/3PL be.\textsc{3sg}.\textsc{rel} reason-\textsc{erg} bowels-\textsc{erg} return-\textsc{caus} line midway oppress \textsc{neg}.\textsc{perf} \textsc{irr} 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \textsc{3sg} say \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{and if I send them away fasting to their own houses, they will faint by the way: for divers of them came from far.}}

\exi{4}
\gll À nùng-zúi-tè ìn, híh mì-tè pìak dìng, híh gàm-lak-àh àn bangci ngàh dìng ì-hí hìam à cìh ùh cìang-ìn \\
     \textsc{3sg} life-follow-\textsc{pl} \textsc{erg} this person-\textsc{pl} give.to \textsc{irr} this land-midst-\textsc{loc} \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{poss} how get \textsc{irr} \textsc{1pl}.\textsc{incl}-be \textsc{q} \textsc{3sg} say.\textsc{nom} 2/3PL then-\textsc{erg} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And his disciples answered him, From whence can a man satisfy these men with bread here in the wilderness?}}

\exi{5}
\gll Jesuh ìn, anlum bàng-zah néi nà hì ùh hìam cí-ìn à dot lèh, sagih néi ung cí-ìn à dawng ùh hì. \\
     \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{erg} food what-quantity have \textsc{2sg} \textsc{decl} 2/3PL \textsc{q} say-\textsc{quot} \textsc{3sg} ask and seven have \textsc{pl}.\textsc{fut} say-\textsc{quot} \textsc{3sg} receive 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And he asked them, How many loaves have ye? And they said, Seven.}}

\exi{6}
\gll Túa cìang-ìn Jesuh ìn leilak-àh mihon-tè tù-sàk à, à anlum sagih lá-ìn Pasian tùngàh lungdam-ná à kohkhit cìang-ìn balnen-ìn, mihonpi-tè à lūi dìng-ìn à nùng-zúi-tè tùngàh à pía hì. À nùng-zúi-tè ìn zòng mihon-tè à lūi ùh hì. \\
     that then-\textsc{erg} \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{erg} ground-\textsc{loc} poor.person-\textsc{pl} act-\textsc{caus} \textsc{3sg} \textsc{3sg} food seven take-\textsc{erg} god on-\textsc{loc} rejoice-\textsc{nmlz} \textsc{3sg} thank then-\textsc{erg} tear-\textsc{erg} noble-\textsc{pl} \textsc{3sg} river \textsc{irr}-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} life-follow-\textsc{pl} on-\textsc{loc} \textsc{3sg} give \textsc{decl} \textsc{3sg} life-follow-\textsc{pl} \textsc{erg} also poor.person-\textsc{pl} \textsc{3sg} river 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And he commanded the people to sit down on the ground: and he took the seven loaves, and gave thanks, and brake, and gave to his disciples to set before them ; and they did set them before the people.}}

\exi{7}
\gll Ngasa néu tàwm-khàt zòng néi ùh àhìh màn-ìn Pasian tùngàh lungdam-ná à kohkhit cìang-ìn híh-tè zòng mì-pì-tè mái-àh à lūi nà-dìng-ùn à nùng-zúi-tè à sawl hì. \\

\exi{36}
\gll Mì khàt-pèuh ìn híh léi-tùng khèmpeuh à ngàh hàng-ìn à nuntak-ná bùl-pì suplawh lèh bàng phàt-tuam-ná ōm àhì hìam? \\
     person one-every \textsc{erg} this land-on all \textsc{3sg} get because-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} live-\textsc{nmlz} nave-\textsc{comp} lose and like praise-promise-\textsc{nmlz} exist be.\textsc{3sg} \textsc{q} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{For what shall it profit a man, if he shall gain the whole world, and lose his own soul?}}

\exi{37}
\gll Àmà nuntak-ná bàng tàwh léi-kík théi nàwn dìng àhì hìam? \\
     \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{poss} live-\textsc{nmlz} like \textsc{com} earth-\textsc{iter} know \textsc{cont} \textsc{irr} be.\textsc{3sg} \textsc{q} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{Or what shall a man give in exchange for his soul?}}

\exi{38}
\gll Pasian théi lò-ìn à gilo híh mì-tè lāk-àh kèima hàng lè kà thù-hìlh-tè hàng-ìn mái-zum-ìn kèi hòng pulak ngam lò mì peuhmah, à Pà' mīn-than-ná vang lè à sìangtho vàn-tùng mì-tè tàwh à mīn-thang-ìn hòng pái-kík cìang-ìn Mì-hìng Tá-pà zòng àmà hàng-ìn mái-zum-ìn pulak ngam lò dìng hì à cí hì. \\
     god know \textsc{neg}-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} enemy this person-\textsc{pl} among-\textsc{loc} \textsc{1sg}.self reason and \textsc{1sg} word-teach-\textsc{pl} because-\textsc{erg} face-bow-\textsc{erg} \textsc{neg}.\textsc{emph} \textsc{3→1} declare dare \textsc{neg} person whosoever \textsc{3sg} father name-bless-\textsc{nmlz} because and \textsc{3sg} holy sky-on person-\textsc{pl} \textsc{com} \textsc{3sg} name-famous-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3→1} go-\textsc{iter} then-\textsc{erg} person-kind child-male also \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{poss} because-\textsc{erg} face-bow-\textsc{erg} declare dare \textsc{neg} \textsc{irr} \textsc{decl} \textsc{3sg} say \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{Whosoever therefore shall be ashamed of me and of my words in this adulterous and sinful generation; of him also shall the Son of man be ashamed, when he cometh in the glory of his Father with the holy angels.}}

\end{exe}
\newpage

\section*{Chapter 9}
\addcontentsline{toc}{section}{Chapter 9}

\begin{exe}
\exi{1}
\gll Túa cìang-ìn Jesuh ìn à thù-gēn zomlai à, híh lái-à à ōm mì pàwl-khàt-tè à sìh mà-ìn vanglian-pì tàwh Pasian' Ukna hòng tùng tak-tak dìng à-híh-ná thù phawk ùn à cí hì. \\
     that then-\textsc{erg} \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} speech journey \textsc{3sg} this midst-\textsc{loc} \textsc{3sg} exist person some-one-\textsc{pl} \textsc{3sg} die self-\textsc{erg} mighty-\textsc{comp} \textsc{com} god rule.\textsc{nmlz} \textsc{3→1} on great\textasciitilde{}REDUP \textsc{irr} \textsc{3sg}-be.\textsc{nom}-\textsc{nmlz} word remember \textsc{imp}.\textsc{pl} \textsc{3sg} say \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And he said unto them, Verily I say unto you, That there be some of them that stand here, which shall not taste of death, till they have seen the kingdom of God come with power.}}

\exi{2}
\gll Túa zàwh nì gùk khìt cìang-ìn Jesuh ìn Peter, James, lè Johan-tè sàm-ìn àmau-tèng guak mual-tùng khàt-àh à paipih-tò hì. Àmaute' mùh-tangpi màh-ìn Jesuh à mel hòng kī-kheel à, \\
     that able day six \textsc{seq} then-\textsc{erg} \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{erg} \textsc{peter} \textsc{james} and \textsc{johan}-\textsc{pl} call-\textsc{cvb} \textsc{3pl}-all back mountain-top one-\textsc{loc} \textsc{3sg} accompany-sit \textsc{decl} \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{pro} see.\textsc{ii}-before likewise-\textsc{erg} \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{3sg} void \textsc{3→1} \textsc{refl}-repent \textsc{3sg} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And after six days Jesus taketh with him Peter, and James, and John, and leadeth them up into an high mountain apart by themselves: and he was transfigured before them.}}

\exi{3}
\gll léi-tùng à pùan-sawp-tè kuamah ìn à paak-sàk zàwh lòh dòng dìng zah-ìn à pùan-tè pa-kin à tee hì. \\
     land-on \textsc{3sg} cloth-white-\textsc{pl} nobody \textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} white-\textsc{caus} able \textsc{neg}-\textsc{nom} until \textsc{irr} fear-\textsc{cvb} \textsc{3sg} cloth-\textsc{pl} completely-destroy \textsc{3sg} glitter \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And his raiment became shining, exceeding white as snow; so as no fuller on earth can white them.}}

\exi{4}
\gll Túa lái-àh Elijah lè Moses hòng ōm-ìn, Jesuh tàwh à ki-ho à mú ùh hì. \\
     that midst-\textsc{loc} \textsc{elijah} and \textsc{moses} \textsc{3→1} exist-\textsc{cvb} \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{com} \textsc{3sg} call \textsc{3sg} see.\textsc{i} 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And there appeared unto them Elias with Moses: and they were talking with Jesus.}}

\exi{5}
\gll Peter zòng hòng pau-ìn Jesuh kìang-àh, sía àw, híh lái-à ì ōm, núam màhmàh hì. Nàng à' dìng buk khàt, Moses à' dìng buk khàt, Elijah à' dìng buk khàt kòng lām-sàk dìng ùh hì à cí hì. \\
     \textsc{peter} also \textsc{3→1} \textsc{pau}-\textsc{erg} \textsc{jesuh} beside-\textsc{loc} evil voice this midst-\textsc{loc} \textsc{1pl}.\textsc{incl} exist want very \textsc{decl} \textsc{2sg}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{3sg} \textsc{irr} ambush one \textsc{moses} \textsc{3sg} \textsc{irr} ambush one \textsc{elijah} \textsc{3sg} \textsc{irr} ambush one \textsc{1sg→3} way-\textsc{caus} \textsc{irr} 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \textsc{3sg} say \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And Peter answered and said to Jesus, Master, it is good for us to be here: and let us make three tabernacles; one for thee, and one for Moses, and one for Elias.}}

\exi{6}
\gll Àmàh lè à lawm-tè nak-lau màhmàh ùh àhìh màn-ìn à cìh dìng mel à thèih lòh mán àhì hì. \\
     \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{pro} and \textsc{3sg} friend-\textsc{pl} nose-fear very 2/3PL be.\textsc{3sg}.\textsc{rel} reason-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} say.\textsc{nom} \textsc{irr} void \textsc{3sg} know.\textsc{ii} \textsc{neg}-\textsc{nom} finish be.\textsc{3sg} \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{For he wist not what to say; for they were sore afraid.}}

\exi{7}
\gll Meii hòng kai-ìn à liim ìn àmaute hòng liah à, túa meii sùng pàn-ìn àw khàt hòng gin-gin, híh pà, kà ít kà Tá-pà àhì hì; àmà thù nà ngái ùn à hòng cí hì. \\
     cloud \textsc{3→1} pull-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} wing \textsc{erg} \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{3→1} circuit \textsc{3sg} that cloud inside \textsc{abl}-\textsc{erg} voice one \textsc{3→1} hear\textasciitilde{}REDUP this father \textsc{1sg} love \textsc{1sg} child-male be.\textsc{3sg} \textsc{decl} \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{poss} word \textsc{2sg} listen.\textsc{i} \textsc{imp}.\textsc{pl} \textsc{3sg} \textsc{3→1} say \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And there was a cloud that overshadowed them: and a voice came out of the cloud, saying, This is my beloved Son: hear him.}}

\exi{8}

     \textsc{3sg} around \textsc{3sg} fold \textsc{3sg} town-near 2/3PL.if \textsc{jesuh} count-unable nobody other \textsc{2sg} exist \textsc{cont} \textsc{neg} \textsc{decl} \\

\exi{9}
\gll Mual-tùng pàn-ìn à pái-sùk kà-om-ùn Jesuh ìn àmaute kìang-àh, sìh-ná pàn-ìn Mì-hìng Tá-pà à thawh-kík matengin híh nà mùh-tè ùh kuama kìang-àh gēn kèi ùn cí-ìn à khàm hì. \\
     mountain-top \textsc{abl}-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} go-\textsc{down} \textsc{1sg}-be-\textsc{pl}.\textsc{incl} \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{erg} \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{pro} beside-\textsc{loc} blood-\textsc{nmlz} \textsc{abl}-\textsc{erg} person-kind child-male \textsc{3sg} resurrection until this \textsc{2sg} see.\textsc{ii}-\textsc{pl} 2/3PL charge beside-\textsc{loc} speak \textsc{neg}.\textsc{emph} \textsc{imp}.\textsc{pl} say-\textsc{quot} \textsc{3sg} gold \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And as they came down from the mountain, he charged them that they should tell no man what things they had seen, till the Son of man were risen from the dead.}}

\exi{10}
\gll Àmà cìh màh bàng-ìn im ùh à, àhì zòng-ìn, sìh-ná pàn-ìn tho-kík à cìh bàng à cìh-nòp-ná hì dìng àhì hìam, cí-ìn à lùng-sìm sùng uhah à ngaihsun ùh hì. \\

\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And they kept that saying with themselves, questioning one with another what the rising from the dead should mean.}}

\exi{11}
\gll Túa cìang-ìn Jesuh kìang-àh, bàng hàng-ìn Thù-khàm hìlh sía-tè ìn, Elijah hòng pái masa dìng, cí ùh àhì hìam cí-ìn à dòng ùh hì. \\
     that then-\textsc{erg} \textsc{jesuh} beside-\textsc{loc} like because-\textsc{erg} law tell evil-\textsc{pl} \textsc{erg} \textsc{elijah} \textsc{3→1} go first \textsc{irr} say 2/3PL be.\textsc{3sg} \textsc{q} say-\textsc{quot} \textsc{3sg} until 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And they asked him, saying, Why say the scribes that Elias must first come?}}

\exi{12}
\gll Jesuh ìn, nà khèmpeuh à bāwl-khol dìng-ìn Elijah hòng pái masa takpi hì. Mì-hìng Tá-pà ìn gìm-ná tampi thùak-ìn simmawh-ná ngàh dìng hì, cí-ìn Lái Sìangtho ìn gēn hì lò àhì hìam? \\
     \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{erg} \textsc{2sg} all \textsc{3sg} make-prepare \textsc{irr}-\textsc{erg} \textsc{elijah} \textsc{3→1} go first indeed \textsc{decl} person-kind child-male \textsc{erg} suffer-\textsc{nmlz} many suffer-\textsc{cvb} blaspheme-\textsc{nmlz} get \textsc{irr} \textsc{decl} say-\textsc{quot} midst holy \textsc{erg} speak \textsc{decl} \textsc{neg} be.\textsc{3sg} \textsc{q} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And he answered and told them, Elias verily cometh first, and restoreth all things; and how it is written of the Son of man, that he must suffer many things, and be set at nought.}}

\exi{13}
\gll Àhì zòng-ìn ke'n kòng cìh-ìn-àh, Elijah hòng pái-khín takpi à, Lái Sìangtho ìn àmà thù à gēn-sá màh bàng-ìn mì pàwl-khàt-tè ìn à u-tù-tun àmàh à bāwl ùh hì cí-ìn à dawng hì. \\
     be.\textsc{3sg} although-\textsc{erg} \textsc{1sg}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{1sg→3} say.\textsc{ii}-\textsc{erg}-\textsc{loc} \textsc{elijah} \textsc{3→1} go-\textsc{imm} indeed \textsc{3sg} midst holy \textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{poss} word \textsc{3sg} speak-\textsc{past} \textsc{emph} like-\textsc{erg} person some-one-\textsc{pl} \textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} want-\textsc{fut}-\textsc{dur} \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{3sg} make 2/3PL \textsc{decl} say-\textsc{quot} \textsc{3sg} receive \textsc{decl} \\

\exi{14}

     \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} life-follow other-\textsc{pl} beside-\textsc{loc} \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{com} like word strife \textsc{2sg} \textsc{decl} 2/3PL \textsc{q} say-\textsc{quot} \textsc{3sg} until \textsc{decl} \\

\exi{17}
\gll Mihon lāk pàn-ìn mì khàt ìn hòng dawng à, sía àw, kà tá-pà ìn dawi véi-ìn pau théi lò àhìh màn-ìn nàngmà kìang-àh kòng pái-pìh hì. \\
     poor.person among \textsc{abl}-\textsc{erg} person one \textsc{erg} \textsc{3→1} receive \textsc{3sg} evil voice \textsc{1sg} child-male \textsc{erg} fear sick-\textsc{erg} \textsc{pau} know \textsc{neg} be.\textsc{3sg}.\textsc{rel} reason-\textsc{erg} \textsc{2sg}.self beside-\textsc{loc} \textsc{1sg→3} go-\textsc{appl} \textsc{decl} \\

\exi{18}
\gll Dawi ìn àmàh à mat sìm-ìn léi-lak den-ná à, à cil-phuan bua-ìn à hà gawi-ìn kòng-kaw-cìp hì. Nà nùng-zúi-tè ìn dawi hòng hawl-khìat-sàk nàdìng kà ngen à, àhì zòng-ìn hawlkhia théi lò ùh hì à cí hì. \\

\exi{19}
\gll Jesuh ìn àmaute kìang-àh, up-ná néi lò mì-tè àw, nòtè bàng tanvei hòng ōm-pìh dìng à, bàng tanvei hòng kī-kholh-pìh dìng kà hì hìam? À nàu-pang hòng pái-pìh ùn à cí hì. \\

\gll Àmaute ìn zòng Jesuh kìang-àh à nàu-pang hòng pái-pìh ùh hì. Dawi ìn Jesuh à mùh phèt-ìn nàu-pang kòng-kaw-sàk àhìh màn-ìn leilak-àh pú-kin kī-khuk à, à cil-phuan à bua hì. \\
     \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{erg} also \textsc{jesuh} beside-\textsc{loc} \textsc{3sg} child-small \textsc{3→1} go-\textsc{appl} 2/3PL \textsc{decl} fear \textsc{erg} \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{3sg} see twin-\textsc{erg} child-small \textsc{1sg→3}-tear-\textsc{caus} be.\textsc{3sg}.\textsc{rel} reason-\textsc{erg} ground-\textsc{loc} grandfather-god \textsc{refl}-pool \textsc{3sg} \textsc{3sg} spittle-foam \textsc{3sg} pour \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And they brought him unto him: and when he saw him, straightway the spirit tare him; and he fell on the ground, and wallowed foaming.}}

\exi{21}
\gll Jesuh ìn, à nat zàwh bàng tanvei sawtta àhì hìam cí-ìn à pà kìang-àh à dòng hì. à néu-tùng à kī-pan àhì hì. \\
     \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} sick able like long great be.\textsc{3sg} \textsc{q} say-\textsc{quot} \textsc{3sg} father beside-\textsc{loc} \textsc{3sg} until \textsc{decl} \textsc{3sg} little-since \textsc{3sg} \textsc{refl}-begin be.\textsc{3sg} \textsc{decl} \\

     \textsc{3sg} die \textsc{purp}.\textsc{erg} furnace inside and water inside-\textsc{loc} many-time-great fall-able \textsc{decl} \textsc{2sg} do-\textsc{abil} and \textsc{1pl}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{3→1} grace and.then \textsc{3→1} help \textsc{erg} say-\textsc{quot} \textsc{3sg} receive \textsc{decl} \\

\exi{23}
\gll Jesuh ìn, bàng hàng-ìn nà híh-thèih lèh, cí nà hì hìam? À um-tè à dìng-ìn nà khèmpeuh hí-thèi hì lò àhì hìam à cí hì. \\
     \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{erg} like because-\textsc{erg} \textsc{2sg} do-\textsc{abil} and say \textsc{2sg} \textsc{decl} \textsc{q} \textsc{3sg} believe-\textsc{pl} \textsc{3sg} \textsc{irr}-\textsc{erg} \textsc{2sg} all be-\textsc{abil} \textsc{decl} \textsc{neg} be.\textsc{3sg} \textsc{q} \textsc{3sg} say \textsc{decl} \\

\exi{24}
\gll Thàk-hàt-ìn nàu-pang' pà kiko à, kà um hì; kà up-ná à kī-cin nàdìngìn hòng huh ìn à cí hì. \\
     new-strong-\textsc{erg} child-small father cry.out \textsc{3sg} \textsc{1sg} believe \textsc{decl} \textsc{1sg} believe-\textsc{nmlz} \textsc{3sg} \textsc{refl}-said \textsc{purp}.\textsc{erg} \textsc{3→1} help \textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} say \textsc{decl} \\

\exi{25}
\gll Mihon-tè àmau kìang-àh à hòng kī-khàwm dìng-ìn à hòng tái-ná ùh Jesuh ìn à mùh cìang-ìn, à pau théi lò, à bilngong dawi àw, híh nàu-pang sùng pàn pái-khìa ìnlà, túm-kík ngèi nàwn kèi ìn cí-ìn à taii hì. \\
     poor.person-\textsc{pl} \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{pro} beside-\textsc{loc} \textsc{3sg} \textsc{3→1} \textsc{refl}-gather \textsc{irr}-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} \textsc{3→1} stay-\textsc{nmlz} 2/3PL \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} see then-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} \textsc{pau} know \textsc{neg} \textsc{3sg} deaf fear voice this child-small inside \textsc{abl} go-exit and.then all-\textsc{iter} \textsc{exp} \textsc{cont} \textsc{neg}.\textsc{emph} \textsc{erg} say-\textsc{quot} \textsc{3sg} rebuke \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{When Jesus saw that the people came running together, he rebuked the foul spirit, saying unto him, Thou dumb and deaf spirit, I charge thee, come out of him, and enter no more into him.}}

\exi{26}
\gll À dawi nak-pì-tàk-ìn kiko-ìn nàu-pang à kòng-kawt-sàk khìt cìang-ìn à tái-khìa hì. Nàu-pang pèn misi tàwh kibang-ìn om-cìp àhìh màn-ìn mì khèmpeuh ìn, sí tá hì à cí ùh hì. \\
     \textsc{3sg} fear strong-big-exact-\textsc{erg} cry.out-\textsc{erg} child-small \textsc{3sg} \textsc{1sg→3}-tear-\textsc{caus} \textsc{seq} then-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} rebuke-out \textsc{decl} child-small \textsc{top} dead \textsc{com} be.alike-\textsc{cvb} be-close be.\textsc{3sg}.\textsc{rel} reason-\textsc{erg} person all \textsc{erg} die child \textsc{decl} \textsc{3sg} say 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And the spirit cried, and rent him sore, and came out of him: and he was as one dead; insomuch that many said, He is dead.}}

\exi{27}

     be.\textsc{3sg} although-\textsc{erg} \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{erg} child-small \textsc{3sg} hand-\textsc{erg} net-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} first-\textsc{up} and \textsc{3sg} \textsc{irr} \textsc{decl} \\

     \textsc{innsungah} \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{3sg} privately-ask then-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} life-follow-\textsc{pl} \textsc{erg} like because-\textsc{erg} \textsc{1pl}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{erg} fear drive.out know \textsc{neg} \textsc{1sg} \textsc{decl} 2/3PL \textsc{q} say-\textsc{quot} \textsc{3sg} ask.secretly 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\

\exi{30}

\exi{31}

\newpage

\section*{Chapter 10}
\addcontentsline{toc}{section}{Chapter 10}

\begin{exe}
\exi{1}
\gll Túa lái pàn-ìn Jesuh dìng-khìa-ìn Judea gàm lè Jordan Gun gàl gàm tèng-àh à pái hì. Àmà kìang-àh mihon tampi hòng kī-khàwm-kík ùh à, à hìlh ngeisa bàng-ìn àmaute tùngàh thù à hìlh hì. \\
     that midst \textsc{abl}-\textsc{erg} \textsc{jesuh} stand-exit-\textsc{erg} \textsc{judea} land and \textsc{jordan} river enemy land dwell-\textsc{loc} \textsc{3sg} go \textsc{decl} \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{poss} beside-\textsc{loc} poor.person many \textsc{3→1} \textsc{refl}-gather-\textsc{iter} 2/3PL \textsc{3sg} \textsc{3sg} tell desire like-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{pro} on-\textsc{loc} word \textsc{3sg} tell \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And he arose from thence, and cometh into the coasts of Judæa by the farther side of Jordan: and the people resort unto him again; and, as he was wont, he taught them again.}}

\exi{2}
\gll Farisi mì pàwl-khàt hòng pái ùh à, àmàh à mawhsak thèih nàdìng ùh à dèih-ná-ìn, mì khàt ìn à zi à mà-thèi dìng màh àhì hìam cí-ìn à dòng ùh hì. \\
     \textsc{farisi} person some-one \textsc{3→1} go 2/3PL \textsc{3sg} \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{3sg} adversary know.\textsc{ii} \textsc{purp} 2/3PL \textsc{3sg} want-\textsc{nmlz}-\textsc{erg} person one \textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} wife \textsc{3sg} raw-\textsc{abil} \textsc{irr} \textsc{emph} be.\textsc{3sg} \textsc{q} say-\textsc{quot} \textsc{3sg} until 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And the Pharisees came to him, and asked him, Is it lawful for a man to put away his wife? tempting him.}}

\exi{3}
\gll Jesuh ìn, moses ìn bàng thù hòng pía àhì hìam cí-ìn à dot cìang-ìn àmaute ìn, \\
     \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{erg} \textsc{moses} \textsc{erg} like word \textsc{3→1} give be.\textsc{3sg} \textsc{q} say-\textsc{quot} \textsc{3sg} ask then-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{erg} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And he answered and said unto them, What did Moses command you?}}

\exi{4}
\gll moses ìn kī-mak-ná lái gelh-sakin mà-sàk théi hì cí-ìn à dawng ùh hì. \\
     \textsc{moses} \textsc{erg} \textsc{refl}-divorce-\textsc{nmlz} midst write-\textsc{caus}.\textsc{erg} raw-\textsc{caus} know \textsc{decl} say-\textsc{quot} \textsc{3sg} receive 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And they said, Moses suffered to write a bill of divorcement, and to put her away.}}

\exi{5}
\gll Jesuh ìn àmaute kìang-àh, nòtè, hìlh-zàwh-ìn ōm lò nà híh manun Moses ìn híh ngèina à bāwl àhì hì. \\
     \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{erg} \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{pro} beside-\textsc{loc} \textsc{2pl}.\textsc{pro} teach-be.able-\textsc{cvb} exist \textsc{neg} \textsc{2sg} this sin \textsc{moses} \textsc{erg} this know-\textsc{nmlz} \textsc{3sg} make be.\textsc{3sg} \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And Jesus answered and said unto them, For the hardness of your heart he wrote you this precept.}}

\exi{6}
\gll Àhì zòng-ìn pian-cil lái-ìn, pasian ìn nu-méi lè pasal à bāwl hì. \\
     be.\textsc{3sg} although-\textsc{erg} born-alone midst-\textsc{erg} god \textsc{erg} woman and husband \textsc{3sg} make \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{But from the beginning of the creation God made them male and female.}}

\exi{7}
\gll Túa àhìh màn-ìn pasal ìn à nù lè à pà nusia-ìn à zi tàwh kī-gawm dìng à, \\
     that be.\textsc{3sg}.\textsc{rel} reason-\textsc{erg} husband \textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} female and \textsc{3sg} father abandon-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} wife \textsc{com} \textsc{refl}-seize \textsc{irr} \textsc{3sg} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{For this cause shall a man leave his father and mother, and cleave to his wife;}}

\exi{8}

\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And James and John, the sons of Zebedee, come unto him, saying, Master, we would that thou shouldest do for us whatsoever we shall desire.}}

\exi{36}
\gll Jesuh ìn, bàng kòng vái-hawm-sak dìng dèih nà hì ùh hìam cí-ìn à dot cìang-ìn \\

     \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{erg} name-famous-\textsc{erg} king throne on-\textsc{loc} \textsc{2sg} sleep then-\textsc{erg} \textsc{2sg} right-\textsc{loc} one \textsc{2sg} faint-side-\textsc{loc} one \textsc{3→1} act-\textsc{caus} offend \textsc{1sg} will 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \textsc{3sg} say 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\

\exi{38}

     be.\textsc{3sg} although-\textsc{erg} \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{erg} \textsc{2pl}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{erg} \textsc{2sg} \textsc{3→1} request 2/3PL \textsc{2sg} know \textsc{neg}.\textsc{emph} 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \textsc{1sg}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{erg} \textsc{1sg} suffer \textsc{irr} suffer-\textsc{nmlz} \textsc{2pl}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{erg} suffer-\textsc{compl} \textsc{irr} \textsc{3sg} \textsc{1sg} \textsc{refl}-immerse \textsc{purp} suffer-\textsc{nmlz}-\textsc{loc} \textsc{refl}-immerse-\textsc{compl} \textsc{irr} \textsc{2sg} \textsc{decl} 2/3PL \textsc{q} say-\textsc{quot} \textsc{3sg} ask then-\textsc{erg} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{But Jesus said unto them, Ye know not what ye ask: can ye drink of the cup that I drink of? and be baptized with the baptism that I am baptized with?}}

\exi{39}
\gll àmaute ìn, kà hí-zò dìng ùh hì cí-ìn à dawng ùh hì. Túa cìang-ìn Jesuh ìn àmaute kìang-àh, kèimah ìn gìm-ná kà thùak dìng màh bàng-ìn nà thùak takpi dìng ùh à, kà thùak dìng kī-phum-ná zòng nà thùak takpi dìng ùh hì. \\

\exi{40}
\gll Àhì zòng-ìn kà tak-lam-à tut dìng lè kà véi-lam-à tut dìng pèn kèi' hòng pìak-thèih hì lò à, à tù dìng-ìn Pasian ìn à vaihawmsak-sá-tè à' dìng àhì hì à cí hì. \\

     be.\textsc{3sg} although-\textsc{erg} \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{erg} \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{pro} call-\textsc{cvb} land-on person \textsc{3sg} rule-\textsc{pl} \textsc{erg} person-\textsc{pl} on-\textsc{loc} \textsc{3sg}-child.\textsc{pl} have-\textsc{erg} person \textsc{3sg} leader-\textsc{pl} \textsc{erg} word-have.\textsc{ii}-\textsc{nmlz} \textsc{com} \textsc{3sg} rule.\textsc{nmlz} word \textsc{2sg} know 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\

\newpage

\section*{Chapter 11}
\addcontentsline{toc}{section}{Chapter 11}

\begin{exe}
\exi{1}
\gll Jerusalem khùa-nái, Bethfage lè Bethany khùa-néu-tè à ōm-ná Oliv Mual à tun ùh cìang-ìn Jesuh ìn à nùng-zúi-tè nìh mà sawl à, \\
     \textsc{jerusalem} town-precious \textsc{bethfage} and Bethany town-small-\textsc{pl} \textsc{3sg} exist-\textsc{nmlz} olive mountain \textsc{3sg} arrive 2/3PL then-\textsc{erg} \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} life-follow-\textsc{pl} two alone send \textsc{3sg} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And when they came nigh to Jerusalem, unto Bethphage and Bethany, at the mount of Olives, he sendeth forth two of his disciples,}}

\exi{2}
\gll mái-à ōm khùa-àh và pái ùn. Khùa nà tun phetun, kuamah à tūan ngèi nái lòh-ná lano khàt khau à ki-khih nà mú dìng ùh hì. Hòng sut ùn-lá hòng kai ùn. \\
     face-\textsc{loc} exist town-\textsc{loc} go.and go \textsc{imp}.\textsc{pl} town \textsc{2sg} arrive hear nobody \textsc{3sg} ride \textsc{exp} near \textsc{neg}-\textsc{nmlz} colt one rope \textsc{3sg} bind \textsc{2sg} see.\textsc{i} \textsc{irr} 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \textsc{3→1} break \textsc{pl}.\textsc{imp}-and \textsc{3→1} ascend \textsc{imp}.\textsc{pl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{and saith unto them, Go your way into the village over against you: and as soon as ye be entered into it, ye shall find a colt tied, whereon never man sat; loose him, and bring him .}}

\exi{3}
\gll Mì khàt-pèuh ìn, bàng hàng-ìn túa lá khau sut nà hì ùh hìam' hòng cìh lèh, topa ìn dèih hì; híh lái màh-àh kòng kà-ì-kík-pah dìng ùh hì' cí-ìn gēn ùn à cí hì. \\
     person one-every \textsc{erg} like because-\textsc{erg} that take rope break \textsc{2sg} \textsc{decl} 2/3PL \textsc{q} \textsc{3→1} say.\textsc{nom} and lord \textsc{erg} want \textsc{decl} this midst likewise-\textsc{loc} \textsc{1sg→3} \textsc{1sg}-need-again-exactly \textsc{irr} 2/3PL \textsc{decl} say-\textsc{quot} speak \textsc{imp}.\textsc{pl} \textsc{3sg} say \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And if any man say unto you, Why do ye this? say ye that the Lord hath need of him; and straightway he will send him hither.}}

\exi{4}
\gll Àmau tegel zòng pái-pah ùh à, kongzing à kòng gei khàt-àh lano à ki-khih khàt mú ùh àhìh màn-ìn à khau à sut-pàh ùh hì. \\
     \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{pro} both also go-arrive 2/3PL \textsc{3sg} harp \textsc{3sg} \textsc{1sg→3} edge one-\textsc{loc} colt \textsc{3sg} bind one see.\textsc{i} 2/3PL be.\textsc{3sg}.\textsc{rel} reason-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} rope \textsc{3sg} spoil-\textsc{neg}.\textsc{abil} 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And they went their way, and found the colt tied by the door without in a place where two ways met; and they loose him.}}

\exi{5}
\gll Túa kiim-à ōm mì-tè ìn, bàng hàng-ìn túa lano khau sut nà hì ùh hìam cí-ìn à dot ùh cìang-ìn, \\
     that around-\textsc{nom} exist person-\textsc{pl} \textsc{erg} like because-\textsc{erg} that colt rope break \textsc{2sg} \textsc{decl} 2/3PL \textsc{q} say-\textsc{quot} \textsc{3sg} ask 2/3PL then-\textsc{erg} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And certain of them that stood there said unto them, What do ye, loosing the colt?}}

\exi{6}
\gll Jesuh' vái-khàk thù-tèng gēn ùh à, bangmah cìh nàwn lò ùh hì. \\
     \textsc{jesuh} go-command word-tell speak 2/3PL \textsc{3sg} nothing say.\textsc{nom} \textsc{cont} \textsc{neg} 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And they said unto them even as Jesus had commanded: and they let them go.}}

\exi{7}
\gll Jesuh kìang-àh à lano tun-pìh ùh à, à lano tùngàh à pùan ùh phah-ìn à tùngàh Jesuh à tuang hì. \\
     \textsc{jesuh} beside-\textsc{loc} \textsc{3sg} colt arrive-\textsc{appl} 2/3PL \textsc{3sg} \textsc{3sg} colt on-\textsc{loc} \textsc{3sg} cloth 2/3PL spread-\textsc{cvb} \textsc{3sg} on-\textsc{loc} \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{3sg} ride \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And they brought the colt to Jesus, and cast their garments on him; and he sat upon him.}}

\exi{8}
\gll Mì tám-pì-tè ìn àmà pái nàdìng lampi-àh à pùan ùh nà phah ùh à, mì pàwl-khàt ìn lolai pàn-ìn à sat ùh sawl-pang-tè nà phah ùh hì. \\
     person many-big-\textsc{pl} \textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{poss} go \textsc{purp} way-\textsc{loc} \textsc{3sg} cloth 2/3PL \textsc{2sg} spread 2/3PL \textsc{3sg} person some-one \textsc{erg} field \textsc{abl}-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} strike 2/3PL send-branch-\textsc{pl} \textsc{2sg} spread 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And many spread their garments in the way: and others cut down branches off the trees, and strawed them in the way.}}

\exi{9}
\gll Jesuh' mái-à à pái mì-tè lè à nùng-à à zúi mì-tè ìn, pasian phàt ùn! Topa' tāng-ìn à hòng pái mipa, Pasian ìn thù-phà pía tá hèn! \\
     \textsc{jesuh} face-\textsc{loc} \textsc{3sg} go person-\textsc{pl} and \textsc{3sg} live-\textsc{loc} \textsc{3sg} follow person-\textsc{pl} \textsc{erg} god worthy \textsc{imp}.\textsc{pl} lord take.hold-\textsc{cvb} \textsc{3sg} \textsc{3→1} go man god \textsc{erg} word-good give child \textsc{juss} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And they that went before, and they that followed, cried, saying, Hosanna; Blessed is he that cometh in the name of the Lord:}}

\exi{10}
\gll À hòng tùng dìng ì pú David' ukna, Pasian ìn thù-phà pía tá hèn! Pasian phàt ùn cí-ìn à áwng ùh hì. \\
     \textsc{3sg} \textsc{3→1} on \textsc{irr} \textsc{1pl}.\textsc{incl} grandfather \textsc{david} rule.\textsc{nmlz} god \textsc{erg} word-good give child \textsc{juss} god worthy \textsc{imp}.\textsc{pl} say-\textsc{quot} \textsc{3sg} open 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{Blessed be the kingdom of our father David, that cometh in the name of the Lord: Hosanna in the highest.}}

\exi{11}
\gll Túa bàng-ìn Jerusalem khùa sùng-àh Jesuh lút à, bìak-ínn sùng-àh pái-ìn nà khèmpeuh à ēn kawi-kawi hì. Túa cìang-ìn nì niam khin-tá àhìh màn-ìn sàwm lè nìh-tè tàwh Bethany khùa-àh à pái hì. \\
     that like-\textsc{erg} \textsc{jerusalem} town inside-\textsc{loc} \textsc{jesuh} enter \textsc{3sg} worship-house inside-\textsc{loc} go-\textsc{erg} \textsc{2sg} all \textsc{3sg} \textsc{en} crooked\textasciitilde{}REDUP \textsc{decl} that then-\textsc{erg} day lowly move-\textsc{nmlz} be.\textsc{3sg}.\textsc{rel} reason-\textsc{erg} ten and two-\textsc{pl} \textsc{com} Bethany town-\textsc{loc} \textsc{3sg} go \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And Jesus entered into Jerusalem, and into the temple: and when he had looked round about upon all things, and now the eventide was come, he went out unto Bethany with the twelve.}}

     \textsc{3sg} morning then-\textsc{erg} Bethany town \textsc{abl} go-exit 2/3PL \textsc{3sg} \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{3sg} stomach \textsc{3sg} hunger \textsc{decl} \\

\exi{13}

     \textsc{3sg} measure \textsc{3sg} \textsc{no} oil-tree one enemy-see be.\textsc{3sg}.\textsc{rel} reason-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} fruit-block and say-\textsc{quot} \textsc{3sg} \textsc{neg} \textsc{irr}-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} go.and go \textsc{decl} know name time \textsc{decl} \textsc{neg} be.\textsc{3sg}.\textsc{rel} reason-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} plain \textsc{3sg} arrive then-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} measure count-unable nothing \textsc{2sg} exist \textsc{neg} \textsc{decl} \\

     this \textsc{2sg}-\textsc{pl} who word \textsc{com} make \textsc{3sg} \textsc{2sg} make \textsc{purp}.\textsc{erg} who \textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg}-child.\textsc{pl} \textsc{3→1} give be.\textsc{3sg} \textsc{q} say-\textsc{quot} \textsc{3sg} ask 2/3PL then-\textsc{erg} \\
