\newpage

\section*{Chapter 12}
\addcontentsline{toc}{section}{Chapter 12}

\begin{exe}
\exi{1}
\gll Túa cìang-ìn Jesuh ìn àmaute kìang-àh thugen-teh-ná zàng-ìn thù hìlh à, mì khàt ìn lò zuan-ìn leeng-gui suan à, à kimkot um-ìn leeng-gah cil nàdìng bāwl à, à hon nàdìng tausang khàt à lām khìt cìang-ìn, lò khawh-làwh-tè khawh-làwh-sàk à, àmàh gàm dàng-àh à pái hì. \\
     that then-\textsc{erg} \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{erg} \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{pro} beside-\textsc{loc} preach-measure-\textsc{nmlz} use-\textsc{cvb} word tell \textsc{3sg} person one \textsc{erg} \textsc{neg} cross-\textsc{cvb} grape-vine plant \textsc{3sg} \textsc{3sg} round believe-\textsc{cvb} grape-cluster beginning \textsc{purp} make \textsc{3sg} \textsc{3sg} flock \textsc{purp} tower one \textsc{3sg} way \textsc{seq} then-\textsc{erg} \textsc{neg} able-earn-\textsc{pl} let-\textsc{abil}-\textsc{caus} \textsc{3sg} \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{pro} land other-\textsc{loc} \textsc{3sg} go \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And he began to speak unto them by parables. A certain man planted a vineyard, and set an hedge about it , and digged a place for the winefat, and built a tower, and let it out to husbandmen, and went into a far country.}}

\exi{2}
\gll Leeng-gah làwh hùn à tun cìang-ìn àmà ngàh dìng tāng-tèng à lá dìng-ìn lò khawh-làwh-tè kìang-àh à nàsèm-tè khàt à pái-sàk hì. \\
     grape-cluster \textsc{perf} time \textsc{3sg} arrive then-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{poss} get \textsc{irr} take.hold-until \textsc{3sg} take \textsc{irr}-\textsc{erg} \textsc{neg} able-earn-\textsc{pl} beside-\textsc{loc} \textsc{3sg} servant-\textsc{pl} one \textsc{3sg} go-\textsc{caus} \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And at the season he sent to the husbandmen a servant, that he might receive from the husbandmen of the fruit of the vineyard.}}

\exi{3}
\gll Lò khawh-làwh-tè ìn túa à nàsèm-pà màn-ìn sat-gàwp ùh à, à guak ciah-sàk-kík ùh hì. \\
     \textsc{neg} able-earn-\textsc{pl} \textsc{erg} that \textsc{3sg} servant-male reason-\textsc{erg} strike-grasp 2/3PL \textsc{3sg} \textsc{3sg} back return-\textsc{caus}-\textsc{iter} 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And they caught him , and beat him, and sent him away empty.}}

\exi{4}
\gll Túa cìang-ìn lò néi pà ìn à nàsèm dàng khàt à sawl hì. Àmaute ìn túa pà à lù-tāng nà liam-sàk-gàwp ùh à, à nà simmawh bāwl ùh hì. \\
     that then-\textsc{erg} \textsc{neg} have father \textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} servant other one \textsc{3sg} send \textsc{decl} \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{erg} that father \textsc{3sg} head-leader \textsc{2sg} wound-cause-\textsc{intens} 2/3PL \textsc{3sg} \textsc{3sg} \textsc{2sg} blaspheme make 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And again he sent unto them another servant; and at him they cast stones, and wounded him in the head, and sent him away shamefully handled.}}

\exi{5}
\gll Túa cìang-ìn à-dàng khàt sawl leuleu à, à nà thàt ùh hì. Túa bàng-ìn à-dàng tampi sawl à, pàwl-khàt nà sat-gàwp ùh à, pàwl-khàt nà thàt ùh hì. \\
     that then-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg}-other one send again \textsc{3sg} \textsc{3sg} \textsc{2sg} kill 2/3PL \textsc{decl} that like-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg}-other many send \textsc{3sg} some-one \textsc{2sg} strike-grasp 2/3PL \textsc{3sg} some-one \textsc{2sg} kill 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\

\gll Mì-tè ìn à lùng-sìm khèmpeuh, à pilna khèmpeuh, lè à hàt-ná khèmpeuh ùh tàwh Pasian itin, àmau pumpi à ít bàng-ìn à vēng-tè à ít dìng ùh àhì hì. Pasian bìak nàdìngìn bìak-ná táu tùngà gán gawhna-tè lè bìak-ná dàng khèmpeuh sàng-ìn híh thù-khàm nìh-tè zùih dìng thù-pì-zàw takpi hì à cí hì. \\
     person-\textsc{pl} \textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} stone-mind all \textsc{3sg} learning all and \textsc{3sg} strong-\textsc{nmlz} all 2/3PL \textsc{com} god lovingly \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{pro} body \textsc{3sg} love like-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} neighborhood-\textsc{pl} \textsc{3sg} love \textsc{irr} 2/3PL be.\textsc{3sg} \textsc{decl} god worship \textsc{purp}.\textsc{erg} worship-\textsc{nmlz} signal on-\textsc{3sg} bear understanding-\textsc{pl} and worship-\textsc{nmlz} other all high-\textsc{erg} this law two-\textsc{pl} follow-\textsc{nom} \textsc{irr} word-big-more indeed \textsc{decl} \textsc{3sg} say \textsc{decl} \\

\gll Jesuh ìn híh mipa' thugen-zia hòih-sá àhìh màn-ìn, pasian' Ukna sùng-àh à ōm dek-tàk màhmàh nà hì hì à cí hì. Túa khìt à ki-pan-ìn Jesuh kìang-àh kuamah ìn thù dòng ngam nàwn lò ùh hì. \\

\section*{Chapter 13}

\begin{exe}
\exi{1}
\gll Bìak-ínn pàn-ìn Jesuh à pusuah lái-tàk-ìn à nùng-zúi-tè khàt ìn, sía àw, híh bìak-ínn-te bàng-zah takin lìan à, à suangte bàng-zah takin gol àhì hìam à cí hì. \\
     worship-house \textsc{abl}-\textsc{erg} \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{3sg} lord midst-exact-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} life-follow-\textsc{pl} one \textsc{erg} evil voice this temples what-quantity really great \textsc{3sg} \textsc{3sg} descendants what-quantity really divide be.\textsc{3sg} \textsc{q} \textsc{3sg} say \textsc{decl} \\

\exi{2}
\gll Jesuh ìn, híh ínn-tè lìan-sá-ìn thù-pì nà sá màhmàh hì. Àhì zòng-ìn híh ínn-tè lám-ná-à à kī-cìang suangte nìh bèk nà-ngawn à kī-thuap-ná à ōm lò zah dòng-ìn à kī-phel-kék gàwp hùn hòng tùng dìng hì cí-ìn à dawng hì. \\
     \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{erg} this house-\textsc{pl} great-\textsc{past}-\textsc{erg} word-big \textsc{2sg} flesh very \textsc{decl} be.\textsc{3sg} although-\textsc{erg} this house-\textsc{pl} build-\textsc{nmlz}-\textsc{loc} \textsc{3sg} \textsc{refl}-announce descendants two only \textsc{2sg}-own \textsc{3sg} \textsc{refl}-stack-\textsc{nmlz} \textsc{3sg} exist \textsc{neg} fear collect-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} \textsc{refl}-break-\textsc{intens} all time \textsc{3→1} on \textsc{irr} \textsc{decl} say-\textsc{quot} \textsc{3sg} receive \textsc{decl} \\

\exi{4}

     this \textsc{2sg} speech fountain then-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3→1} on \textsc{irr} \textsc{3sg} this \textsc{2sg} word-tell-\textsc{pl} all \textsc{3→1} arrive \textsc{irr} then-\textsc{erg} like sign \textsc{3→1} exist \textsc{irr} be.\textsc{3sg} \textsc{q} say-\textsc{quot} \textsc{3sg} until 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\

\exi{7}
\gll À gam-lá à gàl-kido-ná thù-tè lè à nái-à gàl-kido-ná huging nà zàk ùh cìang-ìn pà-táu kèi ùn. Túa-tè à piang dìng màh hì à, hùn bèi-ná dìng hì nái lò hì. \\

\exi{8}
\gll Mì-nam khàt lè mì-nam khàt, kùmpì khàt lè kùmpì khàt kido dìng ùh hì. Mùn tuamtuam-àh zìn hòng ling dìng à, kial zòng hòng tùng dìng hì. Híh-tè khèmpeuh pèn gìm-ná kī-pat-ná hì pàn hì. \\

\exi{9}
\gll lìm-tàk-ìn kī-dawm ùn. Nòtè hòng kiman-ìn thù-khen zum-àh hòng kī-paipih dìng à, kī-khòp-ná ínn sùng-àh zòng hòng ki-sat dìng hì. Ukpi-tè lè kùmpì-tè mái-àh kèima thù gēn nàdìng hùn nà ngàh dìng ùh hì. \\
     sign-true-\textsc{erg} \textsc{refl}-god \textsc{imp}.\textsc{pl} \textsc{2pl}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{3→1} profit-\textsc{erg} word-divide bow-\textsc{loc} \textsc{3→1} \textsc{refl}-accompany \textsc{irr} \textsc{3sg} \textsc{refl}-gather-\textsc{nmlz} house inside-\textsc{loc} also \textsc{3→1} strike \textsc{irr} \textsc{decl} duke-\textsc{pl} and king-\textsc{pl} face-\textsc{loc} \textsc{1sg}.self word speak \textsc{purp} time \textsc{2sg} get \textsc{irr} 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\

\exi{10}
\gll Àhì zòng-ìn hùn bèi-ná à tun mà-ìn mì khèmpeuh tùngàh Lungdam-ná Thù kī-hìlh masa phot dìng hì. \\
     be.\textsc{3sg} although-\textsc{erg} time stone-\textsc{nmlz} \textsc{3sg} arrive self-\textsc{erg} person all on-\textsc{loc} rejoice-\textsc{nmlz} word \textsc{refl}-teach first first \textsc{irr} \textsc{decl} \\

\exi{11}
\gll Nòtè hòng kiman-ìn, thusit-ná à thùak dìng-ìn thù-khen zum-àh hòng kī-paipih cìang-ìn bàng gēn dìng ì-hí hìam, cí-ìn mà lùng-híh-màwh kèi ùn. À thù-gēn dìng pèn nòtè hì lò-ìn Khá Sìangtho àhìh màn-ìn à hùn tak cìang-ìn nà gēn dìng-ùn à hòng kī-sawl peuhpeuh nà gēn ùn. \\
     \textsc{2pl}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{3→1} profit-\textsc{erg} condemn-\textsc{nmlz} \textsc{3sg} suffer \textsc{irr}-\textsc{erg} word-divide bow-\textsc{loc} \textsc{3→1} \textsc{refl}-accompany then-\textsc{erg} like speak \textsc{irr} \textsc{1pl}.\textsc{incl}-be \textsc{q} say-\textsc{quot} alone heart-do-sin \textsc{neg}.\textsc{emph} \textsc{imp}.\textsc{pl} \textsc{3sg} speech \textsc{irr} \textsc{top} \textsc{2pl}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{decl} \textsc{neg}-\textsc{erg} \textsc{neg}.\textsc{perf} holy be.\textsc{3sg}.\textsc{rel} reason-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} time truly then-\textsc{erg} \textsc{2sg} speak \textsc{irr}-\textsc{pl}.\textsc{imp} \textsc{3sg} \textsc{3→1} \textsc{refl}-send every \textsc{2sg} speak \textsc{imp}.\textsc{pl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{But when they shall lead you , and deliver you up, take no thought beforehand what ye shall speak, neither do ye premeditate: but whatsoever shall be given you in that hour, that speak ye: for it is not ye that speak, but the Holy Ghost.}}

\exi{12}
\gll U-nàu khàt-lè-khàt à sìh nà-dìng-ùn kikhia dìng ùh à, pà ìn à tá khìa-ìn, tá ìn à nù lè à pà-tè khìa-ìn à thàt-sàk dìng ùh hì. \\
     elder-younger one-and-one \textsc{3sg} die \textsc{2sg}-\textsc{irr}-\textsc{imp} depart \textsc{irr} 2/3PL \textsc{3sg} father \textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} child out-\textsc{erg} child \textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} female and \textsc{3sg} male-\textsc{pl} out-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} kill-\textsc{caus} \textsc{irr} 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{Now the brother shall betray the brother to death, and the father the son; and children shall rise up against their parents, and shall cause them to be put to death.}}

\exi{13}
\gll Kèima hàng-ìn Gentail mì khèmpeuh ìn nòtè hòng mú-dah dìng ùh à, àhì zòng-ìn à sìh dongun à thùak-zò-tè ìn hot-khìat-ná à ngàh dìng ùh hì. \\
     \textsc{1sg}.self because-\textsc{erg} \textsc{gentail} person all \textsc{erg} \textsc{2pl}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{3→1} see-easy \textsc{irr} 2/3PL \textsc{3sg} be.\textsc{3sg} although-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} die boundary \textsc{3sg} suffer-\textsc{compl}-\textsc{pl} \textsc{erg} save-away-\textsc{nmlz} \textsc{3sg} get \textsc{irr} 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And ye shall be hated of all men for my name's sake: but he that shall endure unto the end, the same shall be saved.}}

\exi{14}
\gll àmà ōm lòh nàdìng pì-àh à lip-khá-phuai zehphit-ná à hòng ōm nà mùh ùh cìang-ìn híh lái à sìm-tè ìn Jesuh' cìh-nòp-ná théi tá ùn Judea gàm à ōm mì-tè mual-tùng-àh tái ùn. \\
     \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{poss} exist \textsc{neg}-\textsc{nom} \textsc{purp} grandmother-\textsc{loc} \textsc{3sg} ruin-place-heap desolation-\textsc{nmlz} \textsc{3sg} \textsc{3→1} exist \textsc{2sg} see 2/3PL then-\textsc{erg} this midst \textsc{3sg} count-\textsc{pl} \textsc{erg} \textsc{jesuh} say.\textsc{ii}-want-\textsc{nmlz} know child \textsc{imp}.\textsc{pl} \textsc{judea} land \textsc{3sg} exist person-\textsc{pl} mountain-top-\textsc{loc} check \textsc{imp}.\textsc{pl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{But when ye shall see the abomination of desolation, spoken of by Daniel the prophet, standing where it ought not, (let him that readeth understand,) then let them that be in Judæa flee to the mountains:}}

\exi{15}
\gll À ínn-khum zàng-àh à ōm lai-tàk àhì khàt-tè zòng, à kúm-sùk cìang-ìn à nèih-sa-te à tái-pìh dìng-ìn à lá dìng-ìn à ínn sùng-àh lút nàwn kèi hèn. \\
     \textsc{3sg} house-cover use-\textsc{loc} \textsc{3sg} exist middle-true be.\textsc{3sg} one-\textsc{pl} also \textsc{3sg} bow-\textsc{down} then-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} possessions \textsc{3sg} rebuke-\textsc{appl} \textsc{irr}-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} take \textsc{irr}-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} house inside-\textsc{loc} enter \textsc{cont} \textsc{neg}.\textsc{emph} \textsc{juss} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{and let him that is on the housetop not go down into the house, neither enter therein , to take any thing out of his house:}}

\exi{16}
\gll Lolai-àh à ōm lai-tàk àhì khàt-tè zòng, à pùan lá dìng-ìn à ínn ùh zuan nàwn kèi hèn. \\
     field-\textsc{loc} \textsc{3sg} exist middle-true be.\textsc{3sg} one-\textsc{pl} also \textsc{3sg} cloth take \textsc{irr}-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} house 2/3PL cross \textsc{cont} \textsc{neg}.\textsc{emph} \textsc{juss} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{and let him that is in the field not turn back again for to take up his garment.}}

\exi{17}
\gll Túa lái-tàk-ìn nù-pì naupai-ì-tè lè nàu-ngek néi-tè à dìng-ìn hàk-sá màhmàh dìng hì. \\
     that midst-exact-\textsc{erg} mother-big infant-\textsc{fem}-\textsc{pl} and child-small have-\textsc{pl} \textsc{3sg} \textsc{irr}-\textsc{erg} \textsc{intens}-\textsc{past} very \textsc{irr} \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{But woe to them that are with child, and to them that give suck in those days!}}

\exi{18}
\gll Phalbi lái-tàk-ìn híh thù hòng pian-khàk lòh nàdìngìn thù nà ngen ùn. \\
     winter midst-exact-\textsc{erg} this word \textsc{3→1} birth-\textsc{res} \textsc{neg}-\textsc{nom} \textsc{purp}.\textsc{erg} word \textsc{2sg} pray \textsc{imp}.\textsc{pl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And pray ye that your flight be not in the winter.}}

\exi{19}

     like reason \textsc{q} say.\textsc{nom} and god \textsc{erg} land-on \textsc{3sg} create-\textsc{caus} beginning \textsc{3sg} from now-time until one-self-\textsc{erg} that like difficult-\textsc{nmlz} \textsc{3sg} exist \textsc{exp} \textsc{neg} day-other then-\textsc{erg} also \textsc{3sg} exist \textsc{exp} \textsc{cont} \textsc{neg} \textsc{irr} that time midst-exact-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3→1} on \textsc{irr} \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{For in those days shall be affliction, such as was not from the beginning of the creation which God created unto this time, neither shall be.}}

\exi{20}
\gll Topa ìn túa gìm-ná hùn à nì khiam lò hí-lèh à sùak-tá-zò kuamah ōm lò dìng hì. Àhì zòng-ìn àmà teel mì-tè à khual-ná-ìn à nì à khiam hì. \\

\exi{21}

\exi{28}
\gll Théi kung tùng pà-ná thù-piang pàn-ìn thù théi ùn. À hiang-tè hòng meeng à, à teh hòng no cìang-ìn khùa-khal hùn hòng naita dìng hì, cí-ìn nà théi ùn. \\

\exi{30}

\exi{31}

\exi{32}
\gll àhì zòng-ìn túa nì lè túa nái hùn dìng kuamah ìn théi lò hì. Vantung-à ōm vàn-tùng mì-tè àhì à, Tá-pà àhì kèimah ìn àhì zòng-ìn kà théi kèi à, kà Pà bèk ìn à théi hì. \\

\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{But of that day and that hour knoweth no man, no, not the angels which are in heaven, neither the Son, but the Father.}}

\exi{33}
\gll Túa hùn dìng théi lò nà híh manun kikem-ìn pil-vang ùn. \\
     that time \textsc{irr} know \textsc{neg} \textsc{2sg} this sin keep-\textsc{erg} learn-wise \textsc{imp}.\textsc{pl} \\

\exi{34}
\gll Mì khàt khual-zin dìng-ìn pái-khìa à, à dinkhiat dìng cìang-ìn àmau' sep dìng ciat à nàsèm-tè tùngàh tavuan pía à, kòng-cíng pà ìn lìm-tàk-ìn à cin dìng à sawl mipa tàwh kī-bàng hì. \\

\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{For the Son of man is as a man taking a far journey, who left his house, and gave authority to his servants, and to every man his work, and commanded the porter to watch.}}

\exi{35}

\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{Watch ye therefore: for ye know not when the master of the house cometh, at even, or at midnight, or at the cockcrowing, or in the morning:}}

\exi{36}
\gll Túa hí-kèi-lèh àmàh thàk-hàt-ìn hòng tùng-ìn nà ihmut lai-tàk-ùn hòng tùak-khá dìng hì. \\

     \textsc{2pl}.\textsc{pro} on-\textsc{loc} \textsc{1sg→3} speak \textsc{emph} like-\textsc{erg} person all on-\textsc{loc} also wait-\textsc{cvb} \textsc{2sg} learn-wise \textsc{imp}.\textsc{pl} \textsc{1sg} say \textsc{decl} \textsc{3sg} say \textsc{decl} \\

\newpage

\section*{Chapter 14}
\addcontentsline{toc}{section}{Chapter 14}

\begin{exe}
\exi{1}
\gll Paisan Pawi lè Silngo Sawh lòh Anlum Pawi à tun mà nì nìh nì-ìn sìam-pì lìan-tè lè Thù-khàm hìlh sía-tè ìn Jesuh sìm-mat-ìn à thàh-thèih nàdìng ùh lam-pì à zòng ùh hì. \\
     god Pawi and feast correct \textsc{neg}-\textsc{nom} food Pawi \textsc{3sg} arrive alone day two day-\textsc{erg} priest-great big-\textsc{pl} and law tell evil-\textsc{pl} \textsc{erg} \textsc{jesuh} deceive-snare-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} slay-\textsc{abil} \textsc{purp} 2/3PL road \textsc{3sg} also 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{After two days was the feast of the passover, and of unleavened bread: and the chief priests and the scribes sought how they might take him by craft, and put him to death.}}

\exi{2}
\gll Àhì zòng-ìn, mihonpi-tè hòng buai khá dìng àhìh màn-ìn híh pawi hùn sùng-ìn híh kèi nì à cí ùh hì. \\
     be.\textsc{3sg} although-\textsc{erg} noble-\textsc{pl} \textsc{3→1} confuse \textsc{neg}.\textsc{perf} \textsc{irr} be.\textsc{3sg}.\textsc{rel} reason-\textsc{erg} this Pawi time inside-\textsc{erg} this \textsc{neg}.\textsc{emph} day \textsc{3sg} say 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{But they said, Not on the feast day , lest there be an uproar of the people.}}

\exi{3}
\gll Bethany khùa-àh, mì-phak àhì ngèi Simon' ínn-àh Jesuh ìn àn à nèk lái-tàk-ìn, nu-méi khàt ìn à manpha màhmàh nard pāk-nam-tui cí-tàk suang-ngo thawl dim-ìn à ōm khàt hòng tawi à, à suang-ngo thawl sukham-ìn Jesuh' lù tùngàh à pāk-nam-tui à sùng-sùk hì. \\
     Bethany town-\textsc{loc} person-half be.\textsc{3sg} \textsc{exp} \textsc{simon} house-\textsc{loc} \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{erg} \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{poss} \textsc{3sg} eat.\textsc{ii} midst-exact-\textsc{erg} woman one \textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} precious very spikenard ointment say-true stone-socket bottle full-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} exist one \textsc{3→1} carry \textsc{3sg} \textsc{3sg} stone-socket bottle grind-\textsc{erg} \textsc{jesuh} head on-\textsc{loc} \textsc{3sg} ointment \textsc{3sg} inside-pour \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And being in Bethany in the house of Simon the leper, as he sat at meat, there came a woman having an alabaster box of ointment of spikenard very precious; and she brake the box, and poured it on his head.}}

\exi{4}
\gll Túa lái-à ōm mì pàwl-khàt à hèh sùak à, bàng hàng-ìn híh pāk-nam-tui màwk bèi-sàk àhì hìam? \\
     that midst-\textsc{loc} exist person some-one \textsc{3sg} anger wither \textsc{3sg} like because-\textsc{erg} this ointment perhaps end-\textsc{caus} be.\textsc{3sg} \textsc{q} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And there were some that had indignation within themselves, and said, Why was this waste of the ointment made?}}

\exi{5}
\gll Kī-zūak lè ngun peek zathum val kī-khawng dìng à, à sum mì-zawng-tè tùngàh ki-pía théi dìng hì cí-ìn nak-pì-tàk-ìn túa nu-méi à mawhsak ùh hì. \\
     \textsc{refl}-sell and silver breadth three.hundred go.quickly \textsc{refl}-about \textsc{irr} \textsc{3sg} \textsc{3sg} extinguish person-all-\textsc{pl} on-\textsc{loc} be.given know \textsc{irr} \textsc{decl} say-\textsc{quot} strong-big-exact-\textsc{erg} that woman \textsc{3sg} adversary 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{For it might have been sold for more than three hundred pence, and have been given to the poor. And they murmured against her.}}

\exi{6}
\gll Àhì zòng-ìn Jesuh ìn, bangmah cìh se kèi ùn! Bàng hàng-ìn nawng-kai-sàk nà hì ùh hìam? Àmàh pèn à kī-lawm à hòih-ìn kèi tùngàh hòng gamta hì. \\
     be.\textsc{3sg} although-\textsc{erg} \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{erg} nothing say.\textsc{nom} dragon \textsc{neg}.\textsc{emph} \textsc{imp}.\textsc{pl} like because-\textsc{erg} \textsc{2sg}-help-\textsc{caus} \textsc{2sg} \textsc{decl} 2/3PL \textsc{q} \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{top} \textsc{3sg} \textsc{refl}-worthy \textsc{3sg} be.good-\textsc{cvb} \textsc{neg}.\textsc{emph} on-\textsc{loc} \textsc{3→1} send.away \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And Jesus said, Let her alone; why trouble ye her? she hath wrought a good work on me.}}

\exi{7}
\gll Mì-zawng-tè ahihleh nòtè tàwh ōm-khàwm tàwn-tùng dìng à, nà huh-nòp hùn pèuh-pèuh-ùn nà huh théi dìng ùh hì. Àhì zòng-ìn kèi pèn nòtè tàwh kòng ōm-khàwm tàwn-tùng kèi dìng hì. \\
     person-all-\textsc{pl} if \textsc{2pl}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{com} exist-gather ever-always \textsc{irr} \textsc{3sg} \textsc{2sg} blow-want time each-\textsc{redup}-\textsc{imp} \textsc{2sg} help know \textsc{irr} 2/3PL \textsc{decl} be.\textsc{3sg} although-\textsc{erg} \textsc{neg}.\textsc{emph} \textsc{top} \textsc{2pl}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{com} \textsc{1sg→3} exist-gather ever-always \textsc{neg}.\textsc{emph} \textsc{irr} \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{For ye have the poor with you always, and whensoever ye will ye may do them good: but me ye have not always.}}

\exi{8}
\gll Àmàh ìn kà luang à ki-vui nàdìngìn pāk-nam-tui à hòng mà nuh-khol hì à, à híh-thèih zah-zah cìang à híh khin-tá àhì hì. \\

     that then-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3→1} go \textsc{3sg} \textsc{3sg} life-follow three-\textsc{pl} \textsc{1pl}.\textsc{incl}-see-\textsc{erg} exist \textsc{3sg} see then-\textsc{erg} \textsc{peter} beside-\textsc{loc} \textsc{simon} voice \textsc{1pl}-see \textsc{2sg} \textsc{decl} 2/3PL \textsc{q} near one inside \textsc{2sg}-own \textsc{3→1} wait south \textsc{neg} shine \textsc{2sg} \textsc{decl} 2/3PL \textsc{q} \textsc{3sg} say \textsc{decl} \\

\exi{69}
\gll Túa nu-méi màh ìn à omna-àh Peter mú à, à gei-à ōm-tè kìang-àh, híh pà, hua mì-tè khàt hì takpi hì à cí-kík leuleu hì. \\
     that woman \textsc{emph} \textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} exist.\textsc{nmlz}-\textsc{loc} \textsc{peter} see.\textsc{i} \textsc{3sg} \textsc{3sg} edge-\textsc{loc} exist-\textsc{pl} beside-\textsc{loc} this father garden person-\textsc{pl} one \textsc{decl} indeed \textsc{decl} \textsc{3sg} say-\textsc{iter} again \textsc{decl} \\

\exi{70}

     that \textsc{seq} twin-\textsc{erg} then two-time-\textsc{nmlz} \textsc{3sg} drum \textsc{decl} that then-\textsc{erg} then two-time \textsc{3sg} dance self-\textsc{erg} \textsc{neg}.\textsc{emph} three.times \textsc{2sg} \textsc{3→1} deny \textsc{irr} \textsc{decl} say-\textsc{quot} \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{poss} on-\textsc{loc} \textsc{3sg} speak-\textsc{past} word \textsc{peter} \textsc{erg} memorial \textsc{3sg} grieve-too-\textsc{inst} \textsc{3sg} weep \textsc{decl} \\

\end{exe}

\begin{exe}
\exi{1}

\exi{29}
\gll Àmàh à và mú-khá mì peuhpeuh ìn à lù ùh sing-ìn zah-pìh-bāwl ùh à, à! Bìak-ínn sù-sía-ìn nì thùm sùng-ìn à lám-kík dìng pà! \\
     \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{3sg} go.and see.\textsc{i}-place person every \textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} head 2/3PL tree-\textsc{erg} wag-head-do 2/3PL \textsc{3sg} \textsc{3sg} worship-house \textsc{caus}-bad-\textsc{erg} day three inside-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} build-\textsc{iter} \textsc{irr} father \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And they that passed by railed on him, wagging their heads, and saying, Ah, thou that destroyest the temple, and buildest it in three days,}}

\exi{30}
\gll Sing-lam-teh tùng pàn-ìn hòng kúm-sùk ìnlà, nangmah ki-honkhia tàwm ìn à cí ùh hì. \\
     wood-cross on \textsc{abl}-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3→1} bow-\textsc{down} and.then \textsc{2sg}.\textsc{pro} escape produce \textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} say 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{save thyself, and come down from the cross.}}

\exi{31}
\gll Túa bàng-màh-ìn sìam-pì lìan-tè lè Thù-khàm hìlh sía-tè ìn zòng zah-pìh bāwl-ìn, midang-tè honkhia-zò napi, àmàh lè àmàh ki-honkhia zò lò! \\
     that what-\textsc{emph}-\textsc{erg} priest-great big-\textsc{pl} and law tell evil-\textsc{pl} \textsc{erg} also fear-\textsc{appl} make-\textsc{cvb} other.person-\textsc{pl} bring.out-\textsc{compl} but \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{pro} and \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{pro} escape south \textsc{neg} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{Likewise also the chief priests mocking said among themselves with the scribes, He saved others; himself he cannot save.}}

\exi{32}
\gll Israel mì-tè' kùmpì-pà Khrih tù-ìn sing-lam-teh tùng pàn-ìn hòng kúm-sùk lèh àmàh um nì à kici ùh hì. Jesuh tàwh à kī-khai khàwm mì nìh-tè ìn zòng à simmawh-bāwl ùh hì. \\
     \textsc{israel} person-\textsc{pl} king-male \textsc{khrih} now-\textsc{erg} wood-cross on \textsc{abl}-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3→1} bow-\textsc{down} and \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{pro} believe day \textsc{3sg} called 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{com} \textsc{3sg} \textsc{refl}-hold gather person two-\textsc{pl} \textsc{erg} also \textsc{3sg} blaspheme-do 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{Let Christ the King of Israel descend now from the cross, that we may see and believe. And they that were crucified with him reviled him.}}

\exi{33}
\gll Túa cìang-ìn sun-kím nái sàwm lè nìh lai-tàk à ki-pan-ìn nái thùm sùng léi-tùng khèmpeuh-àh khim à zing hì. \\
     that then-\textsc{erg} burn-half near ten and two middle-true \textsc{3sg} from near three inside land-on all-\textsc{loc} edge \textsc{3sg} morning \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And when the sixth hour was come, there was darkness over the whole land until the ninth hour.}}

\exi{34}
\gll Nì-tàk nái thùm lái-tàk-ìn Jesuh nak-pì-tàk-ìn kiko à, kà Pasian, kà Pasian àw, bàng hàng-ìn kèi hòng nusia nà hì hìam à cìh-ná àhì, eloi, Eloi, lām-à sabakthani à cí hì. \\
     day-exact near three midst-exact-\textsc{erg} \textsc{jesuh} strong-big-exact-\textsc{erg} cry.out \textsc{3sg} \textsc{1sg} god \textsc{1sg} god voice like because-\textsc{erg} \textsc{neg}.\textsc{emph} \textsc{3→1} forsake \textsc{2sg} \textsc{decl} \textsc{q} \textsc{3sg} say.\textsc{nom}-\textsc{nmlz} be.\textsc{3sg} \textsc{eloi} \textsc{eloi} way-\textsc{loc} forsaken.me[Aramaic] \textsc{3sg} say \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And at the ninth hour Jesus cried with a loud voice, saying, Eloi, Eloi, lama sabachthani? which is, being interpreted, My God, my God, why hast thou forsaken me?}}

\exi{35}
\gll Túa à kī-ko-ná à zàk ùh cìang-ìn túa lái-à ōm mì pàwl-khàt-tè ìn, elijah à sam hì à cí ùh hì. \\
     that \textsc{3sg} \textsc{refl}-cry-\textsc{nmlz} \textsc{3sg} hear.\textsc{ii} 2/3PL then-\textsc{erg} that midst-\textsc{loc} exist person some-one-\textsc{pl} \textsc{erg} \textsc{elijah} \textsc{3sg} open \textsc{decl} \textsc{3sg} say 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And some of them that stood by, when they heard it , said, Behold, he calleth Elias.}}

\exi{36}
\gll Túa lái-tàk-ìn mì khàt và tái à, leeng-gah-zu-hau sùng-àh tùi-hūp-ná diah-ìn pumpeeng dawn-àh à hèn-khit cìang-ìn Jesuh' hūp dìng-ìn tah-tò à, khawl dih ùn, sing-lam-teh tùng pàn-ìn à sut-khìa dìng-ìn Elijah hòng pái hìam, ēn dih nì à cí hì. \\
     that midst-exact-\textsc{erg} person one go.and check \textsc{3sg} eagle-vulture-wine-rich inside-\textsc{loc} water-sponge-\textsc{nmlz} dip-\textsc{cvb} whole top-\textsc{loc} \textsc{3sg} condemn-away then-\textsc{erg} \textsc{jesuh} mouth \textsc{irr}-\textsc{erg} fill-put \textsc{3sg} rest consider \textsc{imp}.\textsc{pl} wood-cross on \textsc{abl}-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} break-out \textsc{irr}-\textsc{erg} \textsc{elijah} \textsc{3→1} go \textsc{q} \textsc{en} consider day \textsc{3sg} say \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And one ran and filled a spunge full of vinegar, and put it on a reed, and gave him to drink, saying, Let alone; let us see whether Elias will come to take him down.}}

\exi{37}
\gll Túa cìang-ìn nak-pì-tàk-ìn Jesuh kiko-ìn à lai-tat hì. \\
     that then-\textsc{erg} strong-big-exact-\textsc{erg} \textsc{jesuh} cry.out-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} writing-end \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And Jesus cried with a loud voice, and gave up the ghost.}}

\exi{38}
\gll Bìak-ínn sùng-à kī-dal-ná pùan à tùng lām pàn à taw dòng-ìn kī-kék-ìn phel-nìh à kī-sùah hì. \\
     worship-house inside-\textsc{3sg} \textsc{refl}-hinder-\textsc{nmlz} cloth \textsc{3sg} on way \textsc{abl} \textsc{3sg} with collect-\textsc{erg} \textsc{refl}-scratch-\textsc{cvb} part-two \textsc{3sg} \textsc{refl}-escape \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And the veil of the temple was rent in twain from the top to the bottom.}}

\exi{39}
\gll Jesuh' mái-àh à dìng gàl-kap máng-pà ìn túa bàng-ìn kiko-ìn à lai-tah à mùh cìang-ìn, híh pà, Pasian' tá tak-tak àhì hì à cí hì. \\
     \textsc{jesuh} face-\textsc{loc} \textsc{3sg} \textsc{irr} soldier chief-father \textsc{erg} that like-\textsc{erg} cry.out-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} time-exact \textsc{3sg} see then-\textsc{erg} this father god child great\textasciitilde{}REDUP be.\textsc{3sg} \textsc{decl} \textsc{3sg} say \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And when the centurion, which stood over against him, saw that he so cried out, and gave up the ghost, he said, Truly this man was the Son of God.}}

\exi{40}
\gll Jesuh à gàl èt nu-méi pàwl-khàt zòng à ōm hì. Túa-tè lāk-àh Magdala khùa-mì Mary, à nàu-zàw James lè Josef' nù Mary, lè Salome àhì ùh hì. \\
     \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{3sg} enemy care woman some-one also \textsc{3sg} exist \textsc{decl} \textsc{dist}-\textsc{pl} among-\textsc{loc} \textsc{magdala} town-person \textsc{mary} \textsc{3sg} child-more \textsc{james} and \textsc{josef} female \textsc{mary} and \textsc{salome} be.\textsc{3sg} 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{There were also women looking on afar off: among whom was Mary Magdalene, and Mary the mother of James the less and of Joses, and Salome;}}

\exi{41}
\gll Galilee gàm sùng-àh Jesuh à ōm lái-ìn híh numei-tè ìn Jesuh zúi-ìn à huh ùh hì. Jerusalem cìang dòng Jesuh à hòng zúi nu-méi dàng tampi zòng à ōm hì. \\
     \textsc{galilee} land inside-\textsc{loc} \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{3sg} exist midst-\textsc{erg} this woman-\textsc{pl} \textsc{erg} \textsc{jesuh} follow-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} help 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \textsc{jerusalem} then until \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{3sg} \textsc{3→1} follow woman other many also \textsc{3sg} exist \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{(who also, when he was in Galilee, followed him, and ministered unto him;) and many other women which came up with him unto Jerusalem.}}

\exi{42}
\gll Túa nì pèn Sabbath nì mà, Kī-gin' nì àhìh màn-ìn nì-tàk lām cìang-ìn, \\
     that day \textsc{top} \textsc{sabbath} day alone \textsc{refl}-fear day be.\textsc{3sg}.\textsc{rel} reason-\textsc{erg} day-exact way then-\textsc{erg} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And now when the even was come, because it was the preparation, that is, the day before the sabbath,}}

\exi{43}
\gll mì-tè ìn à zah-tàk, ulian vaihawm-tè lāk-àh à kī-hel, Pasian' Ùk dìng hùn zòng à lamen, Arimathea khùa-mì Josef, hangtakin Pilat kìang-àh hòng pái-ìn Jesuh' luang à hòng ngen hì. \\
     person-\textsc{pl} \textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} fear-true \textsc{pl}.elder imagine-\textsc{pl} among-\textsc{loc} \textsc{3sg} \textsc{refl}-hell god rule \textsc{irr} time also \textsc{3sg} hope \textsc{arimathea} town-person \textsc{josef} boldly \textsc{pilat} beside-\textsc{loc} \textsc{3→1} go-\textsc{erg} \textsc{jesuh} flow \textsc{3sg} \textsc{3→1} pray \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{Joseph of Arimathæa, an honourable counsellor, which also waited for the kingdom of God, came, and went in boldly unto Pilate, and craved the body of Jesus.}}

\exi{44}
\gll Pilat ìn à lungsim-àh, Jesuh à sí khín takpi màh hì dìng àhì hìam, cí-ìn ngaihsun àhìh màn-ìn gàl-kap máng-pà sàm-sàk à, sí khin-tá àhì hìam, cí-ìn à dòng hì. \\
     \textsc{pilat} \textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} heart-\textsc{loc} \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{3sg} die \textsc{imm} indeed \textsc{emph} \textsc{decl} \textsc{irr} be.\textsc{3sg} \textsc{q} say-\textsc{quot} think be.\textsc{3sg}.\textsc{rel} reason-\textsc{erg} soldier chief-father call-\textsc{caus} \textsc{3sg} die move-\textsc{nmlz} be.\textsc{3sg} \textsc{q} say-\textsc{quot} \textsc{3sg} until \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And Pilate marvelled if he were already dead: and calling unto him the centurion, he asked him whether he had been any while dead.}}

\exi{45}
\gll Gàl-kap máng-pà' gēn-ná pàn-ìn à sìh-khìt-ná thù à thèih cìang-ìn à luang à làk-thèih nàdìngìn Josef tùngàh thù à pía hì. \\
     soldier chief-father speak-\textsc{nmlz} \textsc{abl}-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} pass-finish-\textsc{nmlz} word \textsc{3sg} know.\textsc{ii} then-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} flow \textsc{3sg} take-\textsc{abil} \textsc{purp}.\textsc{erg} \textsc{josef} on-\textsc{loc} word \textsc{3sg} give \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And when he knew it of the centurion, he gave the body to Joseph.}}

\exi{46}
\gll Josef ìn zòng pùan-pāk léi à, sing-lam-teh tùng pàn-ìn Jesuh' luang lá-khìa-ìn, à pùan léi tàwh hòih-tàk-ìn vial-ìn tuam à, tàwh-sá-ìn à ōm suang han sùng-àh à sial hì. Túa cìang-ìn suangtum khàt hual-ìn à kòng-vang à hu hì. \\
     \textsc{josef} \textsc{erg} also cloth-divide buy \textsc{3sg} wood-cross on \textsc{abl}-\textsc{erg} \textsc{jesuh} flow take-out-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} cloth buy \textsc{com} good-exact-\textsc{erg} encircle-\textsc{cvb} swell \textsc{3sg} \textsc{com}-\textsc{past}-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} exist stone sepulchre inside-\textsc{loc} \textsc{3sg} carcass \textsc{decl} that then-\textsc{erg} stone one roll-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} way-empty \textsc{3sg} help \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And he bought fine linen, and took him down, and wrapped him in the linen, and laid him in a sepulchre which was hewn out of a rock, and rolled a stone unto the door of the sepulchre.}}

\exi{47}
\gll Magdala khùa-mì Mary lè Josef' nù Mary ìn, Jesuh à kī-vui-ná mùn à théi ùh hì. \\
     \textsc{magdala} town-person \textsc{mary} and \textsc{josef} female \textsc{mary} \textsc{erg} \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{3sg} \textsc{refl}-bury-\textsc{nmlz} place \textsc{3sg} know 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And Mary Magdalene and Mary the mother of Joses beheld where he was laid.}}

\end{exe}
\newpage

\section*{Chapter 16}
\addcontentsline{toc}{section}{Chapter 16}

\begin{exe}
\exi{1}
\gll Sabbath nì à bèi khìt cìang-ìn Magdala khùa-mì Mary, James nù Mary, lè Salome-tè ìn Jesuh' luang à và zut nà-dìng-ùn pāk-nam-tui à và léi ùh hì. \\
     \textsc{sabbath} day \textsc{3sg} finish \textsc{seq} then-\textsc{erg} \textsc{magdala} town-person \textsc{mary} \textsc{james} female \textsc{mary} and \textsc{salome}-\textsc{pl} \textsc{erg} \textsc{jesuh} flow \textsc{3sg} go.and overlay \textsc{2sg}-\textsc{irr}-\textsc{imp} ointment \textsc{3sg} go.and buy 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And when the sabbath was past, Mary Magdalene, and Mary the mother of James, and Salome, had bought sweet spices, that they might come and anoint him.}}

\exi{2}
\gll Nì-pì nì zing-sàng tùng ni-sùah phèt-ìn han-àh à pái ùh hì. \\
     day-great day morning-high on birthday twin-\textsc{erg} sepulchre-\textsc{loc} \textsc{3sg} go 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And very early in the morning the first day of the week, they came unto the sepulchre at the rising of the sun.}}

\exi{3}
\gll Àmaute khàt-lè-khàt kī-kúm ùh à, han kòng-vang huk-ná suangtum kua'n hòng lik-khìat-sàk dìng àhì hìam à cí ùh hì. \\
     \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{pro} one-and-one \textsc{refl}-year 2/3PL \textsc{3sg} sepulchre way-empty cover-\textsc{nmlz} stone nobody.\textsc{emph} \textsc{3→1} turn.back-depart-\textsc{caus} \textsc{irr} be.\textsc{3sg} \textsc{q} \textsc{3sg} say 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And they said among themselves, Who shall roll us away the stone from the door of the sepulchre?}}

\exi{4}
\gll Túa lái-tàk-ìn à khùa-dāk uhleh à suangtum à kī-lik-khìa khinsa-ìn à mú ùh hì. túa suangtum à gol màhmàh khàt àhì hì \\
     that midst-exact-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} town-near 2/3PL.if \textsc{3sg} stone \textsc{3sg} \textsc{refl}-roll-out mock-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} see.\textsc{i} 2/3PL \textsc{decl} that stone \textsc{3sg} divide very one be.\textsc{3sg} \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And when they looked, they saw that the stone was rolled away: for it was very great.}}

\exi{5}
\gll Han sùng-àh à lút uhleh, à taklam pang uhah, pùan-pāk à silh tangval khàt à tù mú ùh à, lamdang-sá-ìn à lau ùh hì. \\
     sepulchre inside-\textsc{loc} \textsc{3sg} enter 2/3PL.if \textsc{3sg} right side 2/3PL.\textsc{loc} cloth-divide \textsc{3sg} clothe young.man one \textsc{3sg} now see.\textsc{i} 2/3PL \textsc{3sg} different-\textsc{intns}-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} fear 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And entering into the sepulchre, they saw a young man sitting on the right side, clothed in a long white garment; and they were affrighted.}}

\exi{6}
\gll Túa tangval-pà ìn, lamdang-sá kèi ùn. Sing-lam-teh tùngàh à kī-thàt Nà-zareth khùa-mì Jesuh nà zòng ùh hì. Àmàh kī-thok-ik-sàk khín à, híh lái-àh ōm nàwn lò hì. Àmàh à kī-sial-ná mùn hòng ēn ùn. \\
     that youth-father \textsc{erg} different-\textsc{intns} \textsc{neg}.\textsc{emph} \textsc{imp}.\textsc{pl} wood-cross on-\textsc{loc} \textsc{3sg} \textsc{refl}-kill \textsc{2sg}-? town-person \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{2sg} also 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{refl}-rise-\textsc{iter}-\textsc{caus} \textsc{imm} \textsc{3sg} this midst-\textsc{loc} exist \textsc{cont} \textsc{neg} \textsc{decl} \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{3sg} \textsc{refl}-rise-\textsc{nmlz} place \textsc{3→1} \textsc{en} \textsc{imp}.\textsc{pl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And he saith unto them, Be not affrighted: Ye seek Jesus of Nazareth, which was crucified: he is risen; he is not here: behold the place where they laid him.}}

\exi{7}
\gll Tù-ìn pái ùn-lá, Peter lè Jesuh' nùng-zúi dàng-tè kìang-àh híh thù và gēn ùn. Nòtè tùngàh hòng gēn-sá bàng-ìn Galilee gàm àmaute mái-àh pái hì; túa lái-àh àmàh nà mú dìng ùh hì, cí hì, cí ùn à cí hì. \\
     now-\textsc{erg} go \textsc{pl}.\textsc{imp}-and \textsc{peter} and \textsc{jesuh} life-follow other-\textsc{pl} beside-\textsc{loc} this word go.and speak \textsc{imp}.\textsc{pl} \textsc{2pl}.\textsc{pro} on-\textsc{loc} \textsc{3→1} speak-\textsc{past} like-\textsc{erg} \textsc{galilee} land \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{pro} face-\textsc{loc} go \textsc{decl} that midst-\textsc{loc} \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{2sg} see.\textsc{i} \textsc{irr} 2/3PL \textsc{decl} say \textsc{decl} say \textsc{imp}.\textsc{pl} \textsc{3sg} say \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{But go your way, tell his disciples and Peter that he goeth before you into Galilee: there shall ye see him, as he said unto you.}}

\exi{8}
\gll Àmaute ìn lamdang-sá-ìn lau ùh àhìh màn-ìn han pàn-ìn tái-sùak pah ùh à, kuamah dàng kìang-àh híh thù gēn lò ùh hì. \\
     \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{erg} different-\textsc{intns}-\textsc{erg} fear 2/3PL be.\textsc{3sg}.\textsc{rel} reason-\textsc{erg} sepulchre \textsc{abl}-\textsc{erg} rebuke-become do.so 2/3PL \textsc{3sg} nobody other beside-\textsc{loc} this word speak \textsc{neg} 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And they went out quickly, and fled from the sepulchre; for they trembled and were amazed: neither said they any thing to any man ; for they were afraid.}}

\exi{9}
\gll sìh-ná pàn-ìn Jesuh à thawh-kík khìt cìang-ìn àmà sùng pàn dawi sagih à hawl-khìat-ná, Magdala khùa-mì Mary tùngàh Nì-pì nì zing-sàng tùng-ìn kilang masa hì. \\
     blood-\textsc{nmlz} \textsc{abl}-\textsc{erg} \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{3sg} resurrection \textsc{seq} then-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{poss} inside \textsc{abl} fear seven \textsc{3sg} drive-out-\textsc{nmlz} \textsc{magdala} town-person \textsc{mary} on-\textsc{loc} day-great day morning-high on-\textsc{erg} height first \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{Now when Jesus was risen early the first day of the week, he appeared first to Mary Magdalene, out of whom he had cast seven devils.}}

\exi{10}
\gll Túa nù zòng hòng pái-ìn à dah à kàp-ìn à ōm Jesuh' lawm lūi-tè kìang-àh híh thù à và gēn hì. \\
     that female also \textsc{3→1} go-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} put \textsc{3sg} weep-\textsc{cvb} \textsc{3sg} exist \textsc{jesuh} worthy river-\textsc{pl} beside-\textsc{loc} this word \textsc{3sg} go.and speak \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And she went and told them that had been with him, as they mourned and wept.}}

\exi{11}
\gll Àhì zòng-ìn Jesuh à nuntak-ná thù lè túa nù màhmàh ìn à mùh khit-ná thù à gēn-ná à zàk ùh hàng-ìn, à thù-gēn um zò lò ùh hì \\
     be.\textsc{3sg} although-\textsc{erg} \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{3sg} live-\textsc{nmlz} word and that female very \textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} see after-\textsc{nmlz} word \textsc{3sg} speak-\textsc{nmlz} \textsc{3sg} hear.\textsc{ii} 2/3PL because-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} speech believe south \textsc{neg} 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And they, when they had heard that he was alive, and had been seen of her, believed not.}}

\exi{12}
\gll túa khìt cìang-ìn khùa-pì pàn-ìn khùa-néu-àh nùng-zúi nìh-tè à pái lai-tàk-ùn àmaute tùngàh à mel tuam khàt-ìn Jesuh kilang hì. \\
     that \textsc{seq} then-\textsc{erg} village-big \textsc{abl}-\textsc{erg} town-small-\textsc{loc} life-follow two-\textsc{pl} \textsc{3sg} go middle-true-\textsc{pl}.\textsc{imp} \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{pro} on-\textsc{loc} \textsc{3sg} void swell one-\textsc{erg} \textsc{jesuh} height \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{After that he appeared in another form unto two of them, as they walked, and went into the country.}}

\exi{13}
\gll Híh tegel zòng kī-lèh kī-kin à lawm dàng-tè ùh kìang-àh gēn ùh à, àhì zòng-ìn àmau' thù-gēn, nà um lò ùh hì \\
     this both also \textsc{refl}-and \textsc{refl}-god \textsc{3sg} worthy other-\textsc{pl} 2/3PL beside-\textsc{loc} speak 2/3PL \textsc{3sg} be.\textsc{3sg} although-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{pro} speech \textsc{2sg} believe \textsc{neg} 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And they went and told it unto the residue: neither believed they them.}}

\exi{14}
\gll túa khìt cìang-ìn à tawpna-àh, àn à nèk lai-tàk-ùn nùng-zúi sàwm lè khàt-tè màhmàh kìang-àh à kilang hì. À kī-thawh-kík-sàk khìt cìang-ìn àmàh à mú mì-tè' thù-gēn um lò ùh àhìh màn-ìn à lùng-khauh-ná ùh lè à up lòh-ná hangun àmaute à taii hì. \\
     that \textsc{seq} then-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} end.\textsc{nmlz}-\textsc{loc} \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{poss} \textsc{3sg} eat.\textsc{ii} middle-true-\textsc{pl}.\textsc{imp} life-follow ten and one-\textsc{pl} very beside-\textsc{loc} \textsc{3sg} height \textsc{decl} \textsc{3sg} \textsc{refl}-rise-\textsc{iter}-\textsc{caus} \textsc{seq} then-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{3sg} see.\textsc{i} person-\textsc{pl} speech believe \textsc{neg} 2/3PL be.\textsc{3sg}.\textsc{rel} reason-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3sg} heart-strong-\textsc{nmlz} 2/3PL and \textsc{3sg} \textsc{pl}.\textsc{q} \textsc{neg}-\textsc{nmlz} \textsc{hangun} \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{pro} \textsc{3sg} rebuke \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{Afterward he appeared unto the eleven as they sat at meat, and upbraided them with their unbelief and hardness of heart, because they believed not them which had seen him after he was risen.}}

\exi{15}
\gll Túa khìt cìang-ìn àmaute tùngàh, léi-tùng khèmpeuh-àh nòtè pái kawi-kawi ùn-lá, mì khèmpeuh tùngàh Lungdam-ná Thù nà hìlh tá ùn. \\
     that \textsc{seq} then-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{pro} on-\textsc{loc} land-on all-\textsc{loc} \textsc{2pl}.\textsc{pro} go crooked\textasciitilde{}REDUP \textsc{pl}.\textsc{imp}-and person all on-\textsc{loc} rejoice-\textsc{nmlz} word \textsc{2sg} tell child \textsc{imp}.\textsc{pl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And he said unto them, Go ye into all the world, and preach the gospel to every creature.}}

\exi{16}
\gll Lungdam-ná Thù um-ìn tùi à kī-phum mì peuhpeuh ìn hot-khìat-ná ngàh dìng à, à um lò mì peuhpeuh ìn màwh-sàk-ná thùak dìng ùh hì. \\
     rejoice-\textsc{nmlz} word believe-\textsc{cvb} water \textsc{3sg} \textsc{refl}-immerse person every \textsc{erg} save-away-\textsc{nmlz} get \textsc{irr} \textsc{3sg} \textsc{3sg} believe \textsc{neg} person every \textsc{erg} err-\textsc{caus}-\textsc{nmlz} suffer \textsc{irr} 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{He that believeth and is baptized shall be saved; but he that believeth not shall be damned.}}

\exi{17}
\gll À um mì-tè tùngàh híh vangliat-ná lìm-tè ki-pía dìng hì: Kèima hàng-ìn dawi hawlkhia théi dìng ùh à, pau dàng-tè pau théi dìng ùh hì. \\
     \textsc{3sg} believe person-\textsc{pl} on-\textsc{loc} this strong-\textsc{nmlz} sign-\textsc{pl} be.given \textsc{irr} \textsc{decl} \textsc{1sg}.self because-\textsc{erg} fear drive.out know \textsc{irr} 2/3PL \textsc{3sg} \textsc{pau} other-\textsc{pl} \textsc{pau} know \textsc{irr} 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And these signs shall follow them that believe; In my name shall they cast out devils; they shall speak with new tongues;}}

\exi{18}
\gll Gul à lawn' hangun bangmah cí lò dìng ùh à, gú tùi à dawn hangun zòng bangmah cí lò dìng ùh hì. Cí-ná-tè tùngàh à khùt ùh nga dìng ùh à, cí-ná-tè dām dìng ùh hì à cí hì \\
     viper \textsc{3sg} throw \textsc{hangun} nothing say \textsc{neg} \textsc{irr} 2/3PL \textsc{3sg} tree water \textsc{3sg} top \textsc{hangun} also nothing say \textsc{neg} \textsc{irr} 2/3PL \textsc{decl} say-\textsc{nmlz}-\textsc{pl} on-\textsc{loc} \textsc{3sg} hand 2/3PL five \textsc{irr} 2/3PL \textsc{3sg} say-\textsc{nmlz}-\textsc{pl} good \textsc{irr} 2/3PL \textsc{decl} \textsc{3sg} say \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{they shall take up serpents; and if they drink any deadly thing, it shall not hurt them; they shall lay hands on the sick, and they shall recover.}}

\exi{19}
\gll túa bàng-ìn Topa Jesuh ìn àmaute tùngàh thù à gēn khìt cìang-ìn vantung-àh kila-tò-ìn Pasian' taklam-àh à tù hì. \\
     that like-\textsc{erg} lord \textsc{jesuh} \textsc{erg} \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{pro} on-\textsc{loc} word \textsc{3sg} speak \textsc{seq} then-\textsc{erg} heaven-\textsc{loc} woman-\textsc{cont}-\textsc{erg} god right-\textsc{loc} \textsc{3sg} now \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{So then after the Lord had spoken unto them, he was received up into heaven, and sat on the right hand of God.}}

\exi{20}
\gll Nùng-zúi-tè zòng mùn khèmpeuh-àh pái-ìn thù à hìlh ùh hì. Topa ìn zòng àmaute' nasep sep-pìh à, à thuhilhna-tè ùh mán hì, cí-ìn à làh-ná-ìn àmaute tùngàh vangliat-ná lìm-tè à pía hì \\
     life-follow-\textsc{pl} also place all-\textsc{loc} go-\textsc{erg} word \textsc{3sg} tell 2/3PL \textsc{decl} lord \textsc{erg} also \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{pro} work work-with \textsc{3sg} \textsc{3sg} teaching-\textsc{pl} 2/3PL finish \textsc{decl} say-\textsc{quot} \textsc{3sg} let.down-\textsc{nmlz}-\textsc{erg} \textsc{3pl}.\textsc{pro} on-\textsc{loc} strong-\textsc{nmlz} sign-\textsc{pl} \textsc{3sg} give \textsc{decl} \\
\glt \textcolor{kjvcolor}{\textit{And they went forth, and preached every where, the Lord working with them , and confirming the word with signs following. Amen.}}

\end{exe}
